### [1] [Exascale Multi-Task Graph Foundation Models for Imbalanced, Multi-Fidelity Atomistic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15380)
*Massimiliano Lupo Pasini,Jong Youl Choi,Kshitij Mehta,Richard Messerly,Rylie Weaver,Linda Ungerboeck,Isaac Lyngaas,Benajmin Stump,Ashwin M. Aji,Karl W. Schulz,Jorda Polo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于HydraGNN原子图基础模型的百亿级材料发现工作流，通过多任务架构联合训练16个第一性原理数据集，实现了对11亿原子结构的快速筛选，将原本需要数年的计算压缩至50秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统第一性原理方法（first-principles methods）在探索广阔化学设计空间时面临计算成本过高的问题，需要开发能够快速可靠探索大规模材料设计空间的新方法。

Method: 采用基于HydraGNN构建的原子图基础模型（atomistic graph foundation models），通过多任务架构（multi-task architecture）和每个数据集独立的头部（per-dataset heads）联合训练16个开放第一性原理数据集。使用可扩展的ADIOS2/DDStore数据管道，在Frontier超算上进行大规模DeepHyper超参数优化，最终选择基于PaiNN的领先模型。

Result: 模型实现了对11亿原子结构在50秒内的快速评估，将原本需要数年的第一性原理计算压缩到极短时间内。量化了精度-性能权衡（BF16/FP32/FP64），在12个化学多样性下游任务中展示了良好的迁移能力，并在Frontier、Aurora和Perlmutter系统上实现了无缝的强扩展和弱扩展。

Conclusion: 该工作流能够快速可靠地探索原本第一性原理方法无法触及的广阔化学设计空间，支持数据稀缺情况下的跨领域下游任务微调，为大规模材料发现提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: We present an exascale workflow for materials discovery using atomistic graph foundation models built on HydraGNN. We jointly train on 16 open first-principles datasets (544+ million structures covering 85+ elements) using a multi-task architecture with per-dataset heads and a scalable ADIOS2/DDStore data pipeline. On Frontier, we execute six large-scale DeepHyper hyperparameter optimization campaigns in FP64 and promote the top-performing message-passing models to sustained 2,048-node training, yielding a PaiNN-based lead model. The resulting model enables billion-scale screening, evaluating 1.1 billion atomistic structures in 50 seconds, compressing a workload that would require years of first-principles computation, and supports data-scarce fine-tuning across diverse downstream tasks. We quantify precision-performance tradeoffs (BF16/FP32/FP64), demonstrate transfer across twelve chemically diverse downstream tasks, and establish seamless strong- and weak-scaling across Frontier, Aurora, and Perlmutter. This work allows fast and reliable exploration of vast chemical design spaces that are otherwise inaccessible to first-principles methods.

</details>


### [2] [Atomic-scale order enables high thermal boundary conductance at $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$/4H-SiC interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15394)
*Hongao Yang,Yongtao Yang,Yuanbin Liu,Tao Ding,Yang Shen,Jiawei Huang,Weigang Ma,Linfeng Fei,Zhenping Wu,Gábor Csányi,Bingyang Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个结合机器学习原子势与晶格动力学的计算框架，研究界面结构对β-Ga₂O₃/4H-SiC异质结热传输的影响，发现原子级有序界面能保持声子相干性并实现创纪录的高热边界电导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同材料界面间的热边界电导（thermal boundary conductance, TBC）对电子器件性能构成基本限制，但预测和理解实际无序界面的热传输仍具挑战性。需要解决界面结构（从无序到原子级锐利）如何影响β-Ga₂O₃/4H-SiC这一重要技术异质结的热传输这一长期问题。

Method: 开发了一个结合机器学习原子势（machine-learned interatomic potentials）与晶格动力学的计算框架，明确考虑声子的波粒二象性（phonon wave-particle duality）。通过原子尺度模拟研究界面无序对热传输的影响。

Result: 界面无序引入额外的界面声子模式，促进两种高度不同晶体间的振动阻抗匹配，但同时破坏界面声子相干性（interfacial phonon coherence）。原子尺度模拟表明，恢复原子级有序能保持相干性并显著提高电导。实验测量验证了预测，在原子级锐利结处实现了创纪录的231 MW m⁻² K⁻¹高热边界电导。

Conclusion: 保持界面声子相干性是缓解不匹配系统中热瓶颈的有效策略。这些见解推动了具有系统调控界面有序度的β-Ga₂O₃/4H-SiC异质结的受控外延生长。研究结果对β-Ga₂O₃基功率电子器件具有直接意义，并为其他不匹配系统提供了通用策略。

Abstract: Thermal boundary conductance (TBC) at dissimilar interfaces imposes a fundamental limit on electronic device performance, yet predicting and understanding heat transport across realistic, disordered boundaries remains elusive. Here, we develop a computational framework that combines machine-learned interatomic potentials with lattice dynamics to address the long-standing problem of how interfacial structure, from disordered to atomically sharp, affects thermal transport in the technologically important $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$/4H-SiC heterostructure. By explicitly accounting for phonon wave-particle duality, we show that interfacial disorder introduces additional interfacial phonon modes that facilitate vibrational impedance matching between the two highly dissimilar crystals, yet it simultaneously disrupts interfacial phonon coherence and limits the potential heat-transport benefit. Our atomistic simulations further indicate that restoring atomic-scale order preserves coherence and yields markedly higher conductance. These insights motivate the controlled epitaxial growth of $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$/4H-SiC heterostructures with systematically tuned interfacial order. Experimental measurements validate our predictions, achieving a record-high TBC of 231 MW m$^{-2}$ K$^{-1}$ at atomically sharp junctions. Beyond the immediate implications for $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$-based power electronics, our results establish the preservation of interfacial phonon coherence as an effective strategy for mitigating thermal bottlenecks in mismatched systems.

</details>


### [3] [Device-area selection of memristive transport regimes in epitaxial $Hf_{0.5}Zr_{0.5}O_{2}$-based ferroelectric devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15486)
*Priscila A. Tapia Presas,Lautaro Galarregui,Wilson Román Acevedo,Myriam H. Aguirre,José Santiso,Sylvia Matzen,Beatriz Noheda,Diego Rubi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过统计分析不同尺寸的Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂/La₀.₆₇Sr₀.₃₃MnO₃异质结构铁电忆阻器件，发现存在两种具有相反电阻-电压手性的忆阻机制，其主导传输机制由器件横向尺寸控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于氧化铪（hafnia）的铁电忆阻器件在神经形态电子学中具有潜力，但极化调制电阻变化与缺陷介导传输之间的相互作用导致复杂的开关机制存在争议，需要深入理解其竞争关系。

Method: 研究结合结构、铁电和忆阻特性表征，对具有Pt顶电极的外延Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂/La₀.₆₇Sr₀.₃₃MnO₃异质结构进行统计分析，器件面积跨越三个数量级，以系统研究尺寸效应。

Result: 识别出两种具有相反电阻-电压手性（resistance-voltage chiralities）的忆阻机制：小器件显示与面积成反比的低阻态，符合面积分布式隧穿传输；大器件则表现出面积无关的电阻，表明存在局域化导电通道（localized conductive channels）。统计成核模型定量描述该行为，得到交叉特征面积A*≈10³μm²。

Conclusion: 横向器件尺寸是控制外延氧化铪基器件主导传输机制的关键参数，导电通道成核与氧空位（oxygen-vacancy）再分布在大器件中铁电唤醒（ferroelectric wake-up）起始相关，建立了统一的物理图像。

Abstract: Ferroelectric memristive devices based on hafnia are promising systems for neuromorphic electronics, yet the interplay between polarization-modulated resistive changes and defect-mediated transport often leads to complex and debated switching mechanisms. Here, we investigate this competition in epitaxial Hf$_{0.5}$Zr$_{0.5}$O$_2$/La$_{0.67}$Sr$_{0.33}$MnO$_3$ heterostructures with Pt top electrodes by combining structural, ferroelectric, and memristive characterization with a statistical analysis across a broad range of device areas spanning three orders of magnitude. We identify two distinct memristive regimes with opposite resistance--voltage chiralities. Small devices exhibit a low-resistance state that scales inversely with area, consistent with area-distributed tunneling transport, while larger devices display an area-independent resistance indicative of localized conductive channels. A statistical nucleation model quantitatively captures this behavior and yields a crossover characteristic area $A^* \approx 10^3~μ\mathrm{m}^2$. This crossover also correlates with the onset of ferroelectric wake-up in larger devices, linking conductive-channel nucleation and oxygen-vacancy redistribution within a unified physical picture. These results establish lateral device size as a key parameter controlling the dominant transport mechanism in epitaxial hafnia-based devices.

</details>


### [4] [Electronic Signature of Melting Onset in Polycrystalline Copper at Extreme Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15491)
*Edna R. Toro,Tobias Held,Armin Bergermann,Megan Ikeya,Maximilian Maigler,Eric R. Sung,Dirk O. Gericke,Mianzhen Mo,Baerbel Rethfeld,Siegfried H. Glenzer,Benjamin K. Ofori-Okai*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过太赫兹时域光谱技术结合分子动力学模拟，揭示了多晶铜中晶界散射对电子输运的限制作用，以及熔化开始阶段电导率的瞬态增加可作为相变起始的直接标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快熔化本质上是离子晶格的结构转变，这种重排通过改变能量景观和散射机制重塑电子性质。虽然电子几乎瞬时响应，但尚不清楚需要多大程度的晶格无序才能产生显著响应。

Method: 采用单次太赫兹时域光谱（single-shot terahertz time-domain spectroscopy）技术，在宽范围激光通量下激发薄膜样品，推断激发后最初皮秒内的瞬态电导率。数据得到双温度分子动力学（two-temperature molecular-dynamics）模拟的支持。

Result: 实验数据显示，在熔化前，电子输运主要受晶界散射（grain-boundary scattering）限制；熔化开始后，该散射通道被强烈抑制。当熔化从晶界开始时，观察到电导率的瞬态增加，这直接标志着相变的起始。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，在非平衡激光驱动物质中，离子弛豫和电子弛豫阶段紧密耦合，光学测量能够分辨熔化的不同阶段。熔化起始已在多晶铜中产生清晰的电子特征。

Abstract: Ultrafast melting is fundamentally a structural transition of the ionic lattice, but this rearrangement also reshapes the electronic properties by changing the energy landscape and scattering mechanisms. Although the electrons react almost instantaneously, it is not {\it a priori} clear how much lattice disorder is required for a significant response. Here, we show that the onset of melting already produces a clear electronic signature in polycrystalline copper. Using single-shot terahertz time-domain spectroscopy on thin films excited over a wide range of laser fluences, we infer the transient conductivity during the first picoseconds after excitation. The data, supported by two-temperature molecular-dynamics simulations, show that before melting, electron transport is substantially limited by grain-boundary scattering and that melting strongly suppresses this channel. As melting begins at these interfaces, we observe a transient increase in the conductivity that directly marks the onset of the phase transition. More broadly, these results show that ionic and electronic relaxation stages are closely coupled in nonequilibrium laser-driven matter and that optical measurements can resolve distinct stages of melting.

</details>


### [5] [Hole concentrations in doped gray α-Sn on InSb and CdTe measured with infrared ellipsometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15553)
*Jaden R. Love,Carlos A. Armenta,Atlantis K. Moses,Haley B. Woolf,Jan Hrabovsky,Stefan Zollner,Aaron N. Engel,Christopher J. Palmstrøm*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过分子束外延在InSb衬底上生长30nm灰锡薄膜，利用红外椭圆偏振光谱研究其温度依赖介电函数，发现0.45eV处的强吸收峰源于倒带结构，并通过f-求和规则计算重空穴浓度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究灰锡（α-Sn）薄膜的电子性质，特别是其倒带结构（inverted band structure）对光学性质的影响，以及衬底表面处理对掺杂类型的调控作用。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）在InSb(001)衬底上生长30nm厚α-Sn层；通过调整衬底表面处理实现n型或p型掺杂；使用傅里叶变换红外椭圆偏振光谱（Fourier-transform infrared ellipsometry）在0.03-0.8 eV能量范围和10-300 K温度范围内测量介电函数。

Result: 光谱显示0.45 eV处存在强吸收峰，源于倒带结构中Γ_-^7"电子"价带到Γ_+^8重空穴价带的跃迁；应用Thomas-Reiche-Kuhn f-求和规则计算重空穴浓度，本征α-Sn层的结果与简并费米-狄拉克统计预测一致；掺杂偏差归因于衬底表面处理导致的施主或受主离子扩散。

Conclusion: α-Sn的倒带结构导致独特的光学响应，其重空穴浓度可通过光学测量准确表征；衬底表面处理是调控α-Sn掺杂类型的关键因素，为基于α-Sn的器件设计提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Gray tin (α-Sn) layers with 30 nm thickness were grown on InSb (001) substrates using molecular beam epitaxy. The surface preparation of the substrates was adjusted to achieve either n-type or p-type doping in the α-Sn layer. Fourier-transform infrared ellipsometry was used to find the temperature-dependent dielectric function of the α-Sn layers from 0.03 to 0.8 eV and from 10 to 300 K. Because of the inverted band structure of α-Sn, the spectra show a strong absorption peak at 0.45 eV due to transitions from the inverted {Γ_-^7} "electron" valence band to the {Γ_+^8} heavy hole valence band. Applying the Thomas-Reiche-Kuhn f-sum rule, the integrated oscillator strength of this peak was used to calculate the heavy hole concentration as a function of temperature. For a nearly intrinsic α-Sn layer, the heavy hole concentration agrees well with predictions based on degenerate Fermi-Dirac statistics. Deviations from the intrinsic α-Sn carrier concentrations are attributed to substrate surface preparation leading to the diffusion of donor or acceptor ions into the α-Sn layer causing n-type or p-type doping.

</details>


### [6] [Facet-dependent Chemical Kinetics Governed Growth of Twisted Graphene Layers with Pre-designed Angles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15639)
*Chaowu Xue,Mengzhao Sun,Zixuan Zhou,Zhuoran Yao,Li-Qun Shen,Xiao Kong,Honglong Zhao,Feng Ding,Marc Willinger,Zhongkai Liu,Zhu-Jun Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种在铂基底上通过化学气相沉积（CVD）可控制备具有预设扭转角（包括魔角）的扭转石墨烯层（TGLs）的规模化策略，揭示了铂晶粒指数与石墨烯生长动力学之间的关联机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转石墨烯层（TGLs）是研究多种量子现象的重要平台，但其规模化应用受到缺乏精确角度可靠合成方法的限制。本研究旨在通过深入理解晶粒指数与石墨烯生长动力学之间的相互作用，开发可控制备TGLs的方法。

Method: 采用化学气相沉积（CVD）方法在铂（Pt）基底上生长石墨烯，结合多种互补的原位表征技术，识别不同铂晶粒的活性序列及其与表面重构的关系。通过建立晶粒指数与石墨烯生长优先性及取向的关联，利用具有显著不同催化活性和无扭结原子台阶的相邻晶粒对，实现石墨烯覆盖层的可控折叠和撕裂。

Result: 研究发现不同铂晶粒的活性序列取决于石墨烯诱导表面重构过程中暴露(110)晶面的面积比例，且CVD生长的石墨烯取向由依赖于晶粒取向的表面形貌决定。覆盖层诱导的台阶聚束（step bunching）和平台重构（terrace reconfiguration）对畴形态和折叠方向起关键调控作用。基于这些机理认识，建立了基底工程框架，可理性选择特定铂晶粒来制备具有预设扭转角（包括具有平带色散的魔角）的TGLs。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅揭示了铂催化石墨烯CVD生长的基本动力学机制，还提供了一种通过动态基底重构操纵可折叠二维材料的普适性方法学，以在开放表面上可编程生长高质量TGLs为例进行了验证。

Abstract: Twisted graphene layers (TGLs) provide a powerful platform for investigating multiple quantum phenomena, yet their scalable deployment is hindered by the lack of reliable synthesis with precise angle. Here, benefited from a deeper understanding of the interplay between grain index and graphene growth kinetics, we report a scalable strategy to grow TGLs with pre-designed twist angles on platinum (Pt) via chemical vapor deposition (CVD), Through a combination of complementary in situ methods, we identified the activity sequence of different Pt grains and attributed it to the area ratio of exposed (110) facets during graphene-induced surface reconstruction. Moreover, we revealed that CVD-grown graphene orientation is determined by the grain-orientation-dependent surface morphology. By leveraging the so-established correlations between grain index with both graphene growth priority and its orientation, we achieve controlled folding and tearing of graphene overlayer using a pair of adjacent grains with dramatically different catalytical activity and kink-free atomic steps. We reveal that overlayer-induced step bunching and terrace reconfiguration critically govern the domain morphology and folding direction. Building on this mechanistic insight, we demonstrate a substrate-engineering framework where specific platinum grains are rationally selected to yield TGLs with pre-designed twist angles, including magic angle with flat band dispersion. This work not only highlights fundamental kinetics of Pt catalyzed graphene CVD growth, but also offers a generalizable methodology for manipulating foldable two-dimensional materials via dynamic substrate reconstruction, exampled by programmable growth of high-quality TGLs on open surfaces.

</details>


### [7] [Fully compensated and uncompensated ferrimagnetic ferrovalley semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15640)
*Weifeng Xie,Libo Wang,Yunliang Yue,Xiong Xu,Huayan Xia,Hui Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了单轴应变驱动交变磁体（altermagnet）向完全补偿亚铁磁体（fully compensated ferrimagnet）转变的机制，提出了非补偿亚铁磁单层VCrSeTeO以实现大本征谷极化，并揭示了自旋轨道耦合（SOC）可进一步增强谷极化至400 meV以上，以及亚铁磁体中的独特反常谷霍尔效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（AMs）和完全补偿亚铁磁体（FC-FIMs）是结合了反铁磁体和铁磁体优势的新兴磁性材料类别。研究旨在阐明单轴应变驱动AM向FC-FIM转变的机制，并探索在谷电子学（valleytronics）中的应用潜力。

Method: 研究阐明了单轴应变驱动AM向FC-FIM转变的机制，发现伴随的非相对论谷极化（non-relativistic valley polarization）与相反自旋子晶格中磁性原子间的净磁矩正相关。提出了非补偿亚铁磁单层VCrSeTeO以实现大本征谷极化，并利用自旋轨道耦合（SOC）扰动定理（SOC perturbation theorem）解释其增强效应。

Result: SOC在单轴应变下可将谷极化进一步提升至400 meV以上。研究揭示了亚铁磁体VCrSeTeO中独特的反常谷霍尔效应（anomalous valley Hall effect），其中谷霍尔电压在同一谷内发生反转。该工作为从交变磁体衍生的亚铁磁谷半导体（ferrimagnetic ferrovalley semiconductors）在谷电子学中的应用提供了理论指导。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了实现巨大谷极化的策略，并为从交变磁体衍生的亚铁磁谷半导体在谷电子学中的应用提供了理论指导。通过阐明应变驱动转变机制和揭示独特的反常谷霍尔效应，为新型磁性材料在自旋电子学和谷电子学器件中的应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) and fully compensated ferrimagnets (FC-FIMs) are emerging classes of magnetic materials that combine the advantages of antiferromagnets and ferromagnets. Here, we elucidate the mechanism behind the uniaxial strain-driven transformation from AM to FC-FIM and find that the accompanying non-relativistic valley polarization is positively correlated with the net magnetic moment between magnetic atoms in opposite spin sublattices. We then propose an uncompensated ferrimagnetic monolayer VCrSeTeO to achieve large intrinsic valley polarization. Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) is shown to further increase the valley polarization to over 400 meV under uniaxial strains and the reason is explained in terms of SOC perturbation theorem. Furthermore, we reveal a distinctive anomalous valley Hall effect in which the valley Hall voltage is reversed within the same valley in ferrimagnet VCrSeTeO. This work proposes a strategy for realizing giant valley polarization and provides theoretical guidance for the application of ferrimagnetic ferrovalley semiconductors derived from altermagnets in valleytronics.

### [8] [Flat-band energy filtering in interacting systems: conditions for improving thermoelectric performances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15684)
*F. Cosco,R. Tuovinen,F. Plastina,N. Lo Gullo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡格林函数方法分析一维平带（flatband）模型的电子输运性质，发现完全孤立的平带并非有效的热电材料，最佳热电性能出现在平带边缘附近，且电子-电子相互作用会重整化平带结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Ni₃In₁₋ₓSnₓ化合物中平带对热电性质影响的理论与实验研究启发，本研究旨在探究两种一维平带模型（锯齿链和金刚石链）的电子输运特性，这两种模型的关键区别在于平带与色散带（dispersive band）的分离方式不同。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green function）框架，在Hartree-Fock和GW近似水平下处理电子相互作用，计算完整的热电系数和品质因数zT随栅压（gate voltage）与温度的变化关系。

Result: 研究发现完全孤立的平带并非有效的热电体：当化学势进入平带时电导率消失，使得大的塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和明显的维德曼-弗朗兹定律（Wiedemann-Franz law）违反失去物理意义。最佳热电性能出现在平带边缘下方，此处透射函数随能量变化最快，符合Mahan-Sofo图像，且需要平带通过与色散态杂化产生有限展宽。电子-电子相互作用会重整化平带结构，导致带宽的相互作用驱动变窄，并在金刚石链中于半填充附近诱导关联驱动的平带-色散带间隙打开。

Conclusion: 平均场处理会系统性高估zT值，突显了超越平均场的关联效应对于平带热电材料定量可靠预测的重要性。研究强调了平带与色散态杂化产生的有限展宽对于实现最佳热电性能的关键作用。

Abstract: Motivated by recent theoretical and experimental studies on the role of flatbands in the thermoelectric properties of Ni$_3$In$_{1-x}$Sn$_x$ compounds, we investigate electron transport in two minimal one-dimensional flatband models, the sawtooth and diamond chains, which differ in a crucial aspect: the flatband is separated from the dispersive band by a finite gap in the former, while the two bands touch in the latter. Using a non-equilibrium Green function framework with interactions treated at the Hartree-Fock and GW levels, we compute the full set of thermoelectric coefficients and the figure of merit $zT$ as functions of gate voltage and temperature. We show that, contrary to naive expectation, a perfectly isolated flat-band is a physically ill-founded thermoelectric: the electrical conductivity vanishes as the chemical potential enters the flat-band, rendering the large Seebeck coefficient and the apparent violation of the Wiedemann-Franz law physically meaningless. Optimal thermoelectric performance is instead achieved just below the flat-band edge, where the transmission function varies most rapidly with energy, consistent with the Mahan-Sofo picture, and requires a finite broadening of the flat-band through hybridization with dispersive states. We further show that electron-electron interactions renormalize the flat-band structure itself, inducing an interaction-driven narrowing of the bandwidth and, in the diamond chain, a correlation-induced opening of a gap between the flat-band and the dispersive band near half-filling. Mean-field treatments are found to systematically overestimate \(zT\), highlighting the importance of beyond-mean-field correlations for quantitatively reliable predictions in flat-band thermoelectrics.

### [10] [Experimentally-validated multi-slice simulation of electron diffraction patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15899)
*Xinke Xiao,Tianle Ma,Lingxuan Shao,Jun Liu,Qiwei Shi,Canying Cai,Stéphane Roux*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文优化了多片层法（MS）用于电子背散射衍射（EBSD）模拟，通过放弃高能假设和使用高阶泰勒展开来逼近单向薛定谔方程，使MS5（五阶展开）在计算成本与图案精度间取得良好平衡，首次实现了MS EBSD模拟与实验数据的比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前最广泛使用的布洛赫波法（BW）虽然能准确预测菊池极和带的位罝与亮度，但本质上仅限于完美晶体结构。多片层法（MS）虽能模拟各种缺陷结构并提供更多衍射细节，但主要限于理论发展且未与实验数据进行比较。

Method: 本文通过放弃高能假设并利用高阶泰勒展开来逼近单向薛定谔方程，优化了多片层法（MS）。使用多晶Al-Mg合金的实验EBSD图案作为索引参考来挑战MS模拟，并采用定制的各向同性畸变校正模型和标准立体三角形重建来增强精度。

Result: 五阶展开的MS（称为MS5）在计算成本与图案精度之间取得了良好平衡。通过定制的各向同性畸变校正模型和标准立体三角形重建，MS5的精度可与BW相媲美。这是首次将MS EBSD模拟与实验数据进行比较的研究。

Conclusion: 该研究为EBSD表征开辟了新的可能性，例如再现具有各种缺陷的晶体的衍射图案。优化的MS方法能够模拟缺陷结构，弥补了BW方法仅限于完美晶体结构的局限性。

Abstract: High-Resolution Electron Backscatter Diffraction (HR-EBSD) has advanced rapidly in recent years, significantly improving elastic strain measurements and dislocation density evaluation with submicron spatial resolution. To achieve better accuracy in the measurements, high-quality dynamical simulation patterns are required to be matched with experimental ones. Currently, the most widely used pattern simulation method, the Bloch Wave method (BW), can accurately predict the positions and brightness of Kikuchi poles and bands, but is intrinsically limited to perfect crystal structures. Another simulation scheme, the multi-slice method (MS), follows the evolution of electron waves as they travel through the sample. MS is advantageous in simulating various defect structures with more diffraction details.  Yet, it is mainly considered for theoretical developments and has not been compared to experimental data.  This paper optimizes the MS method by abandoning the high-energy hypothesis and utilizing higher-order Taylor expansions to approach the forward-only Schrodinger equation. Experimental EBSD patterns of polycrystal Al-Mg alloys are used to challenge MS simulations as a reference for indexation.  It is demonstrated that the 5th-order expansion of MS, referred to as MS5, achieves a good balance between computational cost and pattern precision. A tailored isotropic distortion correction model and standard stereographic triangle reconstruction enhance the precision of MS5 to be comparable with BW. To the best of our knowledge, this study provides the first comparison of MS EBSD simulations with experimental data. It opens new possibilities for EBSD characterization, such as reproducing diffraction patterns of crystals with various defects.

### [12] [Laser induced surface nitriding of niobium: phase evolution and superconducting behaviour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15981)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光氮化（laser nitriding）是一种调控金属表面性能的通用方法，但其对氮化铌（niobium nitrides）超导响应的影响尚未得到充分探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，通过激光氮化铌来设计兼具机械强度和超导性能的Nb-N层。

Method: 研究采用波长为1064 nm的纳秒脉冲激光，在最高2.50 bar的受控氮气氛下对铌进行激光氮化。通过独立调节氮气压力、二维累积通量（F₂D）和激光辐照度，建立了激光加工图。使用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）、扫描电子显微镜（scanning electron microscopy）和电子背散射衍射（electron backscatter diffraction）进行系统分析。

Result: 当F₂D超过特定值（在2.50 bar下>50 kJ/cm²）时，富氮γ-Nb₄N₃₊ₓ相通过熔融在近表面层形成，其下方为β-Nb₂N层，更深处为嵌入铌基体中的β晶粒带。γ相占主导时，超导临界温度（Tc）显著提升至约15K，并观察到磁不可逆性。低F₂D值（在1.50-2.50 bar下≈7.5 kJ/cm²）时，形成的亚微米β-Nb₂N晶粒均匀氮化物层使表面显微硬度提高约四倍。

Conclusion: 该研究为激光诱导铌氮化提供了基础见解，可用于设计机械强度高且具有超导性能的Nb-N层。研究结果表明，通过精确控制激光加工参数，可以调控氮化物的相组成，从而实现对表面机械性能和超导性能的协同优化。

Abstract: Laser nitriding represents a versatile approach for tailoring the surface properties of metals. Up to now, its effect on the superconducting response of niobium nitrides remains largely unexplored. In this work, the nitriding process of niobium by laser irradiation under a controlled nitrogen atmosphere up to 2.50 bar, using a nanosecond pulsed laser with wavelength of 1064 nm has been investigated. By independently tuning the nitrogen pressure, the two-dimensional accumulated fluence ($F_{2D}$) and the laser irradiance, a laser-processing map for the formation of either a combination of $β$-Nb$_2$N (hexagonal) and $γ$-Nb$_4$N$_{3\pm x}$ (tetragonal) phases or only the $β$-phase has been established. Systematic analysis by X-ray diffraction, scanning electron microscopy and electron backscatter diffraction revealed that the nitrogen-rich $γ$-phase forms in the near-surface layer through melting when $F_{2D}$ exceeds a certain value ($> 50 \,\mathrm{kJ/cm^2}$ at 2.50 bar). A $β$-layer is observed underneath, and further inside, there is a band of embedded $β$-grains in the Nb matrix. Their size gradually decreases with increasing distance to surface, suggesting thermal gradients and a diffusion formation mechanism. When the $γ$-phase becomes predominant, a significant increase in the superconducting critical temperature is observed, up to $T_c \approx 15\,\mathrm{K}$, and magnetic irreversibility. For low $F_{2D}$ values ($\approx 7.5 \,\mathrm{kJ/cm^2}$ at 1.50-2.50 bar), the formation of a uniform nitride layer composed of sub-micron-sized $β$-Nb$_2$N grains results in a ca. fourfold enhancement in surface microhardness. These findings provide fundamental insights into laser-induced nitriding of niobium to engineer mechanically robust and superconducting Nb-N layers.

### [13] [Mircomechanical insights into unconstrained grain boundary sliding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16026)
*Divya Sri Bandla,Subin Lee,Christoph Kirchlechner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过镍双晶微柱压缩实验，揭示了晶界滑移（GBS）的本征行为，发现其低应变率敏感性（SRS≈0.034）表明扩散控制的协调机制缺失，而常见于多晶材料的高SRS主要源于协调过程而非滑移机制本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶界滑移（grain boundary sliding, GBS）是多晶材料高温变形中的关键机制，但其本征行为常被额外的应变协调过程所掩盖。本研究旨在通过受控实验条件分离GBS的本征贡献。

Method: 采用含单一高角度晶界的镍双晶微柱（Ni bicrystal micropillars），在室温至600°C温度范围和5×10⁻⁴至10⁻¹ s⁻¹应变率范围内进行压缩测试。通过对比双晶与单晶响应，分离出GBS的本征贡献。

Result: 实验测得GBS的应变率敏感性（strain-rate sensitivity, SRS）保持较低值（≈0.034±0.017），与室温值相当，表明扩散控制的协调机制不存在。GBS的激活能为234 kJ mol⁻¹，与晶界扩散辅助的晶界位错滑移机制一致。

Conclusion: 多晶材料中通常与GBS相关的高应变率敏感性主要源于协调过程（accommodation processes），而非晶界滑移机制本身。这一发现澄清了GBS本征行为与协调过程贡献的区别。

Abstract: Grain boundary sliding (GBS) is a key deformation mechanism at high homologous temperatures in polycrystalline materials, however, its intrinsic behavior is often obscured by additional strain accommodation processes. In this study, dislocation-mediated unconstrained GBS was investigated using Ni bicrystal micropillars containing a single high-angle grain boundary. Micropillar compression tests were conducted over a temperature range from room temperature to $600\,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ and strain rates between $5\times10^{-4}$ and $10^{-1}\,\mathrm{s}^{-1}$. By comparing bicrystal and single-crystal responses, the intrinsic contribution of GBS was isolated. The strain-rate sensitivity remained low (SRS $\approx 0.034 \pm 0.017$), comparable to room temperature values, indicating the absence of diffusion-controlled accommodation mechanisms. The activation energy for GBS was determined to be $234\,\mathrm{kJ\,mol^{-1}}$, consistent with grain boundary diffusion-assisted glide of grain boundary dislocations. These results demonstrate that the high strain-rate sensitivity commonly associated with GBS in polycrystals originates primarily from accommodation processes rather than the intrinsic sliding mechanism.

### [14] [Formation of photoinduced space-charge field during in-bulk domain creation by femtosecond NIR laser irradiation in MgO:LN crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16048)
*I. A. Kipenko,D. A. Zorikhin,A. R. Akhmatkhanov,V. Ya. Shur*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究分析了近红外飞秒激光在MgO:LN晶体中诱导的畴翻转现象，重点关注微裂纹、折射率改变区域与光致畴的相对位置关系，并首次报道了紧聚焦激光在焦点附近产生光伏电场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在深入理解近红外飞秒激光（NIR fs-laser）在MgO:LN晶体中诱导畴翻转的机制，特别关注光致畴、微裂纹和折射率改变区域在聚焦点附近的相对空间位置关系。

Method: 通过X方向光学成像观察辐照样品的微裂纹和透镜状区域，采用图像重叠技术揭示微裂纹、畴和透镜状区域的相对位置，并研究这些光致结构在退火过程中的温度稳定性。

Result: 发现畴包裹微裂纹并与透镜状区域部分相交；退火后折射率局部改变不可逆消失，而微裂纹和畴保持不变；首次报道紧聚焦近红外飞秒激光在焦点附近产生光伏电场（photovoltaic field）。

Conclusion: 折射率改变源于光折变效应（photorefractive effect），退火后透镜状区域消失是由于体电导率增加导致光致空间电荷场的体屏蔽；该效应可用于通过体畴工程（in-bulk domain engineering）制备三维非线性光子晶体。

Abstract: We have studied the domain switching under NIR fs-laser irradiation in MgO:LN single crystals with special attention to the relative positions of the light-induced domains, microtracks and regions with modified refractive index in the vicinity of the focusing point. The optical imaging along X direction of the irradiated sample demonstrated the narrow microtracks and the lens-shaped regions ("lenses") located in the vicinity of the microtracks. The relative positions of light-induced microtracks, domains and lenses were revealed by overlapping of their images. We have found that the domain envelops the microtrack and partially intersects with the lens. The temperature stability of all light-induced objects during annealing was studied. It was shown that the local modification of the refractive index disappeared irreversibly while the microtrack and domain remain unchanged. The obtained local modification of the refractive index has been considered as a result of the photorefractive effect. The disappearance of the lens after annealing is caused by bulk screening of the photoinduced space-charge field by increased bulk conductivity. The generation of photovoltaic field by tightly focused NIR fs-laser irradiation close to the focusing point is reported for the first time to the authors' knowledge. It should be noted that in LN the photovoltaic field is codirectional with spontaneous polarization and thus cannot switch the polarization. However, it is possible in ferroelectrics with the opposite direction of the photovoltaic field and low value of threshold field. The revealed effect can be utilized for creation of 3D nonlinear photonic crystals by in-bulk domain engineering.

</details>


### [15] [Laser-written reconfigurable energy landscapes and programmable Moiré spin textures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16120)
*Matteo Panzeri,Piero Florio,Davide Girardi,Joseba Urrestarazu,Giacomo Sala,Nicola Pellizzi,Matteo Vitali,Marco Madami,Luca Ciaccarini Mavilla,Silvia Tacchi,Elisa Riedo,Andrea Meo,Vito Puliafito,Mario Carpentieri,Riccardo Tomasello,Efe Ersoy,Kai Wagner,Patrick Maletinsky,Olivier Boulle,Edoardo Albisetti,Daniela Petti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于聚焦激光辅助局部场冷却的技术，实现了对磁性纹理（magnetic textures）的灰度级可重编程控制，并展示了其在信息编码和人工自旋超材料（artificial spin metamaterials）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性纹理（magnetic textures）因其丰富的动力学特性、拓扑性质和纳米尺度特征，在新兴自旋电子学（spintronic）和非传统计算技术中具有核心地位。主要挑战在于实现对磁性纹理及其随外部刺激演化的可调谐、可逆和空间分辨控制，这需要通过空间重编程控制其成核和稳定性的磁性能量景观（magnetic energy landscape）。

Method: 采用聚焦激光辅助局部场冷却技术（focused laser-assisted local field cooling technique），这是一种快速、非接触且可扩展的平台。该方法通过以纳米级分辨率非破坏性地控制薄膜异质结构中的交换偏置各向异性（exchange-bias anisotropy），实现了对局部能量分布的灰度级可重编程控制。

Result: 该方法能够创建具有高度可控磁滞（hysteresis）、场依赖可读性（field-dependent readability）和可调开关阈值（switching thresholds）的磁性图案。研究展示了磁场门控可读性的信息编码，以及人工自旋超材料（artificial spin metamaterials）的实现，包括稳定具有场可重构对称性的自旋晶格，以及通过扭曲磁势的几何叠加创建人工莫尔自旋纹理（artificial Moiré spin textures）。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一个多功能、可重编程的平台，弥合了面向应用的磁性存储器与人工晶格中涌现序（emergent order）基础研究之间的差距。

Abstract: Magnetic textures are central to emerging spintronic and unconventional computing technologies due to their rich dynamics, topological properties and nanoscale dimensions. A major challenge remains achieving tunable, reversible, and spatially resolved control over these textures and their evolution as a function of external stimuli, by spatially reprogramming the magnetic energy landscape that governs their nucleation and stability. Here, we exploit a focused laser-assisted local field cooling technique that establishes a fast, non-contact and scalable platform for grayscale spin texture engineering. By non-destructively controlling the exchange-bias anisotropy with nanoscale resolution in thin-film heterostructures, this approach enables grayscale, reprogrammable control of the local energy profile, which we use to create magnetic patterns with highly controlled hysteresis, field-dependent readability and tunable switching thresholds. Leveraging this capability, we demonstrate information encoding with magnetic field-gated readability, and artificial spin metamaterials, stabilizing spin lattices with field-reconfigurable symmetries and creating artificial Moiré spin textures via the geometric superposition of twisted magnetic potentials. These results establish a versatile, reprogrammable platform that bridges the gap between application-oriented magnetic memory and fundamental studies of emergent order in artificial lattices.

### [16] [ChemGraph-XANES: An Agentic Framework for XANES Simulation and Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16205)
*Vitor F. Grizzi,Thang Duc Pham,Luke N. Pretzie,Jiayi Xu,Murat Keceli,Cong Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: ChemGraph-XANES是一个基于代理的自动化框架，用于X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）模拟和分析，通过自然语言任务规范、并行执行和数据管理简化了计算XANES的工作流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）在化学复杂系统中被广泛用于探测局部配位环境、氧化态和电子结构。然而，大规模应用计算XANES的主要限制在于工作流程的复杂性，而非底层模拟方法本身。

Method: 提出ChemGraph-XANES框架，这是一个自动化XANES模拟和分析的代理框架。该框架基于ASE、FDMNES、Parsl和LangGraph/LangChain工具接口构建，将XANES工作流程操作封装为类型化的Python工具，可由大型语言模型（LLM）代理编排。在多代理模式下，检索增强专家代理参考FDMNES手册进行参数选择，而执行代理将用户请求转换为结构化工具调用。

Result: 框架展示了基于文档的参数检索能力，并证明同一工作流程既支持显式结构文件输入，也支持化学级别的自然语言请求。由于独立的XANES计算本质上是任务并行的，该框架非常适合在高性能计算（HPC）系统上进行高通量部署，能够为下游分析和机器学习应用生成可扩展的XANES数据库。

Conclusion: ChemGraph-XANES为基于物理的XANES模拟、光谱管理和代理兼容的计算光谱学提供了一个可重现且可扩展的工作流程层。

Abstract: Computational X-ray absorption near-edge structure (XANES) is widely used to probe local coordination environments, oxidation states, and electronic structure in chemically complex systems. However, the use of computational XANES at scale is constrained more by workflow complexity than by the underlying simulation method itself. To address this challenge, we present ChemGraph-XANES, an agentic framework for automated XANES simulation and analysis that unifies natural-language task specification, structure acquisition, FDMNES input generation, task-parallel execution, spectral normalization, and provenance-aware data curation. Built on ASE, FDMNES, Parsl, and a LangGraph/LangChain-based tool interface, the framework exposes XANES workflow operations as typed Python tools that can be orchestrated by large language model (LLM) agents. In multi-agent mode, a retrieval-augmented expert agent consults the FDMNES manual to ground parameter selection, while executor agents translate user requests into structured tool calls. We demonstrate documentation-grounded parameter retrieval and show that the same workflow supports both explicit structure-file inputs and chemistry-level natural-language requests. Because independent XANES calculations are naturally task-parallel, the framework is well suited for high-throughput deployment on high-performance computing (HPC) systems, enabling scalable XANES database generation for downstream analysis and machine-learning applications. ChemGraph-XANES thus provides a reproducible and extensible workflow layer for physics-based XANES simulation, spectral curation, and agent-compatible computational spectroscopy.

</details>


### [17] [Bridging Atomistic and Continuum Descriptions of Nanoscale Dislocation Loops in Tungsten](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16246)
*Joseph Duque Lopez,Sergei Dudarev,James Kermode,Thomas Hudson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了预测辐照对钨材料性能的长期影响，需要模拟由辐照损伤产生的位错环相互作用。连续介质模型在缺陷核心附近存在非物理奇异性，但被认为能准确捕捉远场的原子尺度位移。

Method: 开发了钨中纳米尺度位错环的线性弹性模型（linear elastic model），并通过原子模拟（atomistic simulations）进行验证，确保模型能正确捕捉低长度尺度的物理现象。

Result: 当位错环远离材料边界时，原子模拟的预测与连续介质模型的远场行为高度一致。原子结果与连续介质结果的衰减率（decay rate）相互吻合，且随着原子模拟尺寸接近远场极限，结果趋于收敛。

Conclusion: 该连续介质方法能有效模拟钨中辐照损伤位错环的相互作用，特别是在远场区域与原子尺度物理现象保持一致，为预测辐照对材料性能的长期影响提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: In order to predict the long-term effects of irradiation on the material properties of tungsten, a continuum approach to simulating the interactions of dislocation loops, which arise from radiation damage, is proposed. Continuum models of the displacement, strain and stress fields produced by dislocation loops exhibit unphysical singularities near the defect core, but are thought to accurately capture atomistic displacements in the far-field. A linear elastic model of nanoscale dislocation loops in tungsten is developed, and the model is verified using atomistic simulations to ensure that the model is informed by lower-length scale phenomena such that the physics of the problem is correctly captured. We discuss the model and its advantages, and show that predictions produced by atomistic simulations do indeed agree well with the far-field behaviour of the continuum model when dislocation loops are far from material boundaries. In particular, we robustly demonstrate that the decay rate of atomistic results and continuum results coincide with one another, and show that the results converge as the size of the atomistic simulations approach the far-field limit.

### [18] [Atomistic Mechanisms of Stress-Dependent Molten Salt Corrosion in NiCr Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16261)
*Hamdy Arkoub,Jia-Hong Ke,Miaomiao Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过反应分子动力学模拟揭示了镍基合金在熔盐环境中应力状态对晶界腐蚀的影响机制：拉伸应变加速腐蚀，而压缩应变抑制腐蚀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 镍基结构合金在熔盐环境中常同时承受机械载荷和腐蚀侵蚀，但应力-腐蚀相互作用机制尚不明确。先前研究主要关注拉伸应力，而压缩应力的作用研究有限。

Method: 采用反应分子动力学模拟（reactive molecular dynamics simulations）研究Ni₀.₇₅Cr₀.₂₅合金在800°C熔融FLiNaK中的应变与腐蚀耦合效应。使用Σ5(210)晶界模型，施加从拉伸(+4%)到压缩(-4%)的单轴应变，通过氟吸附、电荷重分布和晶界演化评估腐蚀行为。

Result: 拉伸应变通过弹性膨胀减少局部原子堆积并增加晶界处的过剩自由体积，从而增强原子迁移率和熔盐渗透，加速晶间腐蚀。相反，压缩应变通过促进沿晶界形成脊状表面层，限制盐分进入底层合金，从而抑制腐蚀。

Conclusion: 该研究从原子尺度揭示了应力状态如何影响熔盐中的晶界腐蚀，为理解镍基合金在熔盐环境中的应力-腐蚀相互作用提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Ni-based structural alloys in molten salt environments often experience simultaneous mechanical loading and corrosive attack, yet the mechanisms governing stress-corrosion interactions remain unclear. Prior studies largely emphasize tensile stress, while the role of compressive stress has received limited attention. Here, reactive molecular dynamics simulations are used to investigate the coupled effects of applied strain and corrosion in Ni$_{0.75}$Cr$_{0.25}$ exposed to molten FLiNaK at 800$^\circ$C. A $\Sigma5(210)$ grain boundary model is subjected to tensile (+4%) to compressive (-4%) uniaxial strains, and corrosion behavior is evaluated through fluorine adsorption, charge redistribution, and grain boundary evolution. Tensile strain accelerates intergranular corrosion by reducing local atomic packing through elastic dilation and increasing excess free volume at the grain boundary, which enhances atomic mobility and salt infiltration. In contrast, compressive strain suppresses corrosion by promoting the formation of a ridge-like surface layer along the grain boundary, limiting salt access to the underlying alloy. These results provide atomistic insight into how stress states influence grain boundary corrosion in molten salts.

</details>

### [19] [The $Z_3$ soft breaking in the I(2+1)HDM and its cosmological probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15425)
*M. A. Arroyo-Ureña,J. Hernández-Sánchez,C. G. Honorato,S. Moretti,T. Shindou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有Z_3对称性的3-Higgs Doublet Model（3HDM），包含两个惰性双重态和一个活跃双重态（即I(2+1)HDM）。重点分析了引入Z_3软破缺项后模型的行为，探讨了暗物质候选者及长寿命粒子的性质，并研究了在国际直线对撞机上的实验特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有Z_3对称性的3-Higgs Doublet Model（3HDM）在引入软破缺项后的物理行为。该模型包含两个惰性双重态（inert doublets）和一个活跃双重态（active doublet），后者扮演希格斯双重态的角色，这种结构被称为I(2+1)HDM。

Method: 研究方法包括分析Z_3软破缺项对模型行为的影响，研究最轻的Z_3荷电中性标量作为暗物质候选者的可能性。同时考察当破缺尺度足够小时，模型产生长寿命中性态的情况，并分析其在宇宙年龄尺度上的寿命。

Result: 研究结果显示，当破缺尺度足够小时，模型会产生一个与暗物质态具有相反CP宇称的长寿命中性态。该长寿命粒子在寿命与宇宙年龄相当时，可成为另一个有效的暗物质候选者。在国际直线对撞机（ILC）上，长寿命粒子衰变会产生包含位移顶点、横向丢失能量以及多轻子（和喷注）的特征信号。

Conclusion: 结论表明，I(2+1)HDM在Z_3软破缺条件下具有丰富的物理内涵。长寿命中性态既可作为有效暗物质候选者，也可在对撞机实验中产生可观测的位移顶点信号。该模型在暗物质直接探测限制下仍能提供可行的遗迹密度解释，具有重要的现象学意义。

Abstract: A $ Z_3 $ symmetric 3-Higgs Doublet Model (3HDM) with two inert doublets and one active doublet (which plays the role of the Higgs doublet), the so-called I(2+1)HDM, is studied. We discuss the behaviour of this 3HDM realisation when one allows for a $ Z_3 $ soft-breaking term. In this setup, the lightest $Z_3$ charged neutral scalar can be a Dark Matter (DM) candidate. If the breaking scale is small enough, this model provides a long-lived neutral state with the opposite CP parity to the DM state. This long-lived particle could then be another effective DM candidate when its lifetime is comparable to the age of the universe. In this case, we have studied the properties of the ensuing relic density in the presence of the most recent limits from direct searches for DM. Conversely, the case in which the long-lived particle actually decays into the DM particle and Standard Model particles in a detector at a collider experiment is very attractive from the viewpoint of phenomenology. Under such conditions, we have studied signatures involving missing transverse energy and multiple leptons (and jets) at the International Linear Collider (ILC) in the presence of displaced vertices.

### [20] [Theoretical modeling of charged current $ν_μ(\barν_μ)-^{40}Ar$ DIS at DUNE energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15724)
*F. Zaidi,S. Akther,M. Sajjad Athar,S. K. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微观框架，在局部密度近似下使用相对论性核子谱函数（$S_h$）计算核结构函数$F_{iA}(x,Q^2)$。该方法整合了费米运动、结合能、核子关联、介子（π和ρ）贡献，以及核遮蔽和反遮蔽效应。自由核子结构函数$F_{iN}(x,Q^2)$基于MMHT 2014参数化的部分子分布函数计算，包含次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰QCD修正和非微扰靶质量修正。

Abstract: The charged current $ν_μ(\barν_μ)$-induced deep inelastic scattering (DIS) from an $^{40}\mathrm{Ar}$ target is studied using a microscopic framework that incorporates nuclear medium effects due to Fermi motion, binding energy, nucleon correlations, mesonic ($π$ and $ρ$) contributions, and nuclear shadowing and antishadowing across the relevant Bjorken-$x$ region. The nuclear structure functions $F_{iA}(x,Q^2)$ $(i=1\text{-}3)$ are evaluated using a relativistic nucleon spectral function ($S_h$) within the local density approximation employing the free nucleon structure functions, $F_{iN}(x,Q^2)$ $(i=1\text{-}3)$. These $F_{iN}(x,Q^2)$ $(i=1\text{-}3)$ are calculated using parton distribution functions (PDFs) from MMHT 2014 parameterization, including higher-order perturbative QCD corrections up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO), along with nonperturbative target mass corrections (TMC). The resulting nuclear structure functions $F_{iA}(x,Q^2)$ $(i=1\text{-}3)$ are subsequently used to compute the differential DIS cross sections for $^{40}Ar$ nucleus. Numerical results are presented for $ν_μ(\barν_μ)$ beam energies $E=4$ GeV and $E=6$ GeV for the differential scattering cross sections $\frac{d^2σ}{dx dy}$ and $\frac{dσ}{dx}$, relevant to ongoing and upcoming liquid-argon neutrino experiments such as DUNE and the Fermilab Short-Baseline Neutrino program.

### [22] [$δ_{\rm CP}$-free constraints on NSI parameters $\varepsilon_{eμ}$ and $\varepsilon_{eτ}$ using high-purity $ν_μ\,{\rm CC}$ events at IceCube DeepCore](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16157)

TL;DR: 利用IceCube DeepCore的7.5年大气中微子数据，通过ν_μ带电流样本搜索非标准相互作用参数，获得与δ_CP无关的约束，结果与标准模型一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大气中微子为探索超越标准模型理论提供了独特途径。非标准相互作用是重要的BSM场景，能够改变中微子在地球中传播时的味振荡。

Method: 使用IceCube DeepCore的高纯度ν_μ带电流样本，包含7.5年观测数据，搜索非标准相互作用参数ε_{eμ}、ε_{eτ}和ε_{ee}-ε_{μμ}。

Result: 数据样本与标准中微子相互作用一致，对NSI参数设置了与现有实验约束相当的限制。这些约束不受δ_CP简并性影响，与长基线实验的结果互补。

Conclusion: IceCube DeepCore提供的δ_CP无关约束是对长基线中微子振荡实验的重要补充，后者依赖δ_CP的出现通道。

Abstract: Atmospheric neutrinos provide a unique avenue to probe theories beyond the Standard Model (BSM) over a wide range of energies and path lengths. The theory of non-standard interactions (NSI) of neutrinos is one of the important BSM scenarios, which can modify flavor oscillations of atmospheric neutrinos traveling through the Earth. In this work, we use a high-purity $ν_μ$ charged-current (CC) sample of atmospheric neutrinos from IceCube DeepCore with a livetime of 7.5 years to search for the NSI parameters $\varepsilon_{eμ}$, $\varepsilon_{eτ}$, and $\varepsilon_{ee}-\varepsilon_{μμ}$. The $ν_μ$ CC events mainly come from the $ν_μ$ survival channel having no significant dependence on $δ_{\rm CP}$. Therefore, the constraints on $\varepsilon_{eμ}$ and $\varepsilon_{eτ}$ obtained using this $ν_μ$ CC sample are expected to be free from the $δ_{\rm CP}$-degeneracy. The data sample is found to be in agreement with the standard neutrino interactions. Therefore, we place bounds on these NSI parameters that are consistent with and comparable to existing experimental constraints. These $δ_{\rm CP}$-free constraints from IceCube DeepCore are complementary to those from the long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiments, where the appearance channel depends on $δ_{\rm CP}$.

</details>


### [23] [Quantum Tomography and Entanglement in Semi-Leptonic $h\to VV^*$ Decays at Higher Orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16218)
*Dorival Gonçalves,Ajay Kaladharan,Alberto Navarro*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了希格斯玻色子衰变到电弱规范玻色子（h→ZZ*, WW*）的半轻子衰变道中的角关联，包括有限末态费米子质量、NLO QCD和电弱修正的影响，并评估了这些效应对重建密度矩阵和纠缠度量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯衰变到电弱规范玻色子（h→ZZ*, WW*）中的角关联为探测新物理效应和量子信息可观测量提供了有力工具。需要系统研究半轻子衰变道中各种修正效应的影响。

Method: 研究采用系统分析方法，涵盖半轻子衰变h→VV*→ℓ⁺ℓ⁻q̄q和ℓ⁺νℓq̄q'，包括有限末态费米子质量、次领头阶（NLO）QCD修正和次领头阶电弱修正。通过适当的运动学选择来控制有限质量效应。

Result: 有限末态夸克质量在更包容的区间内可产生超越双qutrit描述（two-qutrit description）的效应。QCD修正导致适度的百分比级别偏移，而电弱修正能显著改变角结构，特别是在h→ZZ*道中。这些效应会改变角可观测量，但半轻子道仍保持有效的双qutrit描述。

Conclusion: 尽管有限质量效应和辐射修正会修改角可观测量，半轻子衰变通道仍保持有效的双qutrit描述，为研究希格斯衰变中的量子信息特性提供了可靠框架。

Abstract: Angular correlations in Higgs decays to electroweak gauge bosons, $h \to ZZ^*, WW^*$, provide a powerful probe of both new physics effects and quantum information observables. We present a systematic study of semi-leptonic decays $h \to V V^* \to \ell^+\ell^- q\bar{q}$ and $\ell^\pm ν_\ell q\bar{q}'$, including finite final state fermion masses, NLO QCD, and NLO electroweak corrections. We show that finite final state quark masses can induce effects that go beyond the two-qutrit description in more inclusive regimes, while remaining controllable with suitable kinematic selections. QCD corrections lead to modest percent-level shifts, whereas electroweak corrections can significantly modify the angular structure, particularly in the $h\to ZZ^*$ channels. We assess the impact of these effects on the reconstructed density matrix and entanglement measures, finding that, while they modify the angular observables, semi-leptonic channels retain an effective two-qutrit description.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究辐射对量子系统的影响，特别是在对撞机（colliders）中产生的基本费米子-反费米子对（elementary fermion-antifermion pairs）自旋所定义的量子系统。关注高能末态辐射如何影响这些系统的量子特性。

Method: 研究方法包括对多个过程的理论预测，并研究在具有高能辐射的独占样本（exclusive samples）中实验观测该效应的可行性。分析基于当前和未来的对撞机数据。

Result: 研究结果表明，高能末态辐射能够诱导退相干，并显著降低基本费米子对形成的量子系统的纠缠度。在LHC的$pp \rightarrow t\bar{t}(g)$过程和Belle 2的$e^+e^- \rightarrow τ^{+}τ^{-}(γ)$过程中，利用现有数据可获得统计显著的信号。

Conclusion: 结论指出，未来在$Z$玻色子极点（Z pole）或远高于$t\bar{t}$产生阈值的正负电子对撞机（electron-positron colliders）将进一步扩展该研究前景，为观测辐射诱导的量子退相干效应提供更多机会。

Abstract: We study the impact of radiation on quantum systems defined by the spins of elementary fermion-antifermion pairs produced at colliders. We present predictions for several processes, showing that energetic final-state radiation can induce decoherence and significantly reduce the entanglement of quantum systems formed by elementary fermion pairs. We investigate the feasibility of observing this effect experimentally in exclusive samples with energetic radiation. A statistically significant signal can be obtained with current data in associated $pp \rightarrow t\bar{t}(g)$ production at the LHC and in $e^+e^- \rightarrow τ^{+}τ^{-}(γ)$ production at Belle 2. Future electron-positron colliders operated at the $Z$ pole or well above the $t\bar{t}$ production threshold will extend these prospects further.

### [25] [Delineating neutral and charged mesons in magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15897)
*Toru Kojo,Sakura Itatani*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究采用非相对论夸克模型分析磁场中中性与带电介子的性质，重点关注从弱场到强场区域中相对运动与质心运动的磁场依赖性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究磁场中中性与带电介子的性质差异，特别关注从弱场到强场区域中相对运动与质心运动的磁场依赖性，以理解不同类型介子在磁场中的不同行为特征。

Method: 采用非相对论夸克模型（non-relativistic quark model）并引入谐振子型禁闭势（harmonic oscillator type confining potential），将库仑（Coulomb）和色磁（color-magnetic）等短程关联作为微扰处理。

Result: 中性与带电介子表现出显著不同的定性趋势：中性介子的横向动量守恒且连续，而带电介子则呈现量子化的横向动力学。对于自旋s≥1的带电介子，内部夸克运动的零点能量（zero-point energy）会抵消轨道角动量产生的塞曼能量（Zeeman energy），确保高自旋介子的能量稳定性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了中性与带电介子在磁场中的本质差异，并讨论了强场极限下这些介子的有效降维特性（effectively reduced dimensionality），为理解磁场中不同自旋态介子的稳定性提供了理论解释。

Abstract: We investigate the properties of neutral and charged mesons in magnetic fields, from weak-field to strong-field regimes. To develop analytic insights, we employ a non-relativistic quark model with a confining potential of the harmonic oscillator type. Short-range correlations, such as Coulomb and color-magnetic interactions, are treated as perturbations. In particular, we focus on the magnetic field dependence of the relative and the center-of-mass motions. The qualitative trends differ significantly between neutral and charged mesons: for neutral mesons, the transverse momenta are conserved and continuous, while charged mesons exhibit quantized transverse dynamics. The Zeeman effects, arising from intrinsic spins and orbital angular momenta, are carefully examined. In particular, for charged mesons with spins $s\ge 1$, we discuss how the zero-point energy in the internal quark motion cancels the Zeeman energy from the orbital angular momentum, ensuring the energetic stability of mesons with high spins. The effectively reduced dimensionality of these mesons in the strong-field limit is also discussed.

</details>


### [26] [Tensor decomposition of $e^+e^-\toπ^+π^-γ$ to higher orders in the dimensional regulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16251)
*Thomas Dave,Jérémy Paltrinieri,Pau Petit Rosàs,William J. Torres Bobadilla*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在为未来辐射回返过程（radiative return processes）的次次领头阶（NNLO）预测提供必要的初步见解，超越现有的次领头阶（NLO）计算精度。

Method: 开发了振幅的完整四维张量分解（four-dimensional tensor decomposition），并解析计算了相关的一圈极化振幅（one-loop polarised amplitudes）至更高维度调节器阶数；同时建立了高效的五点费曼积分（five-point Feynman integrals）数值计算框架。

Result: 实现了在整个物理产生区域（physical production region）内稳定且快速的数值计算，评估时间仅需数百毫秒；所得结果适用于蒙特卡洛事件生成器（Monte Carlo event generators）的实现。

Conclusion: 该研究为$e^+ e^-\toπ^+π^-γ$过程的次次领头阶计算建立了完整的解析和数值框架，为未来高精度辐射回返过程的预测提供了必要的基础工具。

Abstract: We present a first study of the scattering process $e^+ e^-\toπ^+π^-γ$ beyond next-to-leading order, aimed at providing preliminary insights required for future NNLO predictions for radiative return processes. A complete four-dimensional tensor decomposition of the amplitude is developed, and the associated one-loop polarised amplitudes are evaluated analytically to higher orders in the dimensional regulator, as required for NNLO accuracy. The calculation is complemented by an efficient numerical framework for the evaluation of the resulting five-point Feynman integrals, enabling stable and fast evaluations across the physical production region with evaluation times of a few hundreds of milliseconds. These results are suitable for implementation in Monte Carlo event generators.

### [27] [Universal Description of Decoherence in Scale-Invariant Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15445)
*Carlos Argüelles,Gabriela Barenboim,Gonzalo Herrera,Tanvi Krishnan,Héctor Sanchis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明，当量子系统耦合到尺度不变环境时，其退相干形式是唯一的：在局域性、洛伦兹不变性、幺正性和连续尺度不变性条件下，任何此类环境的效果在数学上等价于一个"非粒子浴（unparticle bath）"，完全由耦合算符的标度维数 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 表征。这一结论源于共形对称性，而非模型选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子系统耦合到尺度不变环境时的退相干形式问题。作者旨在探索在基本物理原理约束下，此类退相干过程是否具有唯一且普适的数学结构。

Method: 基于局域性（locality）、洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）、幺正性（unitarity）和连续尺度不变性（continuous scale invariance）等基本物理原理，通过理论证明推导出退相干形式的唯一性。使用一致性关系（consistency relations）固定所有退相干和耗散指数。

Result: 证明退相干效果在数学上等价于非粒子浴（unparticle bath），完全由耦合算符的标度维数 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 表征。使用幺正费米气体（unitary Fermi gas）的多通道输运数据验证框架，得到一致的 $d_{\mathcal{U}} = 7/4$。发现量子伊辛临界性（quantum Ising criticality）、暴胀宇宙学（inflationary cosmology）和高能天体物理中微子（high-energy astrophysical neutrinos）都实现同一结构。

Conclusion: 尺度不变环境导致的退相干具有唯一且普适的数学结构，由标度维数 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 完全决定。在 $d_{\mathcal{U}} = 5/2$ 处存在退相干相变（decoherence phase transition），量子相干性在长时间尺度下受到保护而非破坏，这是任何无记忆动力学描述无法预测的定性特征。

Abstract: When a quantum system couples to a scale-invariant environment, what form must its decoherence take? We prove that the answer is unique: under locality, Lorentz invariance, unitarity, and continuous scale invariance, the effect of any such environment is mathematically equivalent to that of an \emph{unparticle bath} -- a scale-invariant continuum of states -- characterized entirely by the scaling dimension $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ of the coupled operator. This is not a modelling choice but a consequence of conformal symmetry. All decoherence and dissipation exponents are fixed by $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ through exact consistency relations, providing falsifiable predictions independent of microscopic details. We validate the framework using multi-channel transport data from the unitary Fermi gas, where two genuinely independent observables yield a consistent $d_{\mathcal{U}} = 7/4$. We further show that quantum Ising criticality, inflationary cosmology, and high-energy astrophysical neutrinos -- spanning more than 25 orders of magnitude in energy -- are unified as specific realizations of the same structure. A decoherence phase transition at $d_{\mathcal{U}} = 5/2$, where quantum coherence is \emph{protected} rather thandestroyed at long times, is a qualitative prediction inaccessible to any memoryless dynamical description.

</details>

### [28] [Divergence of detachment forces in the finite Voronoi model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15481)
*Wei Wang,Brian A. Camley*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 有限Voronoi模型（finite Voronoi model）作为传统Voronoi模型的非汇合扩展，在模拟组织断裂时表现出强烈的时间步长依赖性，需通过正则化（regularization）和物理校准（physical calibration）来解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织断裂（fracture）和分离（detachment）是许多组织水平过程的核心，但传统Voronoi模型通常假设汇合组织（confluent tissue），难以模拟这些现象。有限Voronoi模型作为非汇合扩展，需要解决其模拟断裂时出现的时间步长依赖性问题。

Method: 研究分析了有限Voronoi模型，该模型包含直线Voronoi边和固定半径ℓ的圆弧作为细胞边界。当细胞-介质界面（cell-medium interfaces）的线张力（line tension）超过细胞-细胞接触（cell-cell contacts）张力时，通过正则化处理分离力发散问题，并与可变形多边形模型（deformable polygon model）进行校准。

Result: 有限Voronoi模型在模拟初始完整活性簇（active clusters）断裂时表现出强烈的时间步长依赖性：减小Δt会非物理地抑制簇破裂事件。研究发现分离力在模型中发散，通过正则化可解决此问题。采用两种不同校准策略，研究了关键物理参数如何控制组织断裂时间尺度。

Conclusion: 对于关注非汇合单层（nonconfluent monolayers）中断裂或细胞间粘附（intercellular adhesion）的研究，在有限Voronoi模型中对近分离力学进行物理校准至关重要。这种校准确保了模型在模拟组织断裂过程时的物理合理性和准确性。

Abstract: Detachment and fracture are central to many tissue-level processes, but they are challenging to simulate with Voronoi-type models that typically assume a confluent tissue. Here we analyze the finite Voronoi model, a nonconfluent extension of conventional Voronoi models, in which cell boundaries are composed of straight Voronoi edges and circular arcs of fixed radius $\ell$. When the line tension on cell-medium interfaces exceeds the tension on cell-cell contacts, we find that the model exhibits a strong time-step dependence in the fracture timescale of initially intact active clusters: decreasing $Δt$ can unphysically suppress cluster rupture events. We trace this behavior to a divergence of detachment forces in the finite Voronoi model and introduce a simple regularization. Finally, we calibrate the near-detachment mechanics against a deformable polygon model and examine how key physical parameters control the tissue fracture timescale under two different calibration strategies. Our results show that, for studies focused on fracture or intercellular adhesion in nonconfluent monolayers, a physically motivated calibration of near-detachment mechanics in the finite Voronoi model is essential.

</details>


### [29] [Formation of cylindrical shells via sphere packing from fluidized beds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15517)
*Vinícius Pereira da Silva Oliveira,Danilo da Silva Borges,Erick de Moraes Franklin,Jorge Manuel Peixinho*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟分析了窄垂直圆管中球形颗粒流化床的自发壁面沉降现象，重点关注颗粒在管壁形成的玻璃状或晶体状壳层结构及其稳定性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究窄垂直圆管中流化床颗粒的自发壁面沉降行为，特别关注颗粒在管壁形成的壳层结构特性，这与先前实验观察到的现象存在定性一致。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究球形颗粒在窄垂直圆管中的行为，管径与颗粒直径比D/d为4.3和4.7。通过改变颗粒多分散性（polydispersity）和颗粒间摩擦系数测试壳层稳定性，并通过将圆柱壳展开为平面分析颗粒排列结构。

Result: 在特定流速和床层尺寸范围内，颗粒在管壁沉降形成玻璃状或晶体状壳层，伴随床层高度降低和颗粒脉动减弱。壳层呈现六方晶格结构，缺陷密度随多分散性增加而增加。多分散性阻碍壳层形成，存在临界点使晶体状壳层不稳定；对于双分散床层，仅当颗粒间摩擦足够高时才出现晶体状壳层。

Conclusion: 颗粒在管壁形成的圆柱壳层由颗粒间接触力链和颗粒-壁面接触力共同支撑，其中颗粒间作用力起主导作用。多分散性和颗粒间摩擦系数是影响壳层形成和稳定性的关键因素。

Abstract: The results of a numerical investigation of fluidized beds of spherical particles in a narrow vertical cylindrical pipe, with particular attention to the spontaneous settling along the wall, are reported. Starting from a steady fluidized state, the particles fluctuate because of fluid-particle, particle-particle, and particle-wall interactions. The particles are heavier than the fluid, with diameters d yielding ratios of pipe to particle diameters D/d=4.3 and 4.7. For given ranges of flow velocities and bed sizes, particles settle on the wall, with a decrease in the bed height and particle fluctuations. Either a glass- or crystal-like shell forms along the pipe wall, in qualitative agreement with previous experiments. The polydispersity and the particle-particle friction are varied to test the stability of the particulate shell formation. The shell structure is analyzed by unwrapping it in a plane and locating all particles and their contact points, and we find that it exhibits a hexagonal lattice with a defects density that increases with polydispersity. The shell formation is hindered by polydispersity, and there exists a critical point for polydispersity above which a crystal-like shell is unstable. In a particular case of bidisperse beds, the crystal-like shell only appears when the particle-particle friction is high enough. Finally, we compute the contact forces within particle-particle chains and in particle-wall contacts, which sustain the cylindrical shell, highlighting the dominant role of particle-particle forces.

</details>


### [30] [Universal Loop Statistics from Active Extrusion with Kinetic Barriers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15527)
*A. Chervinskaya,R. Metzler,K. E. Polovnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究建立了染色质无序轨道上黏连蛋白（cohesin）驱动环挤压（loop extrusion）的动力学理论，揭示了障碍物密度和环挤压对称性对环尺寸分布的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解无序染色质轨道上存在瞬时障碍物时，黏连蛋白驱动的环挤压动力学行为，特别是环尺寸分布的统计特性及其与挤压对称性的关系。

Method: 采用动力学理论方法，分析无序染色质轨道上具有瞬时障碍物的环挤压过程，考虑单侧挤压（one-sided extrusion）和双侧挤压（two-sided extrusion）两种对称性模式。

Result: 稳态下平均环尺寸服从由原始持续性和重整化障碍物密度决定的普适定律；单侧挤压产生单指数环长度分布，而双侧挤压产生有限指数模态和峰值分布；实验CTCF锚定环统计显示此类峰值，为挤压对称性提供了直接判别依据。

Conclusion: 该理论建立了无序限制环挤压的统一框架，支持黏连蛋白双臂在活细胞中均主动运作的机制，为理解染色质环挤压动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a kinetic theory of cohesin-driven loop extrusion on a disordered chromatin track with transient barriers. In the stationary state, the mean loop size is shown to obey a universal law determined by the bare processivity and a renormalized obstacle density. Beyond the mean, one-sided extrusion always yields a single-exponential loop-length distribution, whereas two-sided extrusion produces a finite sum of exponential modes and, generically, a peaked distribution. Experimental CTCF-anchored loop statistics exhibit such a peak, thereby providing a direct discriminator of extrusion symmetry. The theory therefore establishes a unified framework for disorder-limited loop extrusion and supports a scenario in which both cohesin arms actively operate in living cells.

### [31] [Voids in liquids: peculiarities of molecular dynamics simulation of fluid systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15852)
*Yu. D. Fomin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了分子动力学模拟中液体出现大空洞现象的原因，指出这种现象发生在系统温度高于液-气临界温度或处于两相共存区域时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子动力学（molecular dynamics）是研究流体系统性质的有力工具，但需要对模拟结果进行正确解释。特别是，一些模拟显示液体中出现大空洞，这与我们对液体的常识认知相矛盾。

Method: 通过分析文献中的多个例子以及作者自身的模拟结果，探讨了液体中大空洞出现的起源和条件。

Result: 研究表明，空洞的出现发生在两种情况下：一是系统温度高于液-气转变（liquid-gas transition）的临界温度；二是系统处于液-气两相（two-phase liquid-gas）区域。

Conclusion: 分子动力学模拟中液体出现大空洞的现象并非异常，而是与系统的热力学状态直接相关，特别是当系统处于超临界或两相共存条件时。

Abstract: Molecular dynamics is a powerful tool to investigate the properties of fluid systems. However, a correct interpretation of the results of simulations is required. In particular, some simulations show appearance of large voids in liquids, which contradicts our common sense on what is liquid. In the present paper we discuss the origin of large cavities liquids in molecular dynamics simulations. We demonstrate that the cavities appear either if the temperature of the system is above the critical temperature of liquid-gas transition or if the system is in two-phase liquid-gas region. These conclusions are illustrated by several examples from literature and our own simulations.

</details>


### [32] [Phase behavior of thermoresponsive colloids drives re-entrant plasmon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15860)
*Angela Capocefalo,Francesco Brasili,Javier Pérez,Edouard Chauveau,Stefano Casciardi,Andrea Militello,Francesco Sciortino,Emanuela Zaccarelli,Federico Bordi,Domenico Truzzolillo,Simona Sennato*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了热响应性聚合物微凝胶中负载等离子体纳米粒子（NPs）时出现的反常再入行为：随着NP负载增加，等离子体耦合先增强后减弱，这一现象由复合物的胶体稳定性决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离子体纳米粒子与热响应性聚合物微凝胶的集成为实现刺激响应光学材料提供了多功能平台，但NP负载量对等离子体耦合的动态控制机制尚不完全清楚，特别是其中可能存在的非直观行为需要深入研究。

Method: 研究结合了光散射和X射线散射技术、光学光谱学以及电泳迁移率测量，通过多角度表征手段分析复合物的结构和光学性质。

Result: 研究发现等离子体耦合不仅受限于单个微凝胶内NP的粒子间距，还受杂化复合物胶体稳定性的影响。中等NP负载时，NP吸附诱导的表面电荷不均匀性促进微凝胶-NP复合物聚集，增强耦合；而复合物保持胶体稳定时，耦合仅由单个微凝胶冠层内的NP组织决定。

Conclusion: 研究建立了连接胶体稳定性与光学响应的相图，识别出胶体稳定性作为设计具有可编程光学性质的软等离子体系统的关键参数，揭示了等离子体耦合与粒子间距之间的定量关系存在两种不同的耦合机制。

Abstract: Plasmonic nanoparticles (NPs) integrated within thermoresponsive polymeric microgels provide a versatile platform for the realization of stimuli-responsive optical materials, where the microgel volume phase transition enables dynamic control of plasmon coupling. This study uncovers a counter-intuitive re-entrant behavior with increasing NP loading in which plasmon coupling initially strengthens and subsequently weakens beyond a critical NP-to-microgel number ratio. By combining light and X-ray scattering techniques with optical spectroscopy and electrophoretic mobility measurements, it is demonstrated that plasmon coupling is governed not only by the interparticle distance between NPs confined within individual microgels, but also by the colloidal stability of the hybrid complexes. At intermediate NP loadings, surface charge inhomogeneities induced by NP adsorption promote aggregation of microgel-NPs complexes, resulting in enhanced plasmon coupling. In contrast, when the complexes remain colloidally stable, coupling is dictated solely by NP organization within the corona of individual microgels. A quantitative relationship between plasmon coupling and interparticle distance reveals two distinct coupling regimes. This behavior is rationalized through a phase diagram linking colloidal stability to optical response. These findings identify colloidal stability as a key parameter for designing soft plasmonic systems with programmable optical properties.

Method: 基于应力和温度相关函数（correlation functions）研究，建立了适用于任意多尺度长度粗糙表面的理论，并与Sutter等人的钢-钢滑动实验数据进行对比验证。

Abstract: The temperature increase in the contact regions between solids in sliding contact has a huge influence on friction and wear. Here we test an analytical theory for the flash temperature, valid for randomly rough surface with multiscale roughness, by comparing the theory predictions with the experimental results of Sutter et al \cite{Sutter} for steel sliding on steel. The theory, which is based on the study of stress and temperature correlation functions, is valid for randomly rough surfaces with roughness on arbitrary many decades in length scale. Within the uncertainty of the experimental data (mainly the surface roughness power spectrum and the steel penetration hardness), there is good agreements between the theory and the experimental results.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了自然电离辐射在引发微米尺度放电中的关键作用，并为研究无电极环境和最小尺度下的放电物理提供了一个实验平台。

Abstract: Electrical discharge at the smallest possible length and charge scales is not well understood. Using optical tweezers, we investigate spontaneous discharges of a single micron-scale particle levitated in air. These ``microdischarges'' have a typical size of $\sim$40 $|e|$, but can be as small as a few $|e|$ and as large as several hundred. The absence of a well-defined trigger charge and the weak dependence on particle size suggest events are not classical gaseous breakdown. Instead, we show that microdischarge events arise from the rapid capture of ions left in the tracks of nearby passing ionizing radiation. Our results highlight the role of natural ionizing radiation in initiating micron-scale discharges and provide a platform for studying discharge physics in electrode-free environments and at the smallest scales.

Method: 研究通过分析非手性活性粒子在动态环境中的自组织行为，特别关注障碍规避型跑动-翻滚（run-and-tumble）粒子与被动布朗粒子波动景观之间的反馈机制。

Abstract: Collective rotations are common in active matter, enhancing cohesion, transport, and mixing. Here, we uncover a different mechanism for rotational order in active matter where a dynamic environment coordinates the self-organization of non-chiral active particles into living crystals exhibiting sustained collective solid-like rotations. At intermediate densities, feedback from a fluctuating landscape of passive Brownian particles stabilizes large living crystals of obstacle-avoiding run-and-tumble agents. Strikingly, this environmental feedback also produces living crystals with qualitatively distinct dynamics: collective solid-like spinning emerges for particles with long persistence times approaching ballistic motion, rather than for particles moving by conventional enhanced diffusion. Beyond revealing a new route to collective rotational order in active matter, these findings highlight the integral role of a dynamic environment in self-organization and suggest environment-mediated design principles for active materials with unconventional dynamical responses.

### [36] [Environmental Control of Self-Aligning Chiral Bristlebots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16185)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在圆形几何结构中，边缘电流的稳定性由粒子内在手性与边缘电流手性之间的相互作用决定。利用鹦鹉螺形状（nautilus-shaped）的障碍物实现了运输的几何整流，该障碍物充当了双重手性敏感的棘轮（doubly chirality-sensitive ratchet）。在刚性连接的组装体中，观察到三角形活性固体在平移和旋转状态之间的自发模式切换。

Conclusion: 研究结果为活性气体的被动控制提供了稳健框架，并阐明了如何利用几何约束在合成活性系统中编程复杂的运输特性。

Abstract: Active matter systems characterized by the interplay of chirality and self-alignment offer a rich landscape for the emergence of non-equilibrium collective behaviors and the development of autonomous materials. We present a versatile experimental platform for studying these dynamics using augmented commercial bristlebots, where custom-designed housings and elastic couplings induce a self-aligning torque and a stable chiral drift. By mapping experimental trajectories to a Langevin-type model, we characterize the single-particle dynamics. In circular geometries, we show that the stability of edge currents is governed by the interaction between intrinsic particle chirality and handedness of the edge current. Furthermore, we demonstrate that transport can be geometrically rectified using a nautilus-shaped obstacle, which acts as a doubly chirality-sensitive ratchet. Finally, we explore the collective dynamics of rigidly linked assemblies, observing spontaneous mode-switching between translational and rotational states in triangular active solids. Our results provide a robust framework for the passive control of active gases and illustrate how geometric constraints can be used to program complex transport properties in synthetic active systems.

Abstract: Freshwater scarcity demands desalination technologies that are efficient, scalable, and sustainable. Using mean-field classical density functional theory and grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that such polymer grafted electrodes enable strongly improved desalination performance, without altering the pore architecture. These results establish interfacial block copolymer grafting as a powerful route toward high-performance, membrane-free desalination.

### [38] [Host-guest co-amorphous structure revealed by the suppression of the first sharp diffraction peak in isotactic poly(4-methyl-1-pentene)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15892)
*Tomoki Ogihara,Yusuke Hiejima,Ayano Chiba*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次报道了室温常压下的主客体共非晶（host-guest co-amorphous）系统，其中癸烷分子占据等规聚(4-甲基戊烯-1)（P4MP1）非晶基体的固有内部空隙，其衍射特征变化类似于主客体共晶中的布拉格峰强度比变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然主客体共晶（host-guest co-crystals）已广为人知，且共非晶固体（co-amorphous solids）在材料科学中得到认可，但主客体共非晶结构的概念仍基本未被探索。研究旨在验证类似SiO2玻璃在高压氦气压力介质中观察到的现象是否能在聚合物体系中实现。

Method: 研究采用等规聚(4-甲基戊烯-1)（isotactic poly(4-methyl-pentene-1), P4MP1）作为模型体系，分析其二维X射线衍射（2D-XRD）图案。通过拉伸样品将非晶的第一尖锐衍射峰（first sharp diffraction peak, FSDP）与重叠的晶体衍射分离，并观察P4MP1浸入癸烷（decane）时FSDP的变化。

Result: 研究发现P4MP1浸入癸烷时FSDP受到抑制，表明癸烷分子占据了P4MP1非晶基体的内部空隙（internal voids）。这证实了室温常压下主客体共非晶系统的存在，其衍射特征变化（FSDP强度比变化）类似于主客体共晶中的布拉格峰强度比变化。

Conclusion: 该研究首次揭示了主客体共非晶结构的存在，其特点是客体分子特异性地占据主体固有空隙。这种结构在衍射测量中的特征变化与主客体共晶类似，表明能够形成共非晶结构的主体材料有望成为分子筛（molecular sieves），特别是液相分子筛（liquid-phase molecular sieves）的候选材料。

Abstract: While host-guest co-crystals are well established, and co-amorphous solids are recognized in materials science, the concept of a host-guest co-amorphous structure remains largely unexplored. A potential analogue is seen in SiO2 glass under high pressure with helium as a pressure medium; the drop in compressibility in this system is ascribed to helium atoms occupying internal voids. In this study, we investigated a semicrystalline polymer, isotactic poly(4-methyl-pentene-1) (P4MP1), which shares key characteristics with SiO2 glass, particularly regarding the first sharp diffraction peak (FSDP). The FSDP in P4MP1 is attributed to internal voids, as evidenced by its suppression under pressure and recovery upon decompression for molten P4MP1. Notably, the response to helium as a pressure medium is also known to parallel the behavior observed in SiO2 glass. Here, we analyzed two-dimensional X-ray diffraction (2D-XRD) patterns of stretched P4MP1 and found a suppression of FSDP when P4MP1 is immersed in decane. The use of stretched samples enabled the clear isolation of the amorphous FSDP from overlapping crystalline diffractions. Our findings reveal the existence of a host-guest co-amorphous system at room temperature and atmospheric pressure, in which decane molecules occupy the amorphous host matrix of P4MP1. Unlike conventional co-amorphous mixtures, this structure is defined by the specific accommodation of guests within the host's inherent voids. Intriguingly, the signature of this structure in diffraction measurements, manifested as changes in the FSDP intensity ratio, may be regarded to parallel the variations in Bragg peak intensity ratios in host-guest co-crystals. Since selective sorption and guest exchange are well-known in co-crystals, hosts capable of forming co-amorphous structures will be promising materials for molecular sieves, or more generally, liquid-phase molecular sieves.

### [39] [Multi-reference GW approximation for strongly correlated molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16013)
*Yuqi Wang,Wei-Hai Fang,Zhendong Li*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了多参考GW（MR-GW）近似方法，通过引入相互作用的多个行列式参考态，将GW近似扩展到强关联系统，克服了传统GW方法在强关联体系中的根本性失效问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW近似是多体微扰理论计算单粒子激发的基石，但在强关联系统中，当单参考态图像失效时，该方法会根本性崩溃。研究旨在克服这一长期存在的局限性。

Method: 引入多参考GW（MR-GW）近似，将强关联效应非微扰地纳入相互作用的多个行列式零阶参考态中。基于广义Dyson方程建立严格的图论框架，定义MR-GW自能，并采用多参考随机相位近似（multi-reference random phase approximation）处理屏蔽相互作用。

Result: 应用于具有挑战性的强关联分子表明，MR-GW能够无缝地捕捉强关联和弱关联效应，提供更准确的电离势，并恢复标准GW方法遗漏的复杂多体卫星峰。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个严格的图论范式，用于将从头算格林函数方法扩展到强关联区域，为处理强关联系统提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The GW approximation is a cornerstone of many-body perturbation theory for computing single-particle excitations, yet it fundamentally breaks down in strongly correlated systems where the single-reference picture fails. To overcome this long-standing limitation, we introduce the multi-reference GW (MR-GW) approximation, which incorporates strong correlation effects non-perturbatively into an interacting multi-determinantal zeroth-order reference. While the standard Dyson equation is inapplicable in this setting, we show that the GW approximation can be naturally generalized by developing a rigorous diagrammatic framework with an interacting reference. Specifically, we define the MR-GW self-energy using a diagrammatic expansion based on the generalized Dyson equation, and utilize a multi-reference random phase approximation for the screened interaction, which captures many-body processes absent in standard GW. Applications to challenging strongly correlated molecules demonstrate that MR-GW seamlessly captures both strong and weak correlations, yielding more accurate ionization potentials and recovering complex many-body satellites missed by standard $GW$. This work establishes a rigorous diagrammatic paradigm for extending ab initio Green's function methods into the strongly correlated regime.

</details>

### [40] [Federated Learning with Quantum Enhanced LSTM for Applications in High Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15775)
*Abhishek Sawaika,Durga Pritam Suggisetti,Udaya Parampalli,Rajkumar Buyya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于高能物理（HEP）大规模数据学习的联邦量子增强长短期记忆模型（QLSTM），该模型结合量子变分电路（VQC）的表示能力和LSTM的时序相关性学习能力，在SUSY数据集上以较少参数和数据量实现了与经典深度学习基准相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（High Energy Physics, HEP）等数据密集型应用需要复杂、大规模且兼具鲁棒性和准确性的模型。为应对这一挑战并满足学习需求，作者设想采用联邦学习（federated learning）框架结合量子增强模型。

Method: 设计了一种混合量子-经典长短期记忆模型（hybrid quantum-classical long-shot-term-memory model, QLSTM）用于分布式节点的本地训练。该模型结合了量子模型在理解特征空间复杂关系方面的表示能力，以及基于LSTM的模型来学习数据点间的必要相关性。考虑到当前独立噪声中等规模量子（noisy-intermediate quantum, NISQ）设备的计算限制和高昂成本，采用了联邦学习设置来分布学习负载。

Result: 在包含500万行的超对称（Supersymmetry, SUSY）数据集分类任务上，该设计的性能不仅优于现有基于变分量子电路（variational quantum circuit, VQC）的量子机器学习（quantum machine learning, QML）技术，而且与经典深度学习基准相当（Δ∼±1%）。该框架仅需<300个参数和2万个数据点即可达到可比性能，相比基线模型有100倍的改进。

Conclusion: 研究表明，所提出的框架通过结合基于LSTM的架构和量子增强VQC的联合模型，在最小化数据和资源需求的情况下展现了改进的学习能力，为大规模数据学习提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Learning with large-scale datasets and information-critical applications, such as in High Energy Physics (HEP), demands highly complex, large-scale models that are both robust and accurate. To tackle this issue and cater to the learning requirements, we envision using a federated learning framework with a quantum-enhanced model. Specifically, we design a hybrid quantum-classical long-shot-term-memory model (QLSTM) for local training at distributed nodes. It combines the representative power of quantum models in understanding complex relationships within the feature space, and an LSTM-based model to learn necessary correlations across data points. Given the computing limitations and unprecedented cost of current stand-alone noisy-intermediate quantum (NISQ) devices, we propose to use a federated learning setup, where the learning load can be distributed to local servers as per design and data availability. We demonstrate the benefits of such a design on a classification task for the Supersymmetry(SUSY) dataset, having 5M rows. Our experiments indicate that the performance of this design is not only better that some of the existing work using variational quantum circuit (VQC) based quantum machine learning (QML) techniques, but is also comparable ($Δ\sim \pm 1\%$) to that of classical deep-learning benchmarks. An important observation from this study is that the designed framework has $<$300 parameters and only needs 20K data points to give a comparable performance. Which also turns out to be a 100$\times$ improvement than the compared baseline models. This shows an improved learning capability of the proposed framework with minimal data and resource requirements, due to the joint model with an LSTM based architecture and a quantum enhanced VQC.

</details>


### [41] [Collective Kernel EFT for Pre-activation ResNets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15742)
*Hidetoshi Kawase,Toshihiro Ota*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对有限宽度深度神经网络，基于G-only闭包层次开发了预激活ResNets的集体核有效场论（collective kernel effective field theory），并诊断了其有限有效性窗口。通过利用残差增量的精确条件高斯性，推导了G的精确随机递归，并系统应用高斯近似得到连续深度ODE系统。研究发现K₀在所有深度保持准确，但V₄方程残差在有限时间累积至O(1)误差，K₁,EFT因源闭包失效而失败，凸显了G-only状态空间约化的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限宽度深度神经网络中，经验核G随层数随机演化。本文旨在开发预激活ResNets的集体核有效场论（collective kernel effective field theory），基于G-only闭包层次并诊断其有限有效性窗口，以理解核演化的统计特性。

Method: 利用残差增量的精确条件高斯性，推导了经验核G的精确随机递归。系统应用高斯近似，得到连续深度ODE系统，包括平均核K₀、核协方差V₄和1/n平均修正K₁,EFT，后者在图表上表现为单圈蝌蚪修正（one-loop tadpole correction）。

Result: 数值结果显示，平均核K₀在所有深度保持准确。然而，V₄方程残差在有限时间累积至O(1)误差，主要由G-only输运项（transport term）的近似误差驱动。此外，K₁,EFT因源闭包（source closure）失效而失败，即使在初始化阶段也表现出系统性不匹配。

Conclusion: 研究结果凸显了G-only状态空间约化的局限性，建议扩展状态空间以纳入sigma-核（sigma-kernel），为理解深度神经网络核演化的统计特性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In finite-width deep neural networks, the empirical kernel $G$ evolves stochastically across layers. We develop a collective kernel effective field theory (EFT) for pre-activation ResNets based on a $G$-only closure hierarchy and diagnose its finite validity window. Exploiting the exact conditional Gaussianity of residual increments, we derive an exact stochastic recursion for $G$. Applying Gaussian approximations systematically yields a continuous-depth ODE system for the mean kernel $K_0$, the kernel covariance $V_4$, and the $1/n$ mean correction $K_{1,\mathrm{EFT}}$, which emerges diagrammatically as a one-loop tadpole correction. Numerically, $K_0$ remains accurate at all depths. However, the $V_4$ equation residual accumulates to an $O(1)$ error at finite time, primarily driven by approximation errors in the $G$-only transport term. Furthermore, $K_{1,\mathrm{EFT}}$ fails due to the breakdown of the source closure, which exhibits a systematic mismatch even at initialization. These findings highlight the limitations of $G$-only state-space reduction and suggest extending the state space to incorporate the sigma-kernel.

Method: 在CERN使用150 GeV μ子束流进行了两次测试束流实验（test beam campaigns），开发了专用算法来测量漂移管在r-φ平面主坐标的单管空间分辨率（single tube spatial resolution）以及沿管方向的次坐标空间分辨率，并评估了探测效率（detection efficiency）随外推命中位置的变化。

Result: 两个数据集在空间分辨率和探测效率方面显示出一致的结果，为漂移室（straw chamber）的性能评估提供了可靠数据，这些发现将帮助建立基准性能指标。

Conclusion: 研究结果为未来高精度径迹探测应用中漂移室的设计、优化和建造提供了有价值的见解（valuable insight），为FCC-ee对撞机径迹探测器的开发奠定了实验基础。

Abstract: We present results from two test beam campaigns that investigate the performance of straw tube detectors as potential candidates for an FCC-ee straw tracker. These studies were carried out at CERN using 150 GeV muon beams. Dedicated algorithms were developed to determine both single tube spatial resolution for the primary coordinate in the $r-φ$ plane and spatial resolution for the secondary coordinate along the tube direction within a straw chamber. Detection efficiency was also evaluated as a function of the extrapolated hit position for each tube. Both datasets showed consistent results for spatial resolutions and efficiency. Our findings will help establish benchmark performance metrics and provide valuable insight for future design, optimization, and construction of straw chambers for high-precision tracking applications.
