### [43] [SHIELD: A Reference Gas-Driven Permeation Platform for Hydrogen Permeation Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15407)
*James Dark,Colin Weaver,Remi Delaporte-Mathurin,Sara Ferry,Kevin B. Woller*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: SHIELD平台是一个用于测量结构材料氢传输特性的气体驱动渗透（GDP）系统，在受控热压条件下提供可靠、可重复的渗透测量，适用于聚变应用中的渗透屏障涂层和先进材料评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为测量聚变装置结构材料在受控热压条件下的氢传输特性，需要开发一个能够最小化实验不确定性并提供可重复条件的渗透测量平台。

Method: SHIELD平台采用静态气体驱动渗透（GDP）配置，具有独立的上游和下游体积，实现驱动压力的精确控制和下游压力上升的准确测量。系统实施了开放记录的数据采集和处理框架以确保数据可追溯性和可重复性。

Result: 在100-600°C温度范围内对316不锈钢和AISI 1018低碳钢进行氢渗透测量，稳态渗透通量从线性下游压力上升中提取并用于确定渗透率。测量的渗透率表现出阿伦尼乌斯（Arrhenius）行为，与两种材料的已发表文献数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: SHIELD平台为氢渗透测量提供了可靠的参考平台，非常适合评估聚变应用中的渗透屏障涂层和先进材料，渗透率测量显示出稳健性和可重复性。

Abstract: A gas-driven permeation (GDP) platform, SHIELD (Salt-compatible Hydrogen barrier Investigation and EvaLuation for fusion Devices), has been developed to measure hydrogen transport properties in structural materials under controlled thermal and pressure conditions. The system is designed to minimise experimental uncertainties associated with leaks, temperature instability, and pressure measurement, while providing reproducible conditions for permeation experiments. The rig operates in a static GDP configuration with independent upstream and downstream volumes, enabling precise control of driving pressure and accurate measurement of downstream pressure rise. An openly documented data acquisition and processing framework is implemented to ensure data traceability and reproducibility. The platform's performance is demonstrated by hydrogen permeation measurements on 316 stainless steel and AISI 1018 low-carbon steel over the temperature range of \SIrange{100}{600}{\degreeCelsius}. Steady-state permeation fluxes are extracted from linear downstream pressure rise and used to determine permeability. The measured permeability exhibits Arrhenius behaviour and agrees well with published literature data for both materials. Permeability measurements are shown to be robust and reproducible. These results demonstrate that SHIELD provides a reliable reference platform for hydrogen permeation measurements and is well-suited to evaluating permeation barrier coatings and advanced materials for fusion applications.

### [44] [Cycle Relations and Global Gluing in Multi-Node Conifold Degenerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16055)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究具有有限个普通双点（ordinary double points）的单参数锥面退化（conifold degenerations），发现当节点通过公共循环几何或同调关系连接时，修正的扩展（corrected extension）被强制进入一个由关系控制（relation-controlled）的更小子空间，而非自由节点数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有有限节点理论（finite-node theory）在反常层（perverse-sheaf）、混合霍奇模（mixed-Hodge-module）和范畴侧为每个节点隔离出一个秩一局部扇区（rank-one local sector），但未能确定哪些全局扩展类（global extension classes）实际上由几何实现。本文旨在研究当节点通过循环几何或同调关系连接时，扩展类如何受到约束。

Method: 引入循环-节点关联数据（cycle-node incidence datum）及其对应的几何实现子空间（geometrically realized subspace），在几何可容许（geometrically admissible）和块适应（block-adapted）的关联假设下，证明修正的反常扩展（corrected perverse extension）通过该子空间分解。局部变分数据（local variation data）沿可容许循环分量（admissible cycle components）的传播（propagation）推导出关联相容性（incidence compatibility）。

Result: 证明修正的反常扩展通过关联控制子空间分解，且相同的关系法则（relation law）相容地提升到混合霍奇模设置。在块分离循环族（block-separated cycle family）中，获得 $R_{\mathrm{res}}=R_{\mathrm{sm}}=R_{\mathrm{ext}}=R_{\mathrm{blk}}$ 的等式关系，表明解析（resolution）、光滑化（smoothing）、扩展（extension）和块（block）侧的关系法则一致。

Conclusion: 当锥面退化（conifold degenerations）的节点通过几何或同调关系连接时，全局扩展类受到严格约束，修正的扩展被强制进入由循环-节点关联数据定义的更小子空间。这一关系法则在反常层、混合霍奇模以及解析与光滑化侧均保持一致，揭示了节点间几何关联对扩展结构的决定性影响。

Abstract: We study projective one-parameter conifold degenerations whose central fiber has finitely many ordinary double points. Existing finite-node theory isolates one rank-one local sector per node on the perverse-sheaf, mixed-Hodge-module, and categorical sides, but does not determine which global extension classes are actually realized by geometry. We show that when the nodes are linked by common cycle geometry or homological relations, the corrected extension is not free nodewise data, but is forced into a smaller relation-controlled subspace. To formalize this, we introduce a cycle-node incidence datum and the associated geometrically realized subspace of the ambient nodewise extension space. Under geometrically admissible and block-adapted incidence hypotheses, we prove that the corrected perverse extension factors through this subspace, with incidence compatibility derived from propagation of local variation data along admissible cycle components, and we show that the same relation law lifts compatibly to the mixed-Hodge-module setting. We then compare this relation law with the resolution and smoothing sides and, in the block-separated cycle family, obtain $R_{\mathrm{res}}=R_{\mathrm{sm}}=R_{\mathrm{ext}}=R_{\mathrm{blk}}$.

### [45] [Hilbert Space Fragmentation and Gauge Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15820)
*Thea Budde,Marina Kristć Marinković,Joao C. Pinto Barros*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究在碎片化的S=1偶极子守恒自旋链中发现了仅在特定子系统中有效的涌现规范对称性，这些非可逆对称性能够标记指数级多的模型扇区，从而为规范理论的精确量子模拟提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格规范理论的哈密顿量表述在规范理论的量子模拟中具有核心作用，理解其谱和其他性质在未来几年将变得至关重要。相关哈密顿量具有局域对称性，并可能展现高阶形式对称性，导致指数级多的动力学断开扇区。

Method: 研究描述了在碎片化的S=1偶极子守恒自旋链（dipole-conserving spin chain）的特定扇区子集中有效的涌现规范对称性。这些非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）能够标记模型中的指数级多扇区。

Result: 通过模拟非规范不变的哈密顿量，实现了规范理论的精确量子模拟。这些涌现的规范对称性仅在碎片化系统的特定子系统中有效，但能够标记指数级多的模型扇区。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了在缺乏明显对称性的系统中，通过涌现规范对称性实现规范理论量子模拟的可能性，为理解希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert space fragmentation）和规范理论模拟提供了新视角。

Abstract: The Hamiltonian formulation of lattice gauge theories plays a central role in quantum simulations of gauge theories, and understanding their spectrum and other properties is expected to become crucial in the upcoming years. The relevant Hamiltonians in this framework possess local symmetry at each lattice site and may exhibit higher-form symmetries. There are then an exponentially large number of dynamically disconnected symmetry sectors, most of which are not translation-invariant. An exponential number of dynamically disconnected sectors, i.e., Hilbert space fragmentation, can also occur in systems in which no such symmetries have been identified. In this contribution, we describe an emergent gauge symmetry that is valid only in a subset of sectors of the fragmented $S=1$ dipole-conserving spin chain. These non-invertible symmetries can label exponentially many of the model's sectors. Simulating this Hamiltonian, which is not gauge-invariant, yields an exact quantum simulation of a gauge theory.

The 2025 run further expanded the sPHENIX dataset with high-statistics $p$+$p$, O+O and Au+Au collisions. This extensive $p$+$p$ sample opens the door to heavy-flavor measurements with orders of magnitude more statistics than previously available at RHIC. Notably, there has been no prior measurement of the $Λ_c^+ / D^0$ baseline in $p$+$p$ collisions at RHIC energies. The large sPHENIX dataset now enables the first exploration of key open questions, such as the hadronization mechanism of baryons and the strange-to-light flavor meson ratio.

Conclusion: 研讨会明确了理解这一未解现象的实验和理论优先事项，强调了跨实验平台协作和理论创新的必要性，以揭示同位旋对称性破缺背后的物理机制。

### [48] [Unraveling the Hyperon Puzzle in Neutron Stars via Novel, High-Precision Hyperon Factories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16028)
*Chang-Zheng Yuan,Marek Karliner*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用质子-质子碰撞产生超子（hyperons）作为研究核子-超子相互作用的高质量源，通过双靶实验设计实现对超子相互作用的精确测量，为解决中子星超子谜题提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核子（nucleons）间的强相互作用对可见宇宙至关重要，而超子（含奇异夸克的强子）与核子的相互作用对理解中子星本质性质至关重要。然而，与核子间相互作用（pp、pn、nn）的广泛研究相比，核子-超子相互作用（NΛ、NΣ、NΞ、NΩ等）由于缺乏合适的超子源而数据有限。

Method: 论文提出利用质子-质子碰撞（如pp→pK⁺Λ、pKΣ、pKπΣ、pKKΞ、pKKKΩ）产生超子作为高质量源。在已知动量的质子束流和液氢靶实验中，通过标记质子和K⁺介子，可以精确确定Λ超子的通量和动量。通过在主靶周围放置次级靶，这些Λ超子成为理想源，实现对Λ与多种靶核相互作用的精确研究。

Result: 该方法可产生具有精确运动学信息的高统计量超子源，为粒子物理和核物理研究提供新机遇，特别是理解中子星超子谜题（hyperon puzzle）。论文提出优化此类测量的新型高亮度双靶实验设计，该概念也可通过添加次级靶的方式整合到现有或计划中的实验中。

Conclusion: 质子-质子碰撞产生的超子可作为研究核子-超子相互作用的高质量源，双靶实验设计能实现对超子相互作用的精确测量。该方法可扩展到其他超子（Σ、Ξ、Ω）的研究，为解决中子星超子谜题提供新实验途径，并可与现有实验设施（如FAIR的HADES和CBM，HIAF的H-NS和HHaS）兼容。

Abstract: The strong forces between nucleons ($N$=$p$, $n$) are fundamental to the visible universe. The interactions between hyperons (baryons with strange quarks) and nucleons are essential for the intrinsic properties of neutron stars. Whereas the interactions between nucleons ($pp$, $pn$, $nn$) have been extensively studied, the interactions between nucleons and hyperons ($NΛ$, $NΣ$, $NΞ$, $NΩ$, ...) are not well understood, due to the small amount of relevant data, limited by the scarcity of suitable hyperon sources. Here we point out and investigate a new high-quality source: hyperons produced in $pp$ collisions, such as $pp\to pK^+Λ$, $pKΣ$, $pKπΣ$, $pKKΞ$, $pKKKΩ$. At a fixed target experiment using proton beam with known momentum and liquid hydrogen target, $pp\to pK^+Λ$ can be produced copiously. By tagging $p$ and $K^+$, the flux and momentum of the $Λ$ can be determined precisely. By placing an additional target around the primary one, these $Λ$-s serve as an ideal source, enabling an unprecedentedly precise study of $Λ$ interactions with a wide range of targets. Similar methods can be used to obtain high-quality sources of other hyperons, such as $Σ$, $Ξ$ and $Ω$. These novel, high-statistics sources of hyperons with precisely known kinematics present new opportunities for applications in particle and nuclear physics, particularly in understanding the hyperon puzzle of neutron stars. We propose a new high-luminosity experiment with two nested concentric targets, optimized for such measurements. This concept can also be incorporated into existing experiments, such as HADES and CBM at FAIR, as well as proposed experiments, such as H-NS and HHaS at HIAF, by adding a second target without significant modification of the current detectors.

</details>

### [49] [Characteristic polynomials of non-Hermitian random band matrices near the threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15355)

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了非厄米随机带矩阵特征多项式二阶关联函数的临界渐近行为，重点关注带宽W与阈值√N成比例时的临界区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究（arXiv:2510.04255）表明，非厄米随机带矩阵特征多项式二阶关联函数的渐近行为在W∼√N处存在转变。本工作旨在将相关技术扩展到临界区域，即带宽W与阈值√N成比例的情况。

Method: 通过扩展arXiv:2510.04255的技术方法，研究当带宽W与阈值√N成比例时的临界区域。该方法涉及分析N×N非厄米随机带矩阵的特征多项式关联函数。

Result: 论文发现关联函数的渐近行为在W∼√N处存在转变：当W≫√N时与Ginibre系综一致，当1≪W≪√N时呈现因子化分解。本工作重点研究了W与√N成比例的临界区域。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了先前关于非厄米随机带矩阵特征多项式关联函数临界行为的分析，重点关注了带宽W与阈值√N成比例的临界区域，深化了对该转变机制的理解。

Abstract: The paper arXiv:2510.04255 shows that the asymptotic behavior of the second correlation function of characteristic polynomials of the $N\times N$ non-Hermitian random band matrices with a bandwidth $W$ exhibits the transition at $W\sim \sqrt{N}$, as $W,N\to \infty$: it coincides with those for Ginibre ensemble for $W\gg \sqrt{N}$, and factorized as $1\ll W\ll \sqrt{N}$. In this work we extend the techniques of arXiv:2510.04255 to study the critical regime when the bandwidth $W$ is proportional to the threshold $\sqrt{N}$.

### [50] [Embedding formulae for diffraction problems on square lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16050)
*A. I. Korolkov,A. V. Kisil*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Wiener-Hopf方法，为方形晶格上的Dirichlet散射体建立了所有可能衍射问题的嵌入公式（embedding formulae），将任意平面波入射的解表示为有限个辅助问题的组合，避免了为每个入射角重新求解边界值问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为离散衍射理论中的Dirichlet散射体建立通用的嵌入公式，以克服连续介质中目前无法实现类似通用公式的限制，提高求解任意入射角衍射问题的效率。

Method: 采用Wiener-Hopf视角，首先推导了半平面、有限条带和直角楔形等典型几何的显式嵌入公式，然后通过基于算子的方法将技术推广到晶格上任意障碍物配置，建立了通用嵌入公式。

Result: 成功建立了方形晶格上Dirichlet散射问题的通用嵌入公式，该公式能将任意平面波入射的解表示为有限个辅助问题的组合，并通过数值实验验证了理论结果的正确性。

Conclusion: Wiener-Hopf方法在离散衍射理论中展现出高效性和通用性，所建立的嵌入公式与连续介质情况形成关键区别，在反问题（inverse problems）及其他物理数学领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We develop embedding formulae for all possible diffraction problems with Dirichlet scatterers on square lattices using the Wiener--Hopf perspective. The embedding formula expresses solutions for arbitrary plane-wave incidence in terms of a finite set of auxiliary problems, eliminating the need to re-solve boundary value problems for each incidence angle. First we derive explicit embedding formulae for canonical geometries including the half-plane, finite strip, and right-angled wedge. We then generalize the method through an operator-based approach, obtaining embedding formula for arbitrary configurations of obstacles on lattices. This general embedding formula is a key difference from the continuous setting where this is currently not possible. To validate the theory, we perform numerical experiments, confirming agreement with the results derived using the embedding formula. The results highlight the efficiency and generality of the Wiener--Hopf approach in discrete diffraction theory, with potential applications in inverse problems and other areas of physics and mathematics.

### [51] [Identification of optimal history variables and corresponding hereditary laws in linear viscoelasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16072)
*Ignacio Romero,Michael Ortiz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文发展了遗传本构模型（hereditary constitutive models）的算子理论表述，基于Kolmogorov N-宽度（Kolmogorov N-widths）刻画了最优有限秩内变量近似（optimal finite-rank internal-variable approximations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为计算力学中的降阶建模（reduced-order modeling）提供严格理论基础。通过建立遗传表示与内变量理论（internal-variable theories）之间的结构关系，解决传统方法缺乏理论保证的问题。

Method: 采用算子理论（operator-theoretic）方法，证明在松弛核（relaxation kernel）满足自然假设条件下，历史算子（history operator）是紧算子（compact operator），从而允许最优低秩近似（optimal low-rank approximations）。

Result: 所得降阶模型继承了热力学一致性（thermodynamic consistency）、稳定性（stability）和可证明的近似界（provable approximation bounds）。数值算例展示了近似解关于秩和采样的最优收敛性（optimal convergence）。

Conclusion: 该研究为计算力学中的降阶建模提供了严格的理论基础，建立了遗传本构模型与内变量理论之间的结构关系，并保证了近似模型的热力学一致性和稳定性。

Abstract: We develop an operator-theoretic formulation of hereditary constitutive models and characterize optimal finite-rank internal-variable approximations in the sense of Kolmogorov $N$-widths. The history operator is shown to be compact under natural assumptions on the relaxation kernel, thereby admitting optimal low-rank approximations. The resulting reduced models inherit thermodynamic consistency, stability, and provable approximation bounds. An analysis clarifies the structural relation between hereditary representations and internal-variable theories and provides a rigorous basis for reduced-order modeling in computational mechanics. Selected numerical examples showcase optimal convergence of approximations with respect to rank and sampling.

### [52] [Universal dualities for Wilson loops in lattice Yang-Mills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16252)
*Thibaut Lemoine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了格点杨-米尔斯理论（lattice Yang-Mills）中威尔逊圈（Wilson loop）期望值的普适有限N结构，适用于任意维度、U(N)规范群和平滑中心格点作用量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于识别格点杨-米尔斯理论中威尔逊圈期望值的普适数学结构，该结构应独立于具体作用量形式，适用于任意维度和平滑中心格点作用量。

Method: 方法基于不可约表示（irreducible representations）的格点标签状态和展开，将每项分解为作用量依赖的谱权重和作用量无关的拓扑系数，并通过三种精确方式分析这些系数。

Result: 结果建立了三种精确分析框架：基于装饰跨越曲面（decorated spanning surfaces）的规范/弦展开、基于对偶关联图（dual incidence graph）的局部自旋泡沫/通道模型，以及有限N主回路方程（master loop equation）。

Conclusion: 结论表明该框架能够统一处理多种格点作用量，近期威尔逊作用量的相关结果均可作为该普适作用量无关框架的特例而得到。

Abstract: We identify a universal finite-$N$ structure underlying Wilson loop expectations in lattice Yang-Mills, in any dimension $d\geq 2$, for gauge group $\mathrm{U}(N)$, and for arbitrary smooth central plaquette actions. The starting point is a state-sum expansion in plaquette labels by irreducible representations, in which each term factorizes into an action-dependent spectral weight and an action-independent topological coefficient. We then analyze these coefficients in three exact ways: as a gauge/string expansion over decorated spanning surfaces, as a local spin-foam/channel model on the dual incidence graph, and as a universal finite-$N$ master loop equation that closes on the coefficient side. As a consequence, several recent Wilson-action results are recovered as specializations of our broader action-agnostic framework.

### [53] [Dark solitons in nonlinear Su-Schrieffer-Heeger lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15634)
*Rujiang Li,Muhammad Imran,Wencai Wang,Yongtao Jia,Ying Liu*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了非线性SSH（Su-Schrieffer-Heeger）晶格中的暗孤子（dark solitons），这些孤子在非零恒定背景下保持强度凹陷，位于半无限带隙或中间有限带隙中，其强度凹陷不受原始线性晶格能带结构影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性拓扑晶格中已发现各种孤子类型，非线性SSH晶格作为最基础的拓扑模型已被扩展至非线性区域。虽然非线性边缘态和体孤子已被广泛研究，但暗孤子在非线性SSH晶格中的系统性研究仍待深入。

Method: 论文系统性地研究了非线性SSH晶格中的暗孤子，这些孤子具有非零恒定背景，在晶格体区或边缘呈现强度凹陷，并位于半无限带隙（semi-infinite gap）或中间有限带隙（middle finite gap）中。

Result: 研究发现暗孤子的强度凹陷保持完好，不受原始线性晶格能带结构影响。尽管大多数暗孤子在广泛参数范围内动态不稳定，但当胞内耦合（intracell coupling）远大于胞间耦合（intercell coupling）时，几种类型表现出线性稳定性。

Conclusion: 这些发现可能为探索非线性拓扑晶格中新型孤子提供有价值的见解，揭示了暗孤子在特定耦合条件下的稳定性特征及其与拓扑结构的相互作用。

Abstract: The introduction of nonlinearities into lattices with topological band structures has led to the discovery of various types of solitons. The Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) lattice, as the most fundamental topological model, has been extended into the nonlinear regime. In particular, nonlinear edge states and bulk solitons exhibiting intensity humps against a zero background have been extensively studied in nonlinear SSH lattices. In this paper, we systematically investigate dark solitons in nonlinear SSH lattices. These dark solitons maintain a nonzero and constant background, featuring intensity dips either in the bulk of the lattice or at its edges, and residing spectrally in the semi-infinite gap or the middle finite gap. Regardless of the specific type of dark soliton, the intensity dip remains wellpreserved and is not affected by the band structure of the original linear lattice. Although the dark solitons we have identified are generally dynamically unstable across a broad range of parameters, several types exhibit linear stability when the intracell coupling is much larger than the intercell coupling. Our findings may provide valuable insights for the exploration of novel types of solitons in nonlinear topological lattices.

### [54] [Ultrastrong Coupling Signatures in Photon Statistics from Terahertz Higgs-Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15417)
*Spenser Talkington,Benjamin Kass,Martin Claassen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了超强耦合（ultrastrong coupling）在腔体嵌入超导体中的可测试特征，通过分析透射光的量子光子统计，发现双光子希格斯极化激元（Higgs polariton）在强耦合下实现了单太赫兹光子级别的光子非线性，为超强耦合提供了新的诊断方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 腔体光子与量子材料的超强耦合（ultrastrong coupling）已成为调控材料性质的新途径，但明确的超强耦合特征仍然难以捕捉。研究旨在寻找超强耦合的可测试特征，特别是在腔体嵌入超导体系统中。

Method: 研究聚焦于通过腔体嵌入超导体的透射光的量子光子统计（quantum photon statistics），推导了非马尔可夫输入输出关系（non-Markovian input output relation），并以2H-NbSe2超导体为例，研究其接近超强光-物质耦合的过程。

Result: 研究发现强耦合下的双光子希格斯极化激元（two-photon Higgs polariton）实现了单太赫兹光子级别的光子非线性。随着光-物质耦合增强，光子统计显示出显著变化，这是由于形成了具有有限光子占据数的混合光子-物质暗腔态（dark-cavity state）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了超强耦合在双光子符合统计（two-photon coincidence statistics）中的诊断特征，这一特征在总计数中不存在，为超强耦合提供了新的实验验证方法。

Abstract: The ultrastrong coupling regime of cavity photons and quantum materials has emerged as a pathway to modify materials properties, however definitive signatures of ultrastrong coupling remain elusive. Focusing on the quantum photon statistics of light transmitted through a cavity-embedded superconductor, we show that a two-photon Higgs polariton at strong coupling realizes a photonic nonlinearity at the single terahertz photon level. We find that as light-matter coupling increases, the photon statistics show pronounced changes due to the formation of a hybrid photon-matter dark-cavity state with finite photon occupancy, producing testable signatures of ultrastrong coupling. We derive a non-Markovian input output relation and study the cavity-embedded superconductor 2H-NbSe2 as it approaches ultrastrong light-matter coupling. Our results reveal a diagnostic for ultrastrong coupling in the two-photon coincidence statistics that is absent in total counts.

### [55] [Inelastic neutron scattering study on the AFM uniform spin-1/2 chain compound CuSb2O6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15608)
*Masashi Hasea,Minoru Soda,Takatsugu Masuda,Shinichi Itoh,Tetsuya Yokoo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究CuSb2O6这一反铁磁均匀自旋-1/2链化合物的磁激发特性，特别是低于反铁磁转变温度（TN = 8.7 K）时出现的能隙现象及其物理起源。

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）实验对粉末样品进行测量，在2.5 K（低于TN）和12.5 K（高于TN）两个温度下观测磁激发谱。

Result: 在2.5 K观测到1.8-13 meV能量范围内的磁激发，其中1.8 meV能隙值与比热测量结果（1.51 meV）接近；高于TN时激发变为无能隙；能隙激发在0.48处最强，对应0.66 nm长度，与理论预测的0.65562 nm Cu对最强相互作用一致。

Conclusion: 磁激发可用反铁磁均匀XXZ链模型描述，参数为Jab = 6.437 meV和DJab = 0.063 meV；1.8 meV能隙源于小的伊辛各向异性（DJab/Jab = 0.0098），即自旋波激发中的各向异性所致。

Abstract: We carried out inelastic neutron scattering experiments on a powdered sample of the antiferromagnetic (AFM) uniform spin-1/2 chain compound CuSb2O6.The magnetic excitations appear in the energy range of 1.8 to 13 meV at 2.5 K below the AFM transition temperature (TN = 8.7 K).The gap value (1.8 meV) is close to that evaluated from the specific heat (1.51 meV). The excitations at 12.5 K (> TN) appear gapless. Thus, the 1.8 meV gap is caused by some anisotropy in spin-wave excitations. The gap excitations are strongest at 0.48 corresponding to a length of 0.66 nm. This result is consistent with the theoretical one that the interaction in a Cu pair with a length of 0.65562 nm (Jab) is strongest. The magnetic excitations can be explained by the AFM uniform XXZ chain with Jab = 6.437 meV and DJab = 0.063 meV. The 1.8 meV gap is caused by the small Ising anisotropy (DJab/Jab = 0.0098).

### [56] [Inductance Meets Memory in the Quantum Magnet Mn3Si2Te6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15635)
*Tristan R. Cao,Gabriel Schebel,Arabella Quane,Hengdi Zhao,Yu Zhang,Feng Ye,Longji Cui,Gang Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究发现在铁磁体Mn3Si2Te6中，手性轨道电流（chiral orbital currents）的非平衡重构能同时产生本征电感和非易失性忆阻特性，揭示了轨道自由度作为一类量子状态变量同时编码反应性和记忆功能的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道自由度（orbital degrees of freedom）为关联量子材料中的涌现动力学现象提供了尚未充分探索的途径。然而，集体轨道态是否能在体系统中本征地同时产生反应性和记忆功能仍不清楚。

Method: 研究以铁磁体Mn3Si2Te6为模型系统，通过分析手性轨道电流的非平衡重构行为，在不同频率和磁场条件下测量其电学响应特性。

Result: 在低频和沿c轴磁场下，相干轨道电流域产生稳健的顺时针感应I-V环；在高频和低场下，电流驱动的一阶重构导致不完全反转和亚稳态俘获，产生本征电动势和零电流时的有限剩余电压。

Conclusion: 研究确立了轨道电流作为一类量子状态变量，能够同时编码反应性和记忆功能，为开发本征可重构和能量高效的电子系统开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Orbital degrees of freedom offer a largely untapped route to emergent dynamical phenomena in correlated quantum materials. However, it remains unclear whether collective orbital states can intrinsically generate both reactive and memory functionalities in a bulk system. Here we show that in the ferrimagnet Mn3Si2Te6, nonequilibrium reconfiguration of chiral orbital currents produces both emergent inductance and nonvolatile memristance as intrinsic properties of a single crystal. At low frequency and under a magnetic field along the c axis, coherent orbital-current domains generate robust clockwise inductive I-V loops. At higher frequency and low field, current-driven first-order reconfiguration leads to incomplete reversal and metastable trapping, producing an intrinsic electromotive force and a finite remanent voltage at zero current. These results establish orbital currents as a class of quantum state variables that encode both reactive and memory functionalities, opening routes toward intrinsically reconfigurable and energy-efficient electronic systems.

### [57] [Enhancing Neural-Network Variational Monte Carlo through Basis Transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15888)
*Zhixuan Liu,Dongheng Qian,Jing Wang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯基变换的神经网络变分蒙特卡洛方法，通过引入可学习的局域性参数α来重塑目标基态波函数，从而在不增加神经网络复杂度的情况下提升变分表达能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络变分蒙特卡洛（NNVMC）已成为解决量子多体问题的有力工具，但系统提升其精度的途径仍主要依赖启发式方法。需要在不增加神经网络架构复杂性的前提下，寻找提升变分表达能力的新途径。

Method: 提出了一种物理驱动的基变换方法，将多体波函数表述在高斯基中，引入单个可学习的局域性参数α来重塑目标基态，使其更易于学习。该方法计算开销极小，可与现有神经网络架构（如FermiNet和消息传递神经网络）直接结合。

Result: 以三维均匀电子气为基准测试，优化的基变换能持续降低FermiNet和消息传递神经网络的变分能量。特别地，对于后者，该方法能更精确地确定费米液体到维格纳晶体的相变。

Conclusion: 基变换为提升连续空间中NNVMC的精度提供了新途径，表明不仅可以通过改进变分波函数来提升精度，还可以通过使目标基态更易于表示来实现。该方法具有广泛适用性，为量子多体问题的数值研究提供了新思路。

Abstract: Neural-network variational Monte Carlo (NNVMC) has emerged as a powerful tool for solving quantum many-body problems, yet systematic pathways for improving its accuracy remain largely heuristic. Here, we introduce a physically motivated basis transformation for NNVMC that enhances variational expressivity without increasing the complexity of the neural-network ansatz itself. By formulating the many-body wave function in a Gaussian basis, we introduce a single learnable locality parameter, $α$, that reshapes the target ground state into a more learnable representation. This approach introduces minimal computational overhead and can be readily combined with existing neural-network architectures. Using the three-dimensional homogeneous electron gas as a benchmark, we show that the optimized basis transformation consistently lowers the variational energy for both FermiNet and message-passing neural-network architectures. Notably, for the latter, it enables a more precise determination of the Fermi liquid to Wigner crystal phase transition. More broadly, our results highlight basis transformation as a new route to improving NNVMC in continuous space, showing that accuracy can be enhanced not only by refining the ansatz but also by making the target ground state easier to represent.

</details>


### [58] [Experimental quantification of electronic symmetry breaking through orbital hybridization phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15906)
*Shungo Aoyagi,Shunsuke Kitou,Yuiga Nakamura,Taka-hisa Arima,Naoya Kanazawa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体结构的对称性分类对预测材料物理性质至关重要，但仅能确定哪些物理响应是允许的，而响应大小由电子态中的对称性破缺程度决定。目前仅少数情况（如电极化和磁化）有明确定量的电子对称性破缺描述符，大多数类型（包括手性）缺乏类似描述符。

Method: 提出通过价电子密度分布各向异性来量化电子对称性破缺的实验框架，证明在位置对称性约束下可唯一确定控制各向异性的轨道杂化相位。将该框架应用于结构手性过渡金属硅化物，通过同步辐射X射线衍射观测的价电子密度确定杂化相位。

Result: 从获得的复杂杂化中量化了电子手性χ，理论上证明χ与圆二色性直接成正比，从而确立χ作为手性响应的预测描述符。该方法可系统应用于各种点群。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种量化电子对称性破缺和预测相关物理性质的通用途径，通过电子手性χ建立了对称性破缺与物理响应之间的定量关系，为材料设计提供了新工具。

Abstract: Symmetry classification of crystal structures has been central to predicting physical properties of materials. While such structural classification identifies which physical responses are symmetry-allowed, the magnitudes of these responses are governed by the degree of symmetry breaking in the electronic state. However, a well-defined quantitative descriptor for the electronic symmetry breaking has been established only in limited cases such as electric polarization and magnetization. No analogous descriptor exists for most other types, including chirality. Here, we propose an experimental framework for quantifying electronic symmetry breaking from the anisotropy of valence electron density distribution. We show that the orbital hybridization phases governing this anisotropy can be uniquely determined under site symmetry constraints. Applying this framework to structurally chiral transition-metal silicides, we determine hybridization phases from their valence electron densities observed by synchrotron X-ray diffraction. From the obtained complex hybridization, we quantify an electronic chirality $χ$ and theoretically demonstrate that it is directly proportional to circular dichroism, establishing $χ$ as a predictive descriptor of chiral responses. This approach is systematically applicable to various point groups, offering a general route to quantifying electronic symmetry breaking and predicting associated physical properties.

### [59] [Ultrafast Current Switching from Quantum Geometry in Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15924)
*Youngjae Kim,Sejoong Kim,Jun-Won Rhim*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出具有非平凡量子几何（non-trivial quantum geometry）特征的半金属系统可作为超快开关的潜在平台，其电流在施加适度电场时瞬时产生并达到稳态值，在开关速度上优于传统材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代电子技术的发展需要实现更快开关速度并降低能耗。由于器件运行速度受限于材料固有特性，因此识别具有内在优越开关能力的系统至关重要。

Method: 研究提出量子几何半金属（quantum geometric semimetals）作为超快开关平台，包括二次能带接触半金属（quadratic band-touching semimetals）和奇异平带（singular flat bands）系统。通过希尔伯特-施密特量子距离（Hilbert-Schmidt quantum distance）控制的带间耦合机制分析电流瞬时响应特性。

Result: 量子几何半金属在施加适度外电场时电流瞬时产生并达到稳态值，在周期性光脉冲下表现出快速稳定的开关行为。其开关速度优于传统金属、半导体和石墨烯。研究还提出了对无带隙和有带隙量子几何半金属电导率的普适分类。

Conclusion: 第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）表明双层石墨烯、环状石墨烯、单层铋和V3F8等材料可实现预测的瞬时电流开关，时变密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory）模拟进一步支持了这一结论。

Abstract: Technological progress towards next-generation electronics critically relies on achieving faster switching with reduced energy consumption. Because device operation speeds are fundamentally constrained by the intrinsic properties of constituent materials, identifying systems with inherently superior switching capabilities is essential. Here, we propose that semimetallic systems characterized by non-trivial quantum geometry, including quadratic band-touching semimetals and singular flat bands, can serve as a promising platform for ultrafast switching at voltages compatible with modern electronics. We show that, in such quantum geometric semimetals, an electric current is generated instantaneously upon application of a moderate external electric field, reaching its steady-state value. As a consequence, the current exhibits rapid and stable on-off switching behaviour under periodic optical pulse trains, demonstrating robustness under experimentally feasible conditions. In terms of switching speed, this quantum geometric semimetal outperforms conventional metals, semiconductors, and graphene. We identify the microscopic origin of this behaviour as interband coupling governed by the Hilbert-Schmidt quantum distance, together with a finite density of states at the band-touching point. This mechanism further leads to a universal classification of conductivity for both gapless and gapped quantum geometric semimetals. Finally, first-principles calculations suggest realistic material platforms, including bilayer graphene, cyclic graphene, monolayer bismuth and V3F8-in which the predicted instantaneous current switching can be directly realized, further supported by time-dependent density functional theory simulations performed for representative systems.

### [60] [Antiferromagnetic Dimers in the Parent Phase of a Correlated Kagome Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15935)
*Yifan Wang,Chenchao Xu,Yi Liu,Jinke Bao,Jiayu Guo,Xiaoran Yang,Yuiga Nakamura,Hiroshi Fukui,Taishun Manjo,Daisuke Ishikawa,Alfred Q. R. Baron,Saizheng Cao,Rui Li,Zilong Li,Yanan Zhang,Ruihan Chen,Ming Shi,Huiqiu Yuan,Guanghan Cao,Chao Cao,Yu Song*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究解析了CsCr₃Sb₅中4×1电荷密度波（CDW）的晶体结构，揭示了其由Cr二聚体和Cr链组成，并发现压力下交织的CDW与磁序被抑制后出现超导穹顶，表明涨落反铁磁二聚体可能在超导电子配对中起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome金属因其平带电子结构而易于出现电荷密度波（charge-density wave, CDW）、磁性和超导相。与弱关联的AV₃Sb₅（A = K, Rb, Cs）具有2×2 CDW不同，CsCr₃Sb₅是关联金属，其平带靠近费米能级，并展现出与磁序交织的4×1 CDW，这为研究关联物理提供了独特平台。

Method: 研究通过解析CsCr₃Sb₅中4×1 CDW态的晶体结构，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析交换相互作用。结构解析显示该CDW态由Cr二聚体（Cr dimers）和Cr链组成。

Result: CsCr₃Sb₅的CDW相变比AV₃Sb₅更强烈的一级相变，且在CDW转变温度之上没有显著的软声子或漫散射。第一性原理计算表明主要交换相互作用在二聚体内为反铁磁性（antiferromagnetic），而链内及二聚体-链间耦合较弱。压力下交织序被抑制，出现从非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）正常态演化的超导穹顶。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，涨落反铁磁二聚体（fluctuating antiferromagnetic dimers）可能在CsCr₃Sb₅的超导电子配对中起主要作用，这为理解Kagome金属中关联电子现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: Kagome metals are prone to charge-density wave (CDW), magnetic, and superconducting phases, with their flat electronic band conducive for correlated physics. In contrast to the weakly correlated $A$V$_3$Sb$_5$ ($A$ = K, Rb, Cs) kagome metals with a $2\times2$ CDW, CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$ is a correlated metal with a flat band close to the Fermi level, and exhibits a $4\times1$ CDW intertwined with magnetic order. Under pressure, the intertwined orders are suppressed and give way to a dome of superconductivity that emerges from a non-Fermi liquid normal state. Here, we solve the crystal structure of the $4\times 1$ CDW state in CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$, and show it consists of Cr dimers separated by Cr chains. First-principles calculations show the dominant exchange interaction is antiferromagnetic within the dimers, while the intra-chain and dimer-chain couplings are much weaker. The CDW transition of CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$ is found to be more strongly first-order than those in $A$V$_3$Sb$_5$, without significant soft phonons or diffuse scattering above the CDW transition temperature. These findings suggest that fluctuating antiferromagnetic dimers may play a major role in the electron pairing of superconducting CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$.

### [61] [Extension of the iterated perturbation theory at arbitrary fillings to nonequilibrium steady states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15942)
*Tommaso Maria Mazzocchi,Enrico Arrigoni*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是将Kajueter-Kotliar迭代微扰理论（KK-IPT）从平衡态扩展到非平衡稳态，并应用于远离半填充的情况。这旨在为相关杂质量子输运问题提供有效的数值计算方法。

Method: 采用非平衡KK-IPT方法，并与辅助主方程方法（AMEA）进行基准测试。AMEA在平衡和非平衡状态下都具有可控的精度，因此作为验证标准。研究重点考察了相关杂质量子输运中的微分电导和谱函数。

Result: 在平衡态下，KK-IPT在不同填充情况下都能高精度地复现AMEA结果，包括谱性质和电子密度。在非平衡态下，两种方法在中等温度和偏压参数范围内表现出很好的一致性，特别是在AMEA可靠的参数区间内。

Conclusion: 非平衡KK-IPT可作为远离半填充非平衡稳态的近似描述方法。虽然在低温低偏压区域缺乏可控基准测试，但非平衡KK-IPT在这些区域保持数值稳定性，可能为该参数区间提供有用的替代计算方法。

Abstract: We extend the Kajueter-Kotliar [Phys. Rev. Lett. 77, 131 (1996)] iterated perturbation theory (KK-IPT) away from half filling to nonequilibrium steady states. We benchmark the resulting nonequilibrium KK-IPT approach against the auxiliary master equation approach (AMEA), whose accuracy is controlled in and out of equilibrium. As expected, in equilibrium, KK-IPT reproduces the AMEA results for different fillings with high accuracy at the level of both spectral properties and electron densities. Out of equilibrium, we study quantum transport across a correlated impurity and compute the differential conductance and spectral functions. We find very good agreement between nonequilibrium KK-IPT and AMEA in the parameter regime where the latter is reliable, in particular at moderate temperatures and biases. These results support nonequilibrium KK-IPT as an approximate description of nonequilibrium steady states away from half filling. Although a controlled benchmark is not available in the low-temperature, low-bias regime, where AMEA becomes less reliable, nonequilibrium KK-IPT remains numerically stable in those regions, suggesting that it may provide a useful alternative for nonequilibrium calculations in this regime.

*Ryosuke Yamashita,Shintaro Takayoshi,Takahiro Morimoto*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过比较二阶非线性电导率和双自旋子激发谱，确认自旋子激发是量子自旋链中直流电流产生的根源，且该体光伏效应通过位移电流机制由自旋子携带的电极化驱动。

Abstract: We theoretically study direct current generation in a quantum spin chain induced by spinon excitations by light irradiation. We consider a s=1/2 1D antiferromagnetic XXZ model with magnetoelectric coupling that describes multiferroics with broken inversion symmetry. We perform the real-time simulation using infinite time-evolving block decimation (iTEBD), and demonstrate the direct current generation under light irradiation. By comparing the second order nonlinear conductivity and the two-spinon excitation spectra of 1D XXZ model, we confirm that the spinon excitations are the origin for the direct current generation in the quantum spin chain. We find that the bulk photovoltaic effect is driven by electric polarization carried by the spinons through the shift current mechanism, and thus is regarded as ``the spinon shift current''.

### [63] [Fluctuating Pair Density Wave in Finite-temperature Phase Diagram of the $t$-$t^\prime$ Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16293)
*Qiaoyi Li,Yang Qi,Wei Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 使用热张量网络方法研究t-t' Hubbard模型的温度-掺杂相图，发现电子掺杂侧存在d波超导相，而空穴掺杂侧未检测到稳健的d波超导相，取而代之的是强对密度波涨落主导的有限温度区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hubbard模型及其扩展是理解关联电子态（包括高温超导铜氧化物中的电子态）的标准理论框架。研究旨在通过先进的热张量网络方法，探索t-t' Hubbard模型的温度-掺杂相图，为高温超导体的配对不稳定性和奇异电子态提供新见解。

Method: 采用最先进的热张量网络方法（thermal tensor network method），系统地绘制了t-t' Hubbard模型的温度-掺杂相图。该方法能够处理有限温度下的关联电子系统，为研究高温超导体的配对机制提供了有效的数值工具。

Result: 在电子掺杂侧发现了d波超导（dSC）区域，支持高温超导的物理图像。在空穴掺杂侧未检测到稳健的dSC相，而是出现了由强对密度波（PDW）涨落主导的有限温度区域，该区域可能随进一步冷却转变为电荷密度波序。PDW态表现出净动量接近(0, π)的弧间配对，与传统dSC的零动量配对不同，且这些涨落的PDW态占据了空穴掺杂侧赝能隙区的下部区域。

Conclusion: 研究提供了与先前基态研究一致的全面有限温度视角，为高温超导体中的配对不稳定性和奇异电子态提供了新的理解。空穴掺杂侧强PDW涨落的存在及其与赝能隙区的关系，揭示了高温超导机制中可能的新物理图像。

Abstract: The Hubbard model and its extensions are canonical theoretical frameworks for understanding correlated electronic states, including those in high-$T_c$ cuprates. Here, we use state-of-the-art thermal tensor network method to map out the temperature-doping phase diagram of the $t$-$t^\prime$ Hubbard model. On the electron-doped side, we find a $d$-wave superconducting (dSC) regime, supporting the scenario of high-$T_c$ superconductivity. In contrast, on the hole-doped side, no robust dSC phase is detected. Instead, a finite-temperature regime dominated by strong pair-density-wave (PDW) fluctuations emerges, which may eventually give way to charge density wave order upon further cooling. The PDW state exhibits inter-arc pairing with net momentum near $(0, π)$, distinct from the zero-momentum pairing in conventional dSC. Furthermore, these fluctuating PDW states occupy the lower portion of the pseudogap regime on the hole-doped side. We provide a comprehensive finite-temperature perspective consistent with previous ground-state studies, shedding new light on pairing instabilities and exotic electronic states in high-$T_c$ superconductors.

### [65] [Converting non-Hermitian degeneracies of any order: Hierarchies of exceptional points and degeneracy manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16139)
*Grigory A. Starkov,Sharareh Sayyad*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非厄米物理中贬义例外点（derogatory EPs）的特性，展示了在微小扰动下如何将其转换为不同结构的例外点而不改变总简并度，并建立了简并层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米物理中各种简并类型的出现对优化和调控不同物理现象至关重要。研究聚焦于贬义例外点（derogatory Exceptional Points），这类点具有对应同一特征值的多个若尔当块（Jordan blocks）。

Method: 通过分析在微小扰动下贬义例外点转换为不同结构例外点的可能性，研究了简并层次结构。系统探索了无对称性和存在伪厄米对称性（pseudo-Hermitian symmetry）两种情况下的层次结构。

Result: 研究表明贬义例外点可在保持总简并度不变的情况下转换为不同结构的例外点，这种转换能增大最大若尔当块尺寸，从而增强特征谱对参数变化的敏感性。建立了相同阶数简并的层次结构。

Conclusion: 该研究促进了非厄米系统各种简并的工程化设计，为扩展非厄米物理的应用意义开辟了道路。

Abstract: The emergence of various types of degeneracies plays a crucial role in optimizing and engineering different physical phenomena in non-Hermitian physics. In our work, we focus on the derogatory Exceptional Points (EPs), which are characterized by multiple Jordan blocks corresponding to the same eigenvalue. We demonstrate that, under certain infinitesimal perturbations, a derogatory EP can be converted into an EP of different structure without varying the total order of degeneracy. In particular, such conversion can increase the size of the largest Jordan block and, hence, the sensitivity of the eigenspectrum to parameter variation, which is an important feature for practical applications. Furthermore, by analyzing all possible conversions, we introduce hierarchies of degeneracies of the same order that appear when perturbing non-Hermitian systems. We systematically explore hierarchies in the absence of any symmetry and when pseudo-Hermitian symmetry is present. Our study facilitates engineering various degeneracies of non-Hermitian systems, paving the way to extending the implications of non-Hermitian physics.

</details>

Abstract: The presence of degeneracies plays a crucial role in describing the behavior of non-Hermitian (NH) systems. Abstract: It is well-known that any two pure quantum states (in the same Hilbert space) can be mapped to any other using unitary transformations. Method: 研究采用非线性薛定谔方程（nonlinear Schrödinger equation）描述动力学，并补充了一个现象学的排斥项以确保高密度下的正则性。通过变分高斯拟设（variational Gaussian ansatz），推导出显式的有效能量泛函。

Abstract: We propose an effective non-relativistic framework in which wave-function collapse emerges as a deterministic dynamical instability induced by gravitational self-interaction and regulated by short-distance repulsion. The dynamics is described by a nonlinear Schrödinger equation supplemented by a phenomenological repulsive sector ensuring regularity at high densities. This loss of stability is associated with a bifurcation in the reduced dynamical system governing the wave-function width, leading to the emergence of stable localized configurations. Within this picture, collapse corresponds to the dynamical selection of one of these localized attractors, driven by infinitesimal asymmetries in the initial state and occurring without stochastic noise or environmental coupling. Possible implications for mesoscopic systems probing the quantum-to-classical transition are briefly discussed.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用耦合链XX模型（XX model on coupled chains），研究畴壁初始态（domain-wall initial states）的动力学演化。基于Lanczos算法（Lanczos algorithm）分析，识别热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下的局域化相变（localization transition）。

Result: 发现畴壁初始态在任意长时间内保持非均匀磁化分布，这源于手性对称性（chiral symmetry）保护的指数多零模（exponentially many zero modes）。在临界耦合强度处观察到局域化相变，反铁磁缺陷（antiferromagnetic defects）和对称性破坏微扰（symmetry-breaking perturbations）恢复缓慢热化，而对称性守恒微扰下非遍历性保持稳健。

Conclusion: 简并的对称性保护子空间（degenerate, symmetry-protected subspaces）可在实验可及量子系统中产生热力学稳定的非遍历动力学，为理解量子多体系统中的热化破坏提供了新机制。

Abstract: Understanding mechanisms for the breakdown of thermalization in closed quantum systems is a central problem in quantum many-body physics. We demonstrate strong non-ergodic behavior in the XX model on coupled chains, where domain-wall initial states retain an inhomogeneous magnetization profile for arbitrarily long times. We find that this effect arises due to exponentially many zero modes protected by chiral symmetry. Using an analysis based on the Lanczos algorithm, we identify a localization transition in the thermodynamic limit at a critical coupling between the chains. We further show that antiferromagnetic defects in the initial state and symmetry-breaking perturbations restore slow thermalization, whereas it remains robust for symmetry-conserving perturbations. These results establish that degenerate, symmetry-protected subspaces can give rise to thermodynamically stable non-ergodic dynamics in experimentally accessible quantum systems.

### [71] [Deterministic multiphoton bundle emission via interference-interaction control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15605)

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于干涉-相互作用工程的方案，用于在腔量子电动力学（cavity-QED）系统中实现可编程的少光子发射。通过结合可调谐的腔介导自旋交换相互作用χ和可控几何相位φ，该方案能够选择性寻址不同激发流形（N=1,2,3），实现高纯度的单光子、双光子和三光子发射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种干涉-相互作用工程（interference-interaction-engineered）方案，采用三个原子与正交腔模式耦合的腔-QED系统。通过绝热消除辅助法布里-珀罗腔（Fabry-Pérot cavity），生成可调谐的腔介导自旋交换相互作用χ，并结合可控几何相位φ，重塑多体缀饰态（many-body dressed-state）谱。

Result: 该方案实现了对不同激发流形（excitation manifolds）的选择性寻址，建立了激发结构与光子发射通道的直接映射。当φ=0时，相长干涉（constructive interference）增强了低激发流形的光谱非谐性（spectral anharmonicity），产生可调谐的单光子和双光子发射。当φ=2π/3时，相消干涉（destructive interference）抑制低阶激发路径，激活源自N=3流形的共振三光子通道。腔介导相互作用χ进一步增强了流形间的光谱分离，显著提高了多光子纯度，同时保持可观的光子布居。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一的干涉-相互作用框架，其中有效光学非线性（effective optical nonlinearities）可通过相位和相互作用进行可编程工程化。这为高纯度多光子源（high-purity multiphoton sources）和可编程量子光子器件（programmable quantum photonic devices）提供了一条可扩展的路径，实现了双光子纯度三个数量级的增强和三光子发射两个数量级的改进。

Abstract: The controlled generation of nonclassical light beyond single photons remains a central challenge in quantum optics, due to the difficulty of enhancing multiphoton processes while suppressing lower-order excitations. Here we propose an interference-interaction-engineered scheme for programmable few-photon emission in a cavity-QED system of three atoms coupled to orthogonal cavity modes. By adiabatically eliminating an auxiliary Fabry-Pérot cavity, we generate a tunable cavity-mediated spin-exchange interaction $χ$, which, combined with a controllable geometric phase $φ$, reshapes the many-body dressed-state spectrum. This interplay enables selective addressing of excitation manifolds ($N=1,2,3$), establishing a direct mapping between excitation structure and photon-emission channels. For $φ=0$, constructive interference enhances the spectral anharmonicity of low-excitation manifolds, yielding tunable single- and two-photon emission associated with the $N=1$ and $N=2$ manifolds. In contrast, for $φ=2π/3$, destructive interference suppresses lower-order excitation pathways and activates a resonant three-photon channel originating from the $N=3$ manifold. Importantly, the cavity-mediated interaction $χ$ further enhances spectral separation between manifolds, enabling a substantial improvement in multiphoton purity while maintaining a sizable photon population. We demonstrate a three-order-of-magnitude enhancement in two-photon purity and more than two orders of magnitude improvement in three-photon emission. Our results establish a unified interference-interaction framework in which effective optical nonlinearities can be programmably engineered through phase and interaction, providing a scalable route toward high-purity multiphoton sources and programmable quantum photonic devices.

### [75] [Discovering quantum phenomena with Interpretable Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16015)

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合变分自编码器和符号方法的可解释机器学习框架，能够从无标签量子数据中自动发现物理规律和序参量，并在多种量子系统中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可解释机器学习技术正成为从复杂量子数据中提取物理洞察的重要工具。当前需要能够从广泛的无标签量子数据集中学习物理意义明确且可解释表示的方法。

Method: 基于变分自编码器（variational autoencoders）的最新进展，从原始测量数据中学习表示，并进一步用符号方法增强学习流程，以发现紧凑的解析描述符作为序参量。

Result: 该框架在实验性里德堡原子快照、簇伊辛模型的经典阴影以及混合离散-连续费米子数据上进行了验证，揭示了先前未报告的现象，如里德堡阵列中的角序模式。

Conclusion: 这些结果为从多样化量子数据集中自动且可解释地发现物理定律建立了一个通用框架，所有方法通过开源Python库qdisc向更广泛社区提供。

Abstract: Interpretable machine learning techniques are becoming essential tools for extracting physical insights from complex quantum data. We build on recent advances in variational autoencoders to demonstrate that such models can learn physically meaningful and interpretable representations from a broad class of unlabeled quantum datasets. From raw measurement data alone, the learned representation reveals rich information about the underlying structure of quantum phase spaces. We further augment the learning pipeline with symbolic methods, enabling the discovery of compact analytical descriptors that serve as order parameters for the distinct regimes emerging in the learned representations. We demonstrate the framework on experimental Rydberg-atom snapshots, classical shadows of the cluster Ising model, and hybrid discrete-continuous fermionic data, revealing previously unreported phenomena such as a corner-ordering pattern in the Rydberg arrays. These results establish a general framework for the automated and interpretable discovery of physical laws from diverse quantum datasets. All methods are available through qdisc, an open-source Python library designed to make these tools accessible to the broader community.

### [76] [Boson correlations are spurious for classical states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16283)
*Daniel E. Salazar,Fabrice P. Laussy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了玻色子关联（boson correlations）与辛普森悖论（Simpson paradox）之间的联系，指出经典量子态中的玻色子关联本质上是统计平均产生的伪相关，源于对称性破缺作为混杂因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在澄清量子关联的本质，特别是对于具有Glauber-Sudarshan表示的经典量子态（包括相干态、热态等），其玻色子关联的起源需要重新审视。

Method: 通过分析具有良好概率分布的Glauber-Sudarshan表示的量子态密度矩阵，揭示玻色子关联与辛普森悖论之间的对应关系，区分量子平均与统计平均。

Result: 研究发现经典量子态的玻色子关联是统计平均产生的伪相关，源于对称性破缺作为混杂因素，波函数编码的玻色子关联在假设的几何结构中形成，但该几何结构在统计系综中并不固定。

Conclusion: 该研究强调需要区分量子平均与统计平均，为理解非经典性（nonclassicality）和量子优势（quantum advantage）等基本问题提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We show that boson correlations from quantum states with a Glauber-Sudarshan representation of their density matrix which provides a well-behaved probability distribution -- including coherent states, thermal states, and all states that can be deemed classical -- are a manifestation of the Simpson paradox: they are spurious correlations from statistical (ensemble) averages over uncorrelated measurements made in varying geometries, due to a process of symmetry-breaking as a confounding factor. Bosonic correlations encoded by the wavefunction appear to be formed in the geometry assumed, which however is not that of the statistical ensemble but varies from realization to realization. This calls to distinguish between quantum and statistical averages and sheds new understandings on the fundamental problems of nonclassicality and quantum advantage.

</details>

### [77] [Exact Analysis of a One-Dimensional Yang-Gaudin Model with Two-Body Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15595)
*Ryutaro Katsuta,Shun Uchino*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 一维杨-高丁模型（Yang-Gaudin model）在存在二体损失（two-body loss）时仍保持精确可解性，无论粒子是玻色子还是费米子。通过将Lindblad算符谱与非厄米有效哈密顿量（non-Hermitian effective Hamiltonian）的右本征值关联，推导了初始粒子损失率的通用表达式，并揭示了耗散对自旋构型稳定性的反转效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维杨-高丁模型在存在二体损失时的精确可解性，探索耗散对玻色子和费米子系统自旋构型稳定性的影响。该工作旨在理解开放量子系统中精确可解模型的行为特征。

Method: 通过将Lindblad算符谱与通过复化相互作用强度得到的非厄米有效哈密顿量的右本征值相关联。精确求解了二体问题，并分析了玻色子单重态（bosonic singlet sector）和多体系统（many-body systems）的行为。

Result: 在玻色子单重态中，有效哈密顿量具有实右本征值，主方程存在稳态解。对于三体或更多粒子的多体系统，耗散反转了自旋构型的稳定性：玻色子系统倾向于反铁磁类构型（antiferromagnetic-like configurations），而费米子系统倾向于铁磁类构型（ferromagnetic-like configurations）。

Conclusion: 一维杨-高丁模型在二体损失下保持精确可解性，耗散对玻色子和费米子系统的自旋构型稳定性产生相反影响，揭示了开放量子系统中粒子统计与耗散相互作用的非平凡效应。

Abstract: We show that the one-dimensional Yang-Gaudin model with two-body loss remains exactly solvable irrespective of whether constituent particles are bosons or fermions. By relating the Liouvillian spectrum to the right eigenvalues of a non-Hermitian effective Hamiltonian obtained by complexifying the interaction strength, we derive a general expression for the initial particle-loss rate. We then solve the two-body problem exactly and show that, in the bosonic singlet sector, the effective Hamiltonian has real right eigenvalues and the master equation admits steady-state solutions. For many-body systems with three or more particles, we further show that dissipation reverses which spin configurations are most stable: in bosonic systems it favors antiferromagnetic-like configurations over ferromagnetic-like ones, whereas in fermionic systems it favors ferromagnetic-like configurations over antiferromagnetic-like ones.

### [78] [Coupled-channels method for the scattering hypervolume in ultracold atomic three-body collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15815)
*P. J. P. Kersbergen,J. van de Kraats,D. J. M. Ahmed-Braun,S. J. J. M. F. Kokkelmans*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于全同玻色碱金属原子弹性三体散射的新型耦合通道方法，该方法基于数值精确的双体离壳跃迁矩阵，能够精确计算三体散射超体积这一关键物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理具有深分子势和多束缚态的碱金属原子三体散射时存在局限性。需要发展一种能够精确捕捉短程物理和多通道耦合特性的方法，避免使用模型赝势（pseudopotentials）。

Method: 该方法基于数值精确的双体离壳（off-the-energy-shell）跃迁矩阵，该矩阵由支持多个束缚态的现实多通道分子相互作用势构建。通过严格考虑离壳结构，方法能够捕捉短程物理和多通道耦合特性。

Result: 核心输出是复三体散射超体积（three-body scattering hypervolume）——双体散射长度的三体类比。以自旋极化的钾-39（potassium-39）为现实基准，在实验相关条件下进行了全耦合通道三体散射计算并提取了超体积。

Conclusion: 该方法具有普适性和可移植性，适用于其他原子种类和具有任意多束缚态的深分子势的相互作用模型，能够以可控且可验证的数值精度获得三体散射超体积。

Abstract: We introduce a novel coupled-channels method for elastic three-body scattering in systems of identical bosonic alkali-metal atoms. The approach relies on the numerically exact two-body off-the-energy-shell transition matrix, constructed from realistic multichannel molecular interaction potentials that support many bound states. By rigorously accounting for this off-shell structure, the method captures both the short-range physics as well as multichannel couplings characteristic of alkali-metal potentials without resorting to model pseudopotentials. The central output is the complex three-body scattering hypervolume -- the three-body analogue of the two-body scattering length -- which we obtain with controlled and verifiable numerical accuracy. As a realistic benchmark, we apply our framework to spin-polarized potassium-39, performing full coupled-channels three-body scattering calculations and extracting the hypervolume over experimentally relevant conditions. The method is general and transferable to other atomic species and interaction models featuring deep molecular potentials with an arbitrarily large number of bound states.

</details>


### [79] [Observation of Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking in a Dephased Fermi Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16137)
*Si Wang,Thomas G. Kiely,Dorothee Tell,Johannes Obermeyer,Marnix Barendregt,Petar Bojović,Philipp M. Preiss,Abhijat Sarma,Titus Franz,Matthew P. A. Fisher,Cenke Xu,Immanuel Bloch*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 首次实验观测到混合量子态中的强-弱自发对称破缺（SW-SSB），该现象在退相干的单组分费米子系统中被量子气体显微镜成像捕获，揭示了开放量子系统中信息理论相变的对称性原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于对称性的量子物相分类是物理学中最基础的组织原则之一，但类似的框架尚未完全建立用于混合、退相干的量子态。强-弱自发对称破缺（SW-SSB）作为混合量子态中的尖锐相变，为理解开放量子系统中的信息理论相变提供了统一语言。

Method: 使用量子气体显微镜（quantum gas microscope）对退相干的单组分费米子物质进行成像。构建基于机器学习高斯参考态的量子-经典估计器，直接访问诊断SW-SSB的非线性Rényi-1和Rényi-2关联函数。通过添加可公度超晶格驱动费米子经历金属-绝缘体相变。

Result: 实验首次观测到SW-SSB，在退相干的费米液体中揭示了长程Rényi序。完全退相干后，金属-绝缘体相变表现为尖锐的SW-SSB相变。量子-经典估计器成功获取了非线性Rényi关联函数。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了开放量子系统中信息理论相变背后的对称性原理，将朗道（Landau）对称性范式扩展到了真实、退相干的量子器件领域。SW-SSB为理解退相干量子动力学中的经典流体力学涌现等现象提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Symmetry-based classification of quantum phases of matter is one of the most foundational organizing principles in physics; however, an analogous framework for mixed, decohered quantum states has only begun to emerge. A central new concept is strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SW-SSB), a sharp transition in mixed quantum states that is invisible to any observable linear in the density matrix and that has since been predicted across a broad class of open and monitored quantum systems. It also provides a unifying language for phenomena as disparate as the decodability of topological quantum memories and the emergence of classical hydrodynamics from decohered quantum dynamics. Here we report the first experimental observation of SW-SSB, in dephased single-component fermionic matter imaged by a quantum gas microscope. A quantum-classical estimator built on a machine-learned Gaussian reference state gives direct access to the nonlinear Rényi-1 and Rényi-2 correlators that diagnose SW-SSB, and reveals long-range Rényi order in the dephased Fermi liquid. Adding a commensurate superlattice drives the underlying fermions through a metal-to-insulator transition that, after full dephasing, manifests as a sharp SW-SSB phase transition. Our results uncover the symmetry principle behind information-theoretic transitions in open quantum systems, and extend Landau's symmetry paradigm into the regime of real, decohering quantum devices.

</details>


### [80] [Renormalised thermodynamics for Bose gases from low to critical temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16290)
*Michael H. Heinrich,Alexander Wowchik,Jürgen Berges*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过非微扰方法计算稀薄玻色气体的热力学性质，系统重整化自洽描述以超越传统高斯近似，确定从低温到高温的凝聚体耗尽及其相变临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高斯近似（如Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov理论）在描述稀薄玻色气体热力学性质时存在局限性，需要发展超越这些近似的系统重整化方法。

Method: 采用两粒子不可约（2PI）有效作用的非微扰近似，通过自洽展开的次领头阶方法系统重整化自洽描述，超越传统高斯近似。

Result: 确定了从低温到高温的凝聚体耗尽（condensate depletion）及其在相变点的临界行为，发现高斯近似下临界处的普适反常维度为零，而在场分量数自洽展开的次领头阶得到非零值。

Conclusion: 通过两粒子不可约有效作用的非微扰近似和系统重整化方法，成功超越了传统高斯近似，获得了稀薄玻色气体更精确的热力学描述，特别是在临界行为方面取得了改进。

Abstract: We compute thermodynamic properties of dilute Bose gases using non-perturbative approximations of the two-particle irreducible (2PI) effective action. It is shown how to systematically renormalise the self-consistent descriptions beyond conventional Gaussian approximations such as Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov theory. This allows us to determine the condensate depletion from low to high temperatures, including its critical behaviour at the phase transition. While the universal anomalous dimension at criticality is vanishing for Gaussian approximations, we determine its non-zero value at next-to-leading order of a self-consistent expansion in the number of field components.

### [81] [$D$-bialgebras, dendrification and embeddings into AWB of almost Poisson algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15346)
*Sami Mabrouk*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了代数与括号代数（AWB）及其与几乎泊松代数的关系，引入了几乎泊松Drinfel'd双代数概念，并建立了匹配对、Manin三元组与几乎泊松D-双代数之间的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代数与括号代数（algebra with bracket, AWB）作为结合代数配备满足Leibniz型相容条件的双线性括号，是非交换的几乎泊松代数的推广。研究AWB与几乎泊松代数的关系，以及建立相应的双代数理论，是本文的主要动机。

Method: 引入几乎泊松Drinfel'd双代数（almost Poisson D-bialgebras）作为泊松D-双代数的类比，并建立匹配对（matched pairs）、Manin三元组（Manin triples）与几乎泊松D-双代数之间的等价关系。此外，定义了几乎三叉泊松代数（almost tridendriform Poisson algebras）这一新代数结构。

Result: 证明了几乎泊松代数可以通过平均算子（averaging operators）嵌入到代数与括号代数中，更一般地，可以通过相对于给定表示的相对平均算子实现嵌入。同时，几乎三叉泊松代数被证明是与几乎泊松代数上的相对Rota-Baxter算子相关的基础代数结构。

Conclusion: 代数与括号代数提供了研究几乎泊松代数的新框架，通过建立双代数理论、嵌入定理以及新代数结构的定义，深化了对这些代数结构之间关系的理解，为非交换几何和数学物理中的相关结构提供了理论支持。

Abstract: An algebra with bracket ({\sf AWB} for short) is an associative algebra endowed with a bilinear bracket satisfying a Leibniz-type compatibility condition, as introduced in \cite{casas}. It can be viewed as a noncommutative generalization of an almost Poisson algebra; indeed, when the associative product is commutative and the bracket is skew-symmetric, one recovers the notion of an almost Poisson algebra. In this paper, we introduce the notion of {almost Poisson Drinfel'd bialgebras ($D$-bialgebras)} as an analogue of Poisson $D$-bialgebras, and we establish the equivalence between matched pairs, Manin triples, and almost Poisson $D$-bialgebras. Furthermore, we define a new algebraic structure, called {almost tridendriform Poisson algebras}, which can be regarded as the underlying algebraic structures associated with relative Rota-Baxter operators on almost Poisson algebras. Finally, we show that every almost Poisson algebra can be embedded into an algebra with bracket ({\sf AWB}) via averaging operators, and more generally via relative averaging operators associated to a given representation of the almost Poisson algebra.

</details>

### [82] [Control of turn-to-turn contact resistivity in resistively insulated REBCO coils](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15587)
*Jun Lu,Kwangmin Kim,Iain Dixon,Justin Deterding,Emsley Marks,Brent Jarvis,Denis Markiewicz,Hongyu Bai,Mark Bird*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究针对电阻绝缘（RI）REBCO磁体中的匝间接触电阻（Rc）压力循环敏感性问题，提出了多种缓解方法，包括添加导电填料、PbSn焊料涂层和不锈钢带氧化处理，成功将Rc控制在预设值并实现压力循环稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电阻绝缘（resistively insulated, RI）REBCO磁体虽然具有快速励磁、低损耗等优势，但其性能关键取决于匝间接触电阻（turn-to-turn contact resistivity, Rc）的精确控制。先前研究发现不锈钢夹层REBCO带材的Rc在压力循环下会急剧下降，这阻碍了不锈钢共绕RI磁体的设计。

Method: 研究提出了三种缓解Rc压力循环敏感性的方法：添加导电填料（如导电浆料或环氧树脂）；在REBCO带上涂覆2-3微米PbSn焊料；通过空气中不同温度加热氧化不锈钢共绕带材。这些方法通过短样测试和6双饼测试线圈进行验证。

Result: 短样测试显示，Rc成功控制在预设值1000和5000微欧-平方厘米，且在4.2K温度下对高达30,000次接触压力循环不敏感。6双饼测试线圈的Rc值与短样结果相当，证明了新方法在大尺寸线圈中的适用性。

Conclusion: 本研究开发的新方法有效缓解了RI REBCO磁体中Rc的压力循环敏感性，实现了Rc的精确控制和长期稳定性，为不锈钢共绕RI磁体的可靠设计提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Resistively insulated (RI) REBCO magnets feature short ramp times and low ramp losses while maintaining the advantages of no-insulation coils with high engineering current density and tolerance for defects in the REBCO conductor. Control of the turn-to-turn contact resistivity Rc is key to RI technology. Rc must be sufficiently high to prevent a large transient current, which could result in high mechanical stress during magnet quenches. Meanwhile it must be lower than the quench propagation limit to avoid conductor burn-out during a quench. Therefore, it is critical to control Rc within a suitable range of values which is usually coil specific. Previously, we discovered that Rc between two REBCO tapes with a stainless steel interlayer decreases dramatically with contact pressure cycling by up to three orders of magnitude. This drastic change made it impossible to design a suitable Rc value for a stainless steel co-wound RI magnet. In this work, we first present methods for mitigating Rc pressure cycling sensitivity. We found that by adding conductive fillers, such as conductive paste or epoxy, the Rc load cycling sensitivity is largely mitigated. For dry-wound coils, Rc load cycling sensitivity is mitigated by coating REBCO tape with a layer of 2- 3 um of PbSn solder. In addition, Rc can be controlled by oxidizing the stainless steel co-wind tape by heating stainless steel tapes at different temperatures in air. Using above methods, short sample tests showed that Rc was controlled to prescribed values of 1000 and 5000 uOhm-cm2 and was not sensitive to contact pressure cycling up to 30,000 cycles at 4.2 K. The new Rc control method was applied to a 6 double-pancake test coil which was tested at 4.2 K. The Rc in this test coil was comparable with the short sample results. This demonstrated the ability of this new method to control Rc in large coils.

</details>


### [83] [Charge Density Wave Driven Topological Phase Transition in Vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15976)
*Zhenhua Zhu,Ziqiang Wang,Dong E. Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个理论框架，表明条纹电荷密度波（stripe CDW）的相位可以在拓扑和非拓扑区域之间切换磁涡旋（magnetic vortex）的拓扑性质，并提出了两种可能的机制来实现这种相位控制的切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDWs）与超导性（superconductivity）之间的相互作用是量子材料（quantum materials）的核心主题，但CDW相位纹理如何调控涡旋拓扑（vortex topology）仍不清楚。该研究旨在理解CDW相位如何作为局部调控涡旋拓扑的手段。

Method: 研究开发了一个理论框架，提出了两种候选机制：直接调制（direct-modulation）场景和反演对称性破缺（inversion-symmetry-breaking, ISB）场景。前者通过CDW作为周期性势能（periodic potential）局部重整化（renormalizes）能带参数；后者通过CDW节点固定在涡旋中心破坏局部反演对称性。

Result: 直接调制场景通常无法在没有精细调节（fine tuning）的情况下重现对称的节点/反节点趋势。相比之下，ISB场景允许自旋三重态配对（spin-triplet pairing）的混合，当该成分占主导时产生稳健的拓扑转变（topological transition）。

Conclusion: CDW相位可以作为调控和测试涡旋拓扑的局部手段，特别是在反演对称性破缺场景下，CDW节点固定在涡旋中心能够实现稳健的拓扑转变。

Abstract: The interplay between charge density waves (CDWs) and superconductivity is a central theme in quantum materials, yet how CDW phase textures govern vortex topology remains poorly understood. We develop a theoretical framework showing that the phase of a stripe CDW can switch a magnetic vortex between topological and trivial regimes. Motivated by recent experiments, we propose two candidate mechanisms enabling phase-controlled switching of vortex topology. In a direct-modulation scenario, the CDW acts as a periodic potential that locally renormalizes band parameters and can induce topological transitions, but it generally cannot reproduce the symmetric node/antinode trend without fine tuning. In contrast, in an inversion-symmetry-breaking (ISB) scenario, a CDW node pinned to the vortex center breaks local inversion and allows for the mixture of spin-triplet pairing of Cooper pairs, producing a robust topological transition when this component dominates. Our results suggests CDW phase as a possible local handle to tune and test vortex topology.

</details>

### [84] [The Phase Transitions in a $p$ spin Glass Model: A Numerical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15433)
*Prerak Gupta,Auditya Sharma,Bharadwaj Vedula,J. Yeo,M. A. Moore*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了平衡的M=4、p=4自旋玻璃模型，作为有限维短程p自旋玻璃模型的一维长程代理，以探究超越平均场理论的玻璃转变本质。通过大规模蒙特卡洛平衡模拟，发现尽管某些参数下平均场理论预测一级复本对称破缺（1RSB）转变，但实际观测到向完全复本对称破缺（FRSB）相的直接连续转变，且三维对应系统中可能不存在相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究超越平均场理论的玻璃转变本质，通过一维长程代理模型来研究有限维短程p自旋玻璃模型。特别关注复本对称破缺（replica symmetry breaking）机制在非平均场情况下的变化，以及三维系统中可能存在的相变行为。

Method: 采用大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）平衡模拟方法，研究完全连接和幂律稀释（power-law diluted）版本的模型。通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling, FSS）分析自旋玻璃磁化率来提取临界温度，并分析自旋重叠分布（spin-overlap distribution）和λ参数值。

Result: 对于长程指数σ=0、0.25和0.55，从自旋玻璃磁化率的有限尺寸标度分析得到的临界温度与理论预测一致。然而，自旋重叠分布和λ参数值并未提供一级复本对称破缺（1RSB）相变的数值证据，而是显示从顺磁态向完全复本对称破缺（FRSB）相的直接转变，重整化后的λ≡ω₂/ω₁<1表明连续FRSB转变。对于σ=0.85（大致对应三维系统），重整化λ值同样小于1，未发现1RSB或连续FRSB转变的迹象。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，强有限尺寸效应和紧密间隔的转变温度消除了在可研究系统尺寸下预期的1RSB转变。三维系统中λ<1且无相变迹象，表明三维结构玻璃的Kauzmann温度T_K可能为零，完全不存在相变。这一发现挑战了平均场理论对玻璃转变的预测。

Abstract: We investigate the balanced $M=4$, $p=4$ spin-glass model for a one-dimensional long-range proxy for the finite dimensional short-range $p$-spin glass model to examine the nature of the glass transition beyond mean-field theory. We perform large-scale Monte Carlo equilibrated simulations for both fully connected and power-law diluted versions of the model. The critical temperatures extracted from the finite-size scaling (FSS) analysis of spin-glass susceptibility are in good agreement with theoretical predictions for $σ= 0, 0.25$, and 0.55. For these values of the long-range exponent $σ$ (which is the power of the decrease of the interactions between the spins with their separation), one might have expected that mean-field theory would provide a good description of the system. However, the spin-overlap distribution and the value of the $λ$-parameter do not provide numerical evidence for a one-step replica symmetry breaking (1RSB) phase transition. Instead, our results indicate a direct transition from the paramagnetic state to a full replica symmetry broken phase, with a renormalized value of $λ\equiv ω_2/ω_1 < 1$ suggesting a continuous FRSB transition, despite this ratio being equal to 2 at mean-field level. A value of $λ> 1$ is required for the discontinuous 1RSB transition. We argue that strong finite-size effects and closely spaced transition temperatures remove the expected 1RSB transition for the system sizes which we can study. For values of the exponent $σ= 0.85$, which roughly corresponds to a three dimensional system, we find that the renormalized value of $λ$ is again less than 1, with no signs of either the 1RSB transition or the continuous FRSB transition, suggesting that the Kauzmann temperature $T_K$ in three dimensions might be zero and the complete absence of phase transitions in structural glasses.

</details>

### [85] [Singlet-only always-on gapless exchange (SAGE) spin qubits: Charge noise effects and two-qubit gates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15419)
*Nathan L. Foulk,Katharina Laubscher,Silas Hoffman,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: SAGE（singlet-only always-on gapless exchange）自旋量子比特是一种新型交换式量子比特，通过四电子单重态编码实现磁梯度误差免疫，但始终开启的交换耦合使其对电荷噪声敏感。本文分析了SAGE量子比特在1/f电荷噪声下的性能，并提出脉冲序列和重聚焦策略来提升相干时间和门保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交换式（exchange-only, EO）量子比特易受局部磁场梯度影响，而SAGE量子比特通过单重态编码和始终开启的交换耦合实现了磁梯度误差免疫。然而，这种始终开启的操作模式增加了量子比特对电荷噪声的敏感性，需要系统研究其噪声性能并开发缓解策略。

Method: 从描述耦合量子点电子结构的Hubbard模型出发，分析了SAGE量子比特在1/f电荷噪声下的性能。该噪声同时引起点化学势和点间隧穿耦合的涨落。计算了SAGE空闲相干时间，并研究了类似CPMG的脉冲序列对相干时间的提升效果。

Result: 研究表明，对于实验相关的电荷噪声强度，现实的CPMG-like脉冲序列能显著延长SAGE单量子比特相干时间。同时分析了电荷和磁噪声下SAGE双量子比特门的保真度，提出了简单的重聚焦策略来缓解噪声影响，并通过增加纠缠脉冲的斜坡时间来抑制向非计算态的泄漏。

Conclusion: SAGE量子比特在磁梯度误差免疫方面具有优势，但需要应对电荷噪声的挑战。通过优化的脉冲序列和重聚焦策略，可以有效提升其相干时间和门操作保真度，为实验实现提供了可行的噪声缓解方案。

Abstract: Singlet-only always-on gapless exchange (SAGE) spin qubits are an alternative type of exchange-only (EO) qubits that encode a single qubit in the spins of four electrons located in four tunnel-coupled quantum dots. While conventional EO qubits are susceptible to local magnetic field gradients caused by local nuclear environments and $g$-factor variations, the SAGE qubit subspace is inherently protected from magnetic-gradient-induced Pauli errors by virtue of the singlet-only encoding, which is invariant under magnetic field gradients, and the always-on exchange couplings, which provide energetic leakage protection. However, the always-on operation simultaneously increases the qubit's sensitivity to charge noise. Here, starting from a Hubbard model describing the underlying electronic structure of the coupled quantum dots, we characterize the performance of SAGE qubits in the presence of $1/f$ charge noise that induces fluctuations in both the dot chemical potentials and the interdot tunnel couplings. We calculate SAGE idle coherence times and show that realistic CPMG-like pulse sequences can be used to significantly extend SAGE single-qubit coherence times for experimentally relevant charge noise strengths. We likewise study the fidelity of SAGE two-qubit gates in the presence of charge and magnetic noise and again propose a simple refocusing strategy to mitigate the noise, while increased ramp times of the entangling pulse suppress leakage into noncomputational states.

</details>

Method: 通过在mumax+中新增d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnets）磁体类别，扩展了原有的反铁磁模拟代码库。利用该软件包模拟了布洛赫畴壁（Bloch domain wall）的线剖面，并研究了磁振子色散关系（magnon dispersion relation）对交换相互作用各向异性的依赖关系。

Conclusion: mumax+软件包通过新增交变磁体模拟功能，能够准确模拟多亚晶格磁性系统的磁学行为，其面向对象设计在静磁场计算方面优于其他微磁模拟器，为交变磁体研究提供了有效的计算工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we demonstrate how altermagnets can be simulated in the recently released micromagnetic simulation package mumax+. We have added a new magnet class for d-wave altermagnets and demonstrate how mumax+ is able to reproduce the analytical solutions for line profiles of the Néel vector and net magnetization for a Bloch domain wall. Next, we show simulation results of the magnon dispersion relation and its dependence on the anisotropic nature of the exchange interaction. Finally, we study the motion of a Néel skyrmion by applying a spin transfer torque. This new feature was implemented by extending the pre-existing code base for antiferromagnetic simulations. The object-oriented design of mumax+ allows for a correct calculation of the magnetostatic field in multi-sublattice systems, a feature that many other micromagnetic simulators lack.

### [87] [Current-Induced Dynamics and Instability Pathways of Skyrmioniums in Chiral Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15692)
*Kaito Nakamura,Yuka Kotorii,Andrey O. Leonov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了手性磁性薄膜中斯格明子泡（skyrmionium）在电流驱动下的动力学行为、结构转变及不稳定性，揭示了其零总拓扑电荷下的有限横向速度机制，并探索了基于斯格明子泡的元物质（meta-matter）集体动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明斯格明子泡（skyrmionium）这一具有零总拓扑电荷的磁性拓扑结构在电流驱动下的非平衡响应机制，特别是其内部结构如何影响动力学行为，并探索基于斯格明子泡的元物质系统的集体动力学特性。

Method: 采用微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）与基于广义蒂勒方程（generalized Thiele equation）的解析描述相结合的方法，分析孤立斯格明子泡和集体态（skyrmionium-based meta-matter）的电流驱动行为，并通过拓扑电荷和局部旋转度量的演化解析微观路径。

Result: 研究发现斯格明子泡在零总拓扑电荷下仍表现出有限横向速度，即斯格明子泡霍尔效应（skyrmionium Hall effect），源于内部斯格明子与外围环的正负拓扑贡献面积不平衡。电流诱导形变进一步增强该不平衡，产生与斯格明子相当的霍尔角。高电流密度下，斯格明子泡根据磁场和单轴各向异性发生不同不稳定性转变，包括伸长、坍缩为斯格明子、转变为拓扑平凡液滴（topologically trivial droplet）及扩展为条纹织构（stripe textures）。混合斯格明子-斯格明子泡晶格展现出丰富的集体动力学行为，包括弹性输运、多态转变、孤子交换和条纹形成。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了斯格明子泡及其元物质作为可调谐非平衡系统，能够探测远离平衡态的拓扑能量景观（topological energy landscape），为拓扑磁性结构的非平衡动力学研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of current-driven dynamics, transformations, and instabilities of skyrmioniums in chiral magnetic films, considering both isolated objects and collective states forming skyrmionium-based meta-matter. Using micromagnetic simulations combined with an analytical description based on the generalized Thiele equation, we clarify how the internal structure of skyrmioniums governs their nonequilibrium response to electric currents. Despite having zero total topological charge, skyrmioniums exhibit a finite transverse velocity under applied currents. We show that this skyrmionium Hall effect originates from an imbalance between positive and negative topological contributions of the inner skyrmion and surrounding ring, which typically occupy different areas. Current-induced deformations further enhance this imbalance, yielding Hall angles comparable to those of skyrmions. At higher current densities, skyrmioniums undergo distinct instabilities depending on magnetic field and uniaxial anisotropy, including elongation, collapse into a skyrmion, transformation into a topologically trivial droplet, and expansion into stripe textures. We map these regimes in current--field and current--anisotropy phase diagrams and resolve their microscopic pathways via the evolution of topological charge and local rotational measures. Beyond isolated textures, mixed skyrmion--skyrmionium lattices display rich collective dynamics, including elastic transport, polymorphic transitions, soliton exchange, and stripe formation. Pulsed currents provide additional control, enabling access to regimes beyond continuous driving. Our results establish skyrmioniums and their meta-matter as tunable nonequilibrium systems probing the topological energy landscape far from equilibrium.

Abstract: GaAs quantum dots grown by droplet etching epitaxy are high-quality solid-state sources of quantum light. This review presents a detailed overview of the droplet etching epitaxy growth technique in the molecular beam epitaxy environment, with emphasis on the growth parameters necessary to realize high-quality quantum dots. We systematically cover the three main phases of droplet etching epitaxy - droplet deposition, droplet etching, and nanohole regrowth - and relate experimental results to theories on crystal growth. ### [89] [Amplitudes of Hall field-induced resistance oscillations with a two-harmonic density of states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15700)
*Miguel Tierz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立霍尔场诱导电阻振荡（Hall field-induced resistance oscillations, HIRO）在强场极限下的精确理论框架，以提供从实验数据中提取关键散射时间参数的可靠方法。

Method: 基于Vavilov-Aleiner-Glazman动力学框架，首先推导单谐波态密度下的强场渐近行为，然后扩展到双谐波态密度，获得了非对角混合核γ₁₂的精确单积分表示。

Result: 对于单谐波态密度，主导振荡幅度由完全背散射率1/τ(π)决定；对于双谐波态密度，奇次谐波（特别是m=1和m=3）的系数由1/τ(0)和1/τ(π)的组合决定，而主导的m=2幅度保持不变。

Conclusion: 建立的提取协议能够在传输弛豫时间τ_tr和内部弛豫时间τ_in固定的情况下，以亚百分之一的精度恢复量子弛豫时间τ_q、背散射时间τ(π)，并在解析m=1,3谐波时恢复τ(0)，后者为无序描述提供了一致性检验。

Abstract: We derive explicit strong-field asymptotics for the normalized differential resistance in Hall field-induced resistance oscillations (HIRO) within the Vavilov-Aleiner-Glazman kinetic framework. For a single-harmonic density of states, the leading oscillation amplitude is set by the full backscattering rate $1/τ(π)$. Extending the theory to a two-harmonic density of states, we show that the off-diagonal mixed kernel $γ_{12}$ admits an exact single-integral representation, from which the strong-field asymptotics follow directly. The resulting odd harmonics, notably $m=1$ and $m=3$, have coefficients determined by combinations of $1/τ(0)$ and $1/τ(π)$, while the leading $m=2$ amplitude remains unchanged. On exact-kernel mock data generated and fit within the same model, with $τ_{\rm tr}$ and $τ_{\rm in}$ held fixed, the resulting extraction protocol recovers $τ_q$, $τ(π)$, and -- when the $m=1,3$ harmonics are resolved -- $τ(0)$ to sub-percent accuracy, with $τ(0)$ providing a consistency check on the disorder description.

### [90] [Persistence of large and gate-tunable anisotropic magnetoresistance in an atomically thin antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15793)

Here, we demonstrate electrical readout of the Néel vector down to 1.3 nm (two layers) in the two-dimensional van der Waals (vdW) AFM semiconductor NiPS3. We achieve full gate control over these contributions, enabling tunability of both the magnitude and sign of magnetoresistance.
