### [91] [Observation of ring states in a delicate topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15983)
*Caroline Tornow,Julia Rupprecht,Pascal Engeler,Ute Drechsler,Kukka-Emilia Huhtinen,Chiara Devescovi,Sebastian D. Huber*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入强局域杂质作为光谱探针，在声子超材料中实现了对脆弱拓扑绝缘体的探测，观察到拓扑指标——环态（ring states），并发现这些环态即使在多胞性被移除后仍然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脆弱拓扑（delicate topology）作为一种新型能带拓扑，其定义特性——多胞性（multicellularity）可以通过在能谱中任何位置引入局域轨道耦合而被移除，这使得传统仅探测低能自由度的探针难以诊断脆弱拓扑。

Method: 研究引入强局域杂质（strong local impurities）作为光谱探针，在声子超材料（phononic metamaterial）中实现脆弱拓扑绝缘体。通过调节杂质强度并进行轨道分辨读取（orbital-resolved readout），观察拓扑指标——环态。

Result: 观察到环态（ring states）——带隙内束缚态，其频率在强杂质极限下保持固定，而其实空间分布围绕杂质位点形成明显的环状结构。这些环态即使在通过弱杂化额外轨道移除系统的多胞性后仍然持续存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了杂质诱导环态作为复杂多带物理（包括脆弱拓扑相）的探针，为探测传统方法难以诊断的拓扑特性提供了新途径。

Abstract: Topological insulators are typically characterized by particularly stable properties, such as global invariants, and can be identified by probing their robust surface states. A recently discovered novel form of band topology, delicate topology, challenges this paradigm: its defining property, multicellularity, can be removed by introducing a coupling to local orbitals anywhere in the spectrum, even far above the relevant band gap. This makes it hard to diagnose delicate topology with conventional probes that access only low-energy degrees of freedom. Here, we introduce strong local impurities as a spectroscopic probe of a delicate topological insulator which we realize in a phononic metamaterial. By tuning the impurity strength and performing orbital-resolved readout, we observe recently proposed indicators of topology: ring states, in-gap bound states whose frequencies remain pinned in the strong-impurity limit while their real-space profiles form a pronounced ring around the impurity site. We find that these ring states persist even when the multicellularity in our system is removed by a weakly hybridizing additional orbital. Our results establish impurity-induced ring states as probes of complex multiband physics, including delicate topological phases.

</details>


### [92] [Machine Learning and Deep Learning in Quantum Materials: Symmetry, Topology, and the Rise of Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15985)
*Mahyar Hassani-Vasmejani,Hosein Alavi-Rad,Meysam Bagheri Tagani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该综述分析了机器学习（ML）和深度学习（DL）如何克服传统第一性原理方法（如密度泛函理论DFT）的立方标度瓶颈，加速量子材料奇异相的发现，特别关注于自动识别拓扑相以及发现超越铁磁/反铁磁二分法的第三类磁性——交变磁体（Altermagnet）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝聚态物理领域正面临高通量第一性原理（ab initio）工作流和快速扩张的实验数据集带来的前所未有的数据激增。传统的密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）方法虽然具有基础性作用，但其立方标度（cubic scaling）特性在探索量子材料广阔化学空间时成为主要瓶颈。

Method: 综述分析了从刚性基于描述符（descriptor-based）的模型向灵活的、对称性感知（symmetry-aware）架构的转变，特别是尊重旋转和平移不变性的E(3)-等变图神经网络（E(3)-equivariant Graph Neural Networks, GNNs）。重点讨论了利用对称性指标（symmetry indicators）和基本能带表示（elementary band representations）来诊断非平凡拓扑性而无需昂贵能带结构积分的ML模型。

Result: 通过结合图论与晶体学对称性分析的专业化AI搜索引擎，发现了d波、g波甚至i波交变磁体（altermagnets），扩展了已知磁序的版图。这揭示了超越铁磁、反铁磁二分法的第三类磁性——交变磁体。

Conclusion: 综述最后讨论了可解释性差距（interpretability gap），并提倡使用符号回归（symbolic regression）和主动学习框架（active-learning frameworks）来连接黑盒预测与实验可验证的机制。

Abstract: The landscape of condensed matter physics is facing an unprecedented data surge driven by high-throughput ab initio workflows and rapidly expanding experimental datasets. Traditional first-principles methods such as Density Functional Theory (DFT), despite their foundational role, suffer from cubic scaling, creating a major bottleneck when exploring the vast chemical space of quantum materials. This review analyzes how Machine Learning (ML) and Deep Learning (DL) are overcoming these limitations and accelerating the discovery of exotic phases of matter. We examine the shift from rigid descriptor-based models to flexible, symmetry-aware architectures, particularly E(3)-equivariant Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) that respect rotational and translational invariance. A central focus is the automated identification of topological phases, where ML models exploit symmetry indicators and elementary band representations to diagnose non-trivial topology without costly band structure integrations.
  The discussion culminates in a case study of the Altermagnet, a recently identified third class of magnetism beyond the ferromagnetic, antiferromagnetic dichotomy. We highlight how specialized AI search engines, combining graph theory with crystallographic symmetry analysis, have uncovered d-wave, g-wave, and even i-wave altermagnets, expanding the known landscape of magnetic order. The review concludes by addressing the interpretability gap and advocates for symbolic regression and active-learning frameworks to connect black-box predictions with experimentally verifiable mechanisms.

</details>


### [93] [Disambiguating electrical detection of magnetization dynamics in magnetic insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15999)
*Hanchen Wang,William Legrand,Shangyuan Wang,Davit Petrosyan,Hiroki Matsumoto,Richard Schlitz,Ka Shen,Pietro Gambardella*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了区分磁性绝缘体中自旋泵浦（spin pumping）与自旋力矩铁磁共振（ST-FMR）贡献的分析框架，解决了两种效应产生相反符号电压信号导致的物理解释模糊问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在重金属/磁性绝缘体异质结构中，自旋泵浦和自旋力矩铁磁共振通常在不同测量构型中被分开处理，但实践中这两种效应的竞争会产生符号相反的电压信号，导致对基础物理的模糊解释。

Method: 研究系统性地在非局域和局域器件中，使用铂覆盖的铥铁石榴石和铋钇铁石榴石薄膜，研究了自旋泵浦和ST-FMR效应。通过分析自旋波特性、磁耗散、磁场取向和器件几何结构对信号符号和大小的影响。

Result: 研究发现微波激发产生的电压在面外或面内磁场构型之间会改变符号。成功区分了由指数衰减传播自旋波引起的自旋泵浦贡献，以及由感应耦合远程诱导的弱距离依赖性ST-FMR贡献。

Conclusion: 薄膜厚度上的自旋波激发剖面和磁阻尼（magnetic damping）在很大程度上决定了两种贡献中哪一种占主导，因此电信号的符号不能唯一地归属于磁振子模式的手性（chirality）。

Abstract: Electrical detection of magnetization dynamics in magnetic insulators underpins both fundamental studies of magnon transport and the development of low-loss magnonic devices. In heavy-metal/magnetic-insulator heterostructures, spin pumping and spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance (ST-FMR) are widely used for this purpose and are often treated separately in different measurement geometries. In practice, the competition between these two effects gives rise to electrical voltage signals of opposite signs, which can lead to ambiguous interpretations of the underlying physics. Here, we show how to disambiguate their respective contributions and provide a framework for interpreting experiments involving microwave excitation of magnetic insulators and detection of magnetization dynamics via spin-charge conversion in heavy metals. We systematically investigate spin pumping and ST-FMR in nonlocal and local devices using Pt-capped thin films of thulium and bismuth-yttrium iron garnets. We show how spin-wave character, magnetic dissipation, magnetic field orientation and device geometry govern the sign and magnitude of the resulting signals. In several cases, the voltage generated by microwave excitation changes sign between an out-of-plane or in-plane magnetic configuration. We disentangle a contribution due to spin pumping, induced by exponentially decaying propagating spin waves, and a weakly distance-dependent contribution from ST-FMR, remotely induced by inductive coupling. We show that both the spin wave excitation profile across the film thickness and magnetic damping largely determine which of the two contributions dominates. Hence, the sign of the electrical signal cannot be uniquely assigned to the chirality of the magnon modes.

</details>


### [94] [Hopping-Mediated Charge Transport in Graphene Beyond the Ballistic Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16152)
*J. P. Dadario Pereira,Raphael Tromer,Luiz A. Ribeiro Junior,Douglas S. Galvao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轨迹解析框架，用于研究石墨烯及相关二维碳系统的电荷输运，超越了理想弹道和完全相干极限。该方法通过预设原子晶格上的动力学蒙特卡洛跳跃描述输运，能够同时处理无序、热激活和外场效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常局限于理想弹道或完全相干输运极限，缺乏能够统一处理无序、热激活和外场效应的计算框架。本文旨在开发一种轨迹解析方法，以更真实地描述石墨烯及相关二维碳材料的电荷输运行为。

Method: 采用动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）跳跃方法，在预设原子晶格上模拟载流子轨迹。该方法能够直接从随机载流子轨迹中提取电流和有效透射率，无需引入唯象输运系数。

Result: 本征石墨烯表现出近似欧姆响应，电流约7-8 μA，有效透射率接近0.98-1.00，电导率约为(5.8-7.8)×10⁻⁵ S（0.10 V下）。空位缺陷强烈抑制输运，10%空位浓度下透射率降至约0.45-0.75。高温加速跳跃并部分恢复输运，但无法克服严重连接性损失。磁场进一步降低输运，尤其在无序网络中更为显著。

Conclusion: 该框架为真实二维碳材料提供了统一的计算方案，能够同时从载流子位移和渡越时间中提取扩散系数和有效迁移率。该方法超越了传统理想化输运模型，为研究复杂条件下的电荷输运行为提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We present a trajectory-resolved framework for charge transport in graphene and related two-dimensional carbon systems beyond the ideal ballistic and fully coherent limits. Transport is described by kinetic Monte Carlo hopping on a predefined atomic lattice, allowing the combined treatment of disorder, thermal activation, and external fields. Current and effective transmittance are extracted directly from stochastic carrier trajectories, without phenomenological transport coefficients.
  We apply the method to graphene under bias voltage (0-0.10 V), temperature (300-900 K), magnetic field (0-10 T), in-plane strain (2-10%, uniaxial and biaxial), and vacancy concentration (0-10%). Pristine graphene shows an almost ohmic response, with currents of about 7-8 uA, effective transmittance near 0.98-1.00, and conductance of about (5.8-7.8) x 10^-5 S at 0.10 V, depending on direction. Vacancies strongly suppress transport, reducing transmittance to about 0.45-0.75 at 10% vacancy. Higher temperature accelerates hopping and partly restores transport, but cannot overcome severe connectivity loss. Magnetic fields further reduce transport, especially in disordered networks. The framework provides a unified computational scheme for realistic two-dimensional carbon materials and also yields diffusion coefficients and effective mobilities from carrier displacements and transit times.

</details>

Method: 研究系统设计和比较了四种电流-电压（I-V）放大器架构：单级线性（single-stage linear）、串联线性（series-linear）、对数（logarithmic）和多级级联（multi-stage cascaded），专门针对断裂结技术（break junction techniques）优化，包括扫描隧道显微镜断裂结（STM-BJ）和机械可控断裂结（MCBJ）。

Abstract: Accurate electrical amplification is essential in molecular electronics for measuring conductance through atomic and molecular junctions, where currents often span several orders of magnitude. In this work, we present a systematic design and comparative analysis of four current-to-voltage ($I\text{--}V$) amplifier architectures: single-stage linear, series-linear, logarithmic, and multi-stage cascaded, specifically optimized for break junction (BJ) techniques, including scanning tunneling microscopy (STM-BJ) and mechanically controllable break junctions (MCBJ). Each configuration is evaluated based on sensitivity, noise performance, and dynamic range. Our results characterize the trade-offs between circuit complexity and noise, providing a robust framework and practical guidelines for selecting amplification schemes in quantum transport experiments.

### [96] [PySCo-EFT and ECOSMOG-EFT: a tandem of N-body simulation codes for the Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15434)
*Himanish Ganjoo,Yann Rasera,Emilio Bellini,Michel-Andrès Breton,Fabien Castillo,Sandrine Codis,Stephane Colombi,Pier-Stefano Corasaniti,Giulia Cusin,Yohan Dubois,Sylvain de la Torre,Eric Jullo,Guilhem Lavaux,Amandine Le Brun,Sebastian Peirani,Sandrine Pires,Vincent Reverdy,Iñigo Sáez-Casares,Shohei Saga,Atsushi Taruya,Wangzheng Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了两种用于暗能量有效场论（EFTofDE）宇宙学的新型N体模拟代码：基于Python的粒子网格代码PySCo-EFT和基于RAMSES的自适应网格细化代码ECOSMOG-EFT，用于研究修正引力理论对非线性尺度物质分布的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 修正引力理论（modified gravity theories）是解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀现象的标准宇宙学模型替代方案。暗能量有效场论（Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy, EFTofDE）框架能以有限参数描述广泛的此类理论，但需要高分辨率N体模拟来获得非线性尺度的精确预测，以约束未来大规模结构巡天的观测数据。

Method: 开发了两种N体模拟代码：PySCo-EFT（Python-based particle mesh code）和ECOSMOG-EFT（RAMSES-based code with adaptive mesh refinement）。考虑具有光速引力波速度的Horndeski模型，使用迭代求解器和多重网格方案求解额外标量场方程，并纳入非线性Vainshtein屏蔽机制（Vainshtein screening mechanism）。

Result: 代码验证显示：大尺度上与线性理论的一致性优于0.5%，两个代码在非线性尺度上具有相似的一致性。物质功率谱提升的主要数值效应包括质量分辨率、有限体积效应、细化阈值和起始红移，但在最大波数（k=10 h/Mpc）处限制在2%以下。研究了EFTofDE参数对物质功率谱比值的影响，发现屏蔽机制相对于线性化场方程的作用可忽略或主导。

Conclusion: 开发的代码为生成EFTofDE对物质成团影响的快速准确预测提供了工具，能够纳入非线性屏蔽效应，有助于约束修正引力理论参数。

Abstract: Modified gravity theories constitute viable alternatives to the standard cosmological model for explaining the observed late-time accelerated expansion of the Universe. The Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy (EFTofDE) is an efficient framework to describe a wide range of such theories with a limited number of parameters. To robustly constrain them by comparison with clustering and weak lensing data from upcoming large-scale structure surveys, high-resolution cosmological N-body simulations are required to obtain accurate predictions for the matter distribution on non-linear scales. We introduce two new N-body simulation codes for EFTofDE cosmologies: PySCo-EFT, a Python-based particle mesh code, and ECOSMOG-EFT, a RAMSES-based code with adaptive mesh refinement. We consider Horndeski models with a luminal gravitational wave speed. We use iterative solvers and multigrid schemes to solve for the additional scalar field equation in both codes, incorporating the non-linear Vainshtein screening mechanism. We present validation and convergence tests of the codes. We obtain a sub-0.5 percent agreement with linear theory on large scales and a similar agreement between the two codes on non-linear scales. The dominant numerical effects on the matter-power-spectrum boost are mass resolution, finite-volume effects, refinement threshold, and starting redshift, but they are limited to below 2% at the largest wavenumbers (k=10 h/Mpc) for the range of tested values. We investigate the impact of the EFTofDE parameters on the matter-power-spectrum ratios between EFTofDE and $Λ$CDM cases. Depending on the EFTofDE parameters, the screening plays a negligible or dominant role compared to the linearised field equations. Our codes provide tools for generating fast and accurate predictions of the impact of the EFTofDE on the clustering of matter, incorporating non-linear screening.

*Joao R. L. Santos,Guillem Domènech,Amilcar R. Queiroz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速射电暴（Fast Radio Bursts, FRBs）是射电天文学中引人注目的现象，其探测数量正迅速增加。通过探测或未探测到引力透镜化的FRB事件，可以探测原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）作为暗物质组分的可能性，这为研究宇宙中的PBHs提供了独立且互补的探测手段。

Method: 研究评估了三个即将投入使用的射电望远镜：LOFAR2.0、FAST Core Array和BINGO，通过分析它们探测引力透镜化FRB事件的能力，来测试PBH作为暗物质组分的假设。

Abstract: Fast Radio Bursts (FRBs) are among the most intriguing phenomena observed in radio astronomy. So far, about 130 FRB signals have been confirmed and characterized by different surveys, and the CHIME telescope has recently reported a new catalog of 4539 bursts. Therefore, these numbers are expected to increase in the coming years. The detection, or lack thereof, of lensed FRB events can be used to probe Primordial Black Holes (PBHs) as a fraction of dark matter. We investigate the potential of three upcoming radio telescopes, LOFAR2.0, FAST Core Array, and BINGO, to test the PBH scenario. We forecast that LOFAR2.0 will constrain $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} < 0.16$ for PBH masses $M_{\rm PBH}>1\,{M_{\odot}}$, while FAST Core Array and BINGO will restrict $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} < 0.39$ for $M_{\rm PBH}>10\,{M_{\odot}}$ and $M_{\rm PBH}>10^{-2}\,{M_{\odot}}$, respectively. Despite the existence of stricter constraints, FRB lensing offers an independent and complementary probe of PBHs in the Universe, which will improve in the future.

### [98] [GRMHD accretion beyond the black hole paradigm: Light from within the shadow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15430)
*Saurabh,Maciek Wielgus,Parth Bambhaniya,Elisabete M. de Gouveia Dal Pino,Andrei P. Lobanov,Pankaj S. Joshi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文首次进行了三维广义相对论磁流体动力学模拟，研究物质持续吸积到无视界奇点（JMN-1时空）的过程。研究发现系统演化成持续的磁滞吸积盘状态，吸积率与黑洞模型估计一致，并识别出黑洞与JMN-1的关键观测区别：JMN-1的"可观测"阴影内部存在可探测的亮度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究物质持续吸积到无视界奇点（horizonless singularity）的过程，特别是JMN-1时空作为黑洞模拟体（black hole mimicker）的情况。研究动机包括检验这类奇点天体是否能够支持持续吸积，并与黑洞模型的预测进行比较。

Method: 采用三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic）模拟，研究JMN-1时空中的吸积过程。JMN-1时空源于广义相对论中具有各向异性压力的引力坍缩。使用偏振广义相对论辐射传输（polarized general relativistic radiative transfer）计算230 GHz的合成射线追踪图像。

Result: 系统演化成持续的磁滞吸积盘（magnetically arrested disk）状态。对于M87*低光度活动星系核的参数，获得吸积率约为(3.0±0.5)×10⁻⁶ Ṁ_Edd，与黑洞模型估计完全一致。合成图像与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）观测基本相符，但识别出关键区别：JMN-1的"可观测"阴影内部存在可探测亮度。

Conclusion: JMN-1时空能够支持持续吸积，其吸积率与黑洞模型相当。虽然当前观测无法区分，但JMN-1阴影内部的亮度特征为下一代射电干涉仪提供了检验黑洞范式的可靠测试方法。这一特征源于靠近中心奇点的区域，在黑洞时空中会被事件视界隐藏。

Abstract: We present the first three-dimensional general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic simulation of sustained accretion onto a horizonless singularity in which matter reaches the central object rather than being accumulated outside of it or expelled in outflows. We consider a Joshi-Malafarina-Narayan (JMN-1) spacetime, a well-motivated black hole mimicker that arises from gravitational collapse with anisotropic pressure in general relativity, and adopt a compactness parameter for which the central singularity is null. We find that the system evolves into a sustained magnetically arrested disk state. For parameters appropriate to the low-luminosity active galactic nucleus M87*, we obtain an accretion rate of $\sim(3.0 \pm 0.5)\times 10^{-6} \dot{M}_{\rm Edd}$, in full agreement with estimates based on black hole models and, in particular, comparable to that of our reference Schwarzschild black hole simulation. Synthetic ray-traced images at $230\,{\rm GHz}$, computed using polarized general relativistic radiative transfer, are broadly consistent with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87*. We identify a key observational discriminant between a black hole and JMN-1: the presence of detectable brightness inside of the ``observable" shadow of JMN-1. This emission originates very close to the central singularity, in a region that would be hidden behind the event horizon in a black hole spacetime. Although this signature is beyond the reach of current observations, it falls within the projected imaging dynamic range of next-generation radio interferometric instruments, offering a robust test of the black hole paradigm.

</details>


### [99] [Circular polarization images of Sgr A* for different magnetic field geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15673)
*Hao Yin,Songbai Chen,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过克尔时空中的半解析辐射无效吸积流模型，系统分析了Sgr A*在230 GHz的持续负圆偏振现象，探讨了六种极向磁场构型对圆偏振产生的影响，并基于ALMA观测数据对Sgr A*的磁场几何结构施加了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sgr A*在230 GHz表现出持续的负圆偏振（circular polarization），这为探测其吸积流中的磁场几何结构提供了有力工具。研究旨在通过系统分析不同磁场构型下的圆偏振特性，理解Sgr A*的磁场几何并解释观测现象。

Method: 采用克尔时空（Kerr spacetime）中的稳态半解析辐射无效吸积流模型（RIAF model），结合偏振辐射转移（polarized radiative transfer）方法。系统分析了六种极向磁场构型（poloidal magnetic field configurations）在不同黑洞自旋、倾角和磁场极性下的圆偏振图像。

Result: 研究发现径向、抛物线、四极子和组合磁场构型中的圆偏振主要由法拉第转换（Faraday conversion）主导，而偶极子和垂直磁场中则由本征发射（intrinsic emission）主导。径向和抛物线构型产生极性不变的净圆偏振，而偶极子和垂直磁场产生极性敏感的圆偏振。当吸积盘相对于黑洞自旋为顺行时，所有六种磁场构型的圆偏振产生在高自旋情况下均较低，逆行情况则更复杂。此外，除四极子构型外，边缘观测视角的净圆偏振V_net ≈ 0。

Conclusion: 通过与ALMA观测数据比较，研究排除了高倾角下的反向磁场模型，从而对Sgr A*的磁场几何结构施加了约束。该分析为理解银河系中心黑洞的磁场构型提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Sgr A* exhibits a persistent negative circular polarization (CP) at 230\,GHz, offering a powerful probe of the magnetic field geometry in its accretion flow. Using a stationary semi-analytic radiatively inefficient accretion flow (RIAF) model in Kerr spacetime with polarized radiative transfer, we systematically analyze CP images for six poloidal magnetic field configurations across varying black hole spins, inclinations, and field polarities. We find that CP production is dominated by Faraday conversion in radial, parabolic, quadrupole, and combined geometries, but by intrinsic emission in dipole and vertical fields. The radial and parabolic configurations produce the polarity-invariant net CP, while dipole and vertical fields yield the polarity-sensitive one. As the accretion disk is prograde with respect to the black hole spin, the CP production across all six field geometries is found to be lower at high spin case, while the situation is more complicated in the retrograde case. Moreover, the net CP observed from edge-on views $V_{\rm net} \approx 0$ except for the quadrupole geometry. Comparing with ALMA data, the reversed-field model is excluded at high inclinations and then the magnetic field geometry of Sgr A* is constrained.

</details>


### [100] [Constraining the Pulsar Beaming Fraction with TeV-Selected Galactic Pulsar Wind Nebulae and unidentified TeV Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16187)
*Takumi Shimasue,Shota Kisaka,Aya Bamba,Shinpei Shibata*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析TeV波段选出的脉冲星风云（PWNe）和未识别（Unid）TeV源，估算了脉冲星在不同观测波段（射电、γ射线和X射线）以及不同TeV巡天（H.E.S.S.、HAWC和LHAASO）中的束流分数（beaming fraction），揭示了巡天间差异并提出了统一的时间依赖开口角框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星束流分数（beaming fraction）是将观测到的脉冲星群体与银河系内禀群体相连接、并约束脉冲星发射几何的关键参数。准确估计该参数对于理解脉冲星辐射机制和群体统计特性至关重要。

Method: 研究利用TeV波段选出的脉冲星风云（pulsar wind nebulae, PWNe）和未识别（unidentified, Unid）TeV源来估算束流分数。该方法基于两个关键假设：PWNe的TeV辐射近似各向同性，且Unid源是由束流未指向地球视线的脉冲星驱动的PWNe。

Result: 在每个巡天内部，推断的束流分数在射电、γ射线和X射线波段均相似（约0.1-0.3）。然而，H.E.S.S.与HAWC/LHAASO之间的束流分数差异超过两倍，这反映了巡天依赖的选择效应，包括角分辨率和能量范围的差异，也可能表明HAWC/LHAASO样本更倾向于选择与更延展PWNe相关的较老脉冲星。

Conclusion: 研究进一步表明，推断的束流分数可以通过时间依赖开口角（time-dependent opening angle）的统一框架重现，且该框架与观测脉冲星群体的统计特性保持兼容，为理解不同巡天间的差异提供了理论解释。

Abstract: The pulsar beaming fraction is a fundamental quantity for connecting the observed pulsar population to the intrinsic Galactic population and for constraining pulsar emission geometry. In this study, we estimate the beaming fraction in each observational band (radio, $γ$-ray, and X-ray) and for each TeV survey (H.E.S.S., HAWC, and LHAASO) using TeV-selected pulsar wind nebulae (PWNe) and unidentified (Unid) TeV sources, assuming that the TeV emission from PWNe is approximately isotropic and that Unid sources are PWNe powered by pulsars whose beams do not intersect our line of sight. Within each survey, the inferred beaming fractions $\sim 0.1-0.3$ are comparable across bands. In contrast, the values differ by more than a factor of two between H.E.S.S. and HAWC/LHAASO. This discrepancy likely reflects survey-dependent selection effects, including differences in angular resolution and energy range, and is also consistent with the possibility that HAWC/LHAASO selected samples preferentially include older pulsars associated with more extended PWNe than those in the H.E.S.S. sample. We further show that the inferred beaming fractions can be reproduced within a unified framework using a time-dependent opening angle, and that this framework remains compatible with the statistical properties of the observed pulsar population.

</details>

### [101] [Cosmological dynamics and structure formation in a generalized mass-to-horizon entropy-inspired modified gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15399)
*Subhra Mondal,Amitava Choudhuri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究基于广义质量-视界熵关系启发的修正宇宙学框架，探讨其对宇宙动力学、结构形成、晕质量函数和星系团计数的影响，并通过多种诊断测试验证该模型相对于标准ΛCDM范式的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探索基于广义质量-视界熵关系（generalized mass-to-horizon entropy relation）和克劳修斯关系（Clausius relation）启发的修正宇宙学框架，旨在理解熵修正对宇宙演化和结构形成的影响。

Method: 采用重力-热力学猜想（gravity-thermodynamics conjecture）推导修正的弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）和哈勃参数演化；通过球对称塌缩形式（spherical collapse formalism）在平坦FLRW背景下构建扰动场方程，研究线性物质扰动增长；运用诊断方法比较不同宇宙学模型与ΛCDM框架。

Result: 广义质量-视界熵启发的修正宇宙学模型（n≠1）成功通过所有检验测试，证伪了平坦和非平坦ΛCDM范式；该模型满足宇宙在遥远未来达到热力学平衡的要求；修正熵项影响膨胀历史、结构增长率和塌缩晕丰度，大质量塌缩结构更稀少且形成时期更晚。

Conclusion: 基于广义熵关系的修正宇宙学模型在宇宙动力学、结构形成和热力学平衡方面展现出优于标准ΛCDM模型的特性，符合大尺度结构形成的等级模型预期，为宇宙学研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In this article, our goal is to investigate the cosmological dynamics and structure formation in a modified cosmological framework inspired by a generalized mass-to-horizon entropy relation and consistent with the Clausius relation. Invoking the gravity-thermodynamics conjecture leads to alterations in the Friedmann equations as well as Hubble parameter evolution. The effects of the generalized entropy on various cosmographic parameters and on the growth of the linear matter perturbations by constructing perturbed field equations via employing spherical collapse formalism in a flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker background have been explored. We discuss a novel and well-known diagnostic approach to differentiate various cosmological models vis-à-vis flat and non-flat $Λ$CDM frameworks, and find that the generalized mass-to-horizon entropy-inspired modified cosmology ($n\ne 1$) successfully passes all the litmus tests by falsifying both the flat and non-flat $Λ$CDM paradigms. It is shown that this model also satisfies the requirements for the Universe to achieve thermodynamic equilibrium in the distant future. We also study the halo mass function and cluster number counts in this modified gravity scenario. All the results are compared with the fiducial $Λ$CDM profile, showing that the additional entropic correction influences the expansion history, the growth rate of structures, and the abundance of collapsed halos. We observe that the more massive collapsed structures are less abundant and form at later epochs, which is expected from the hierarchical model of large-scale structure formation.}

### [102] [Highly eccentric non-spinning binary black hole mergers: quadrupolar post-merger waveforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15431)
*Nishkal Rao,Gregorio Carullo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了针对非自旋、可比较质量、高偏心轨道双黑洞并合后主导谐波(ℓ,m)=(2,2)的数值驱动闭式波形表达式，通过233个RIT模拟构建了时间依赖的准正则模式振幅，模型失配约10^{-3}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为高偏心轨道非自旋双黑洞并合的后并合发射（post-merger emission）建立精确的波形模型，这对于从引力波信号中提取天体物理和基础物理参数至关重要。

Method: 使用RIT目录中的233个非自旋偏心模拟，通过贝叶斯程序（Bayesian procedure）构建时间依赖的复准正则模式（quasinormal mode）振幅，并建立以对称质量比ν、并合时的质量重标有效能量$\hat{E}_{\mathrm{eff}}^{\mathrm{mrg}}$和角动量$j_{\mathrm{mrg}}$为变量的多元多项式模型。

Result: 模型在包括近极端偏心率的情况下达到约10^{-3}的失配（mismatch），并通过与SXS目录模拟的对比进一步验证了后并合非圆形波形模型（post-merger non-circular waveform model）的准确性。

Conclusion: 该模型可直接与有效单体（effective-one-body）和唯象（phenomenological）旋进波形结合，产生精确的旋进-并合-环降（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形，这对于信号源的天体物理和基础物理性质的参数估计至关重要。

Abstract: We present numerically-informed closed-form expressions for the dominant $(\ell,m)=(2,2)$ waveform harmonic of the post-merger emission from mergers of non-spinning binary black holes with comparable masses on highly eccentric orbits. Using 233 non-spinning eccentric simulations from the RIT catalog, we construct time-dependent complex quasinormal mode amplitudes via a Bayesian procedure. We build multivariate polynomial models, represented as functions of the symmetric mass ratio $ν$ and two dynamics parameters evaluated at merger: the mass-rescaled effective energy $\hat{E}_{\mathrm{eff}}^{\mathrm{mrg}}$ and angular momentum $j_{\mathrm{mrg}}$. We further validate the post-merger non-circular waveform model by comparing it against simulations from the SXS catalog. Our models achieve mismatches around $\sim10^{-3}$, including for near-extreme eccentricities. The model can be directly combined with effective-one-body and phenomenological inspiral waveforms to produce accurate inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms, essential for parameter estimation of both astrophysical and fundamental physics properties of the signals' sources.

### [103] [Hamiltonian formulation of a gravity model from (A)dS Yang-Mills theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15479)
*Goffredo Chirco,Alfonso Lamberti,Patrizia Vitale*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了从(A)dS李代数单参数族到庞加莱代数的收缩极限下，引力模型的哈密顿表述，证明了在选定规范条件下理论仅有两个传播自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨从杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）导出的引力模型在代数收缩极限下的哈密顿结构，特别关注当(A)dS李代数单参数族收缩至庞加莱代数时的理论行为。

Method: 方法包括推导正则结构（canonical structure）和第一类约束（first-class constraints），分析收缩极限下的代数结构，并通过洛伦兹协变规范条件选择非传播挠率（non-propagating torsion）扇区。

Result: 结果显示在收缩极限下，约束生成残余的洛伦兹规范不变性（Lorentz gauge invariance），AdS势（AdS potential）分量转化为标架（tetrads）和洛伦兹联络（Lorentz connection），理论仅有两个传播自由度（propagating degrees of freedom）。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在从(A)dS代数到庞加莱代数的收缩极限下，该引力模型在选定规范条件下仅具有两个传播自由度，保持了理论的一致性。

Abstract: We study the Hamiltonian formulation of a gravity model obtained from a Yang--Mills theory for a one-parameter family of (A)dS Lie algebras parametrized by $α$, when the family of algebras is contracted to the Poincaré algebra in the limit $α\to 0$. We derive the canonical structure and first-class constraints and analyze the resulting algebra in the contraction limit. In this limit, the constraints generate the residual Lorentz gauge invariance, and the components of the AdS potential transform as tetrads and Lorentz connection. Finally, we determine the number of physical degrees of freedom, showing that in the non-propagating torsion sector - selected by a Lorentz-covariant gauge condition preserved under dynamical evolution - the theory exhibits only two propagating degrees of freedom.

### [104] [A Semilinear Wave Sector in Force-Free Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15630)
*Yafet E. Sanchez Sanchez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一种闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中无力电动力学（force-free electrodynamics）的试探解（ansatz），将非线性系统简化为依赖于两个时空变量的半线性标量波方程（semilinear scalar wave equation），从而获得显式时间依赖解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无力电动力学在闵可夫斯基时空中的非线性系统通常难以求解。研究旨在寻找一种简化方法，以获得显式的时间依赖解，包括具有有限单位横向面积能量（finite energy per unit transverse area）的类型变化构型（type-changing configurations）。

Method: 引入一种特定的试探解（ansatz），将原始的无力电动力学非线性系统简化为一个仅依赖于两个时空变量的半线性标量波方程（semilinear scalar wave equation）。该方法允许构造行波解（traveling-wave solutions）并分析磁场主导区域（magnetically dominated regime）的场结构。

Result: 获得了显式的时间依赖解，包括具有有限单位横向面积能量的类型变化构型，以及一个零扭结型（null kink-type）示例。在磁场主导区域的行波解中，场的核分布（kernel distribution）定义了最小场叶状结构（minimal field-sheet foliations）。

Conclusion: 提出的试探解成功地将无力电动力学的复杂非线性系统简化为可处理的半线性标量波方程，为获得显式时间依赖解和深入理解场几何结构提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We introduce an ansatz for force-free electrodynamics in Minkowski spacetime under which the nonlinear system reduces to a semilinear scalar wave equation depending on two spacetime variables. This reduction yields explicit time-dependent solutions, including type-changing configurations with finite energy per unit transverse area and a null kink-type example. For traveling-wave solutions in the magnetically dominated regime, the kernel distribution of the field defines minimal field-sheet foliations.

### [105] [Geometrically Regular Black Holes with Hedgehog Scalar Hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15758)
*Sebastian Bahamonde*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一种基于广义相对论的简单理论，该理论与受约束的标量三重态和非传播三形式场耦合，在球对称hedgehog ansatz下得到了一族渐近平坦、几何正则的黑洞解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在广义相对论框架下，通过引入受约束的标量三重态和辅助非传播三形式场，能否构造出几何正则的渐近平坦黑洞解，特别是研究其拓扑标量毛和正则性特征。

Method: 采用基于广义相对论的理论框架，最小耦合到受约束的标量三重态（constrained scalar triplet）和辅助非传播三形式场（auxiliary non-propagating three-form sector）。在球对称hedgehog ansatz下求解场方程，分析其视界结构、热力学性质和强场特性。

Result: 理论允许连续精确的渐近平坦几何正则黑洞族。对于简单的动能函数选择，解具有de Sitter核心并渐近于Schwarzschild解，一阶修正仅出现在r^{-4}阶。黑洞携带拓扑标量毛（topological scalar hair）和连续次级参数，但无标量荷。正则性是几何的：曲率不变量保持有限，尽管物质场在中心不完全光滑。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构造了一族几何正则的渐近平坦黑洞解，这些解具有de Sitter核心、拓扑标量毛和连续参数，为研究正则黑洞和标量毛提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study a simple theory based on general relativity, minimally coupled to a constrained scalar triplet and to an auxiliary non-propagating three-form sector. Within a spherically symmetric hedgehog ansatz, the theory admits a continuous exact family of asymptotically flat geometrically regular black holes. For a simple choice of kinetic function, the solutions possess a de Sitter core and approach Schwarzschild with the first correction appearing only at order $r^{-4}$. We analyse their horizon structure, thermodynamics, and main strong-field properties. The black holes carry topological scalar hair and a continuous secondary parameter, but no scalar charge. The regularity established here is geometric: the curvature invariants remain finite, although the matter sector is not completely smooth at the centre.

### [106] [Mechanical Long Baseline Differential Gradiometers as Low Frequency Gravitational Wave Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15759)
*Enrico Calloni,Annalisa Allocca,Antonino Chiummo,Rosario De Rosa,Luciano Errico,Marina Esposito,Edoardo Imparato,Bruno Mantice,Luigi Rosa,Paolo Ruggi,Alessandra Ruggiero,Valeria Sequino,Daniela Stornaiuolo,Vittorio Tortorella,Lucia Trozzo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新型差分机械梯度仪，用于探测0.05-1 Hz频段的低频引力波，填补了LISA等空间探测器和地面观测站之间的频率空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在填补引力波探测的频率空白，特别是0.05至1 Hz频段，这一范围既未被未来的空间探测器如LISA覆盖，也未被地面观测站如爱因斯坦望远镜或宇宙探索者覆盖。

Method: 提出了一种新型差分机械梯度仪，采用垂直操作设计，在每根杆的一端配置配重，另一端通过长线悬挂质量块。该配置在不改变系统转动惯量的情况下增大了作用在系统上的引力，从而将信号从Δθ≈h提升到Δθ≈h(L/D)，其中L为悬挂线长度，D为臂长。

Result: 该设计是倾斜仪和双悬臂平衡仪的最新发展，其主要工作原理已经过测试。论文将基于提出的参数和现有技术讨论预期灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该新型差分机械梯度仪设计解决了传统扭摆天线的物理限制问题，通过垂直操作和特定配置增强了引力波信号，为填补低频引力波探测空白提供了创新方案。

Abstract: We present a new differential mechanical gradiometer for the detection of low-frequency Gravitational Waves. The frequency range is 0.05 to 1 Hz, a frequency gap not covered either by future space-based detectors such as LISA or by ground-based observatories such as Einstein Telescope or Cosmic Explorer. The proposed detection principle is similar to antennas based on torsion pendulums but solves the problem of physical confinement of these antennas by operating vertically and by having a counterweight at one end of each bar and a mass suspended from a long wire at the other. With this configuration, we enlarge the gravitational force acting on the system \textit{without} changing the moment of inertia of the system, so that we move from a signal $Δθ$ of the order of $Δθ= h$, where h is the amplitude of the gravitational wave, to a signal of the order $Δθ= h\frac{L}{D}$, where D is the length of the arm and L is the length of the wire suspending the test mass. This configuration is a further evolution of the recent development of tiltmeters and balances with double suspended arms and interferometric read-out, where the main working principles are already tested. The expected sensitivity will be discussed with respect to the proposed parameters and the present technology.

</details>


### [107] [Gravitational-wave astronomy requires population-informed parameter estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15885)
*Matthew Mould,Rodrigo Tenorio,Davide Gerosa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文指出引力波事件的贝叶斯后验推断通常使用非物理参考先验，导致源属性估计存在系统性偏差。通过分层参数估计（hierarchical parameter estimation）对整个观测目录进行联合分析，不仅能减少统计不确定性，还能确定正确的先验分布，从而获得适合天体物理解释的源属性估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波事件的参数估计通常基于非物理参考先验（unphysical reference priors）进行贝叶斯后验推断，这些估计在整个目录中普遍存在偏差，不适合直接用于天体物理解释。因此需要开发更可靠的方法来获得准确的源属性估计。

Method: 采用分层参数估计（hierarchical parameter estimation）方法，对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测到的整个引力波事件目录进行联合分析。这种方法不仅减少统计不确定性，还能确定正确的先验分布。

Result: 通过分层推断获得的群体信息源属性（population-informed source properties）自然适合天体物理解释和目录统计，能够识别先前和正在进行观测运行中的特殊事件。使用最新LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA数据证明了群体推断的必要性。

Conclusion: 群体推断（population inference）对于正确解释引力波观测不是可选的，而是必需的。分层参数估计方法能够提供适合天体物理解释的源属性估计，解决了传统基于非物理参考先验的贝叶斯后验推断存在的系统性偏差问题。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave events are interpreted in terms of Bayesian posteriors for their source properties inferred under unphysical reference priors. Though these parameter estimates are important intermediate data products for downstream analyses, across the catalog they provide generically biased sourced properties and are therefore unsuitable for direct astrophysical interpretation. Hierarchical parameter estimation is the solution, where joint analysis of the entire catalog of observations not only reduces statistical uncertainties but actually informs the correct prior. Population-informed source properties from there derived are naturally suited to astrophysical interpretation and catalog statistics, such as identification of exceptional events from previous and ongoing observing runs. Using the latest LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA data, we thus demonstrate that population inference is not optional to interpret gravitational-wave observations.

### [108] [Viable Cosmological Solutions from Hybrid Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15914)
*Koralia Tzanni,John Miritzis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有完美流体物质源和标量场的平坦FLRW宇宙学模型，标量场通过幂律-指数"混合"势与物质最小耦合。通过展开归一化变量，将场方程构建为约束三维动力系统，并分析其平衡结构，发现可行的宇宙学历史仅出现在参数空间的受限区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有标量场与物质最小耦合的平坦Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker（FLRW）模型，其中标量场采用幂律-指数"混合"势（power-law-exponential "hybrid" potential）。旨在理解此类模型中可行的宇宙学历史，包括瞬态物质或辐射时代以及晚期加速膨胀。

Method: 采用展开归一化变量（expansion-normalised variables），将场方程构建为约束三维动力系统（constrained three-dimensional dynamical system），并确定其平衡结构。通过中心流形分析（centre-manifold analysis）研究加速点$\mathcal{C}$的稳定性性质。

Result: 可行的宇宙学历史（瞬态物质/辐射时代后接晚期加速膨胀）仅出现在参数空间的受限区域。物理相关轨迹被限制在一个不变平面（invariant plane）内，该平面包含瞬态物质点$\mathcal{B}$和加速点$\mathcal{C}$。加速点$\mathcal{C}$不是全局吸引子：吸引$\phi>0$的轨迹，排斥$\phi<0$的轨迹。对于尘埃（dust），标准物质时代要求标量场与物质的耦合为零；对于辐射，相互作用项恒为零。

Conclusion: 标量场势能的具体函数形式可能不影响宇宙学动力学的定性行为。该研究为理解具有标量场-物质相互作用的宇宙学模型提供了动力系统分析框架，揭示了可行宇宙学历史的参数限制条件。

Abstract: We study flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) models with a perfect fluid matter source and a scalar field minimally coupled to matter with power-law-exponential \textquotedblleft hybrid\textquotedblright potential. Using expansion-normalised variables, we formulate the field equations as a constrained three-dimensional dynamical system and determine its equilibrium structure. We show that viable cosmological histories, consisting of a transient matter or radiation era followed by late-time accelerated expansion, arise in restricted regions of parameter space. A central result is that the physically relevant trajectories are confined to an invariant plane, which contains both the transient matter point $\mathcal{B}$ and the accelerated point $\mathcal{C}$. We further show, by centre-manifold analysis, that the accelerated point $\mathcal{C}$ is not a global attractor: it attracts trajectories with $φ>0$ and repels those with $φ<0$. For dust, a standard matter era requires vanishing coupling of the scalar field to matter, while for radiation the interaction term vanishes identically. Finally, we discuss the issue that the qualitative cosmological dynamics may be independent of the precise functional form of the scalar-field potential.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 结果显示：存在一类非平凡初始条件会弛豫到与Starobinsky解连续连接的吸引子慢滚分支；在所研究分支上，熵模保持充分抑制，其对曲率扰动的源贡献可忽略；张量部分保持不变。

Conclusion: 结论表明：暴胀观测量（inflationary observables）保持有效的Starobinsky特征，这为Starobinsky暴胀模型对抗最小辐射标量-张量形变提供了稳健性检验。

Abstract: We study a minimal two-field scalar-tensor completion of Starobinsky inflation motivated by the one-loop effective action of scalar-tensor gravity. The model admits an exact Starobinsky branch, but the relevant question is whether nearby trajectories generate observable multifield effects. We show that a non-trivial class of initial conditions relaxes to an attractor-connected slow-roll branch continuously connected to the Starobinsky solution. We then solve the coupled adiabatic and entropy perturbation equations numerically. On the branch studied here, the entropy mode remains sufficiently suppressed that its sourcing of the curvature perturbation is negligible, while the tensor sector is unchanged. The inflationary observables therefore remain effectively Starobinsky-like, providing a robustness test of Starobinsky inflation against a minimal radiative scalar-tensor deformation.

Our results reinforce the validity of General Relativity, particularly the Kerr hypothesis, and highlight the progress enabled by GWTC-4.

Abstract: The double Schwarzschild solution in the equal mass case is
  studied in bispherical coordinates. An explicit conformal transformation
  from cylindrical Weyl coordinates to bispherical coordinates is
  given in terms of elliptic functions. A multi-domain spectral method for spacetimes in
  bispherical coordinates is presented to numerically reconstruct
  this solution.

### [112] [Measuring the rate of glitches in interferometric gravitational wave detectors with a hierarchical Bayesian model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16039)
*Gregory Ashton,Colm Talbot,Andrew Lundgren,Ann-Kristin Malz,Joseph Areeda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种分层贝叶斯模型来测量引力波探测器中的非高斯噪声（glitch）率，该方法通过分层推断与分位数压缩（HIQC）等技术，能够在低信噪比区域准确估计噪声率，并应用于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四观测期的数据分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地面引力波探测器中的非高斯噪声（glitch）会降低信号检测灵敏度并产生有偏的天体物理推断。现有触发计数方法在低信噪比区域存在局限性，需要更精确的噪声率测量方法。

Method: 提出分层贝叶斯模型（hierarchical Bayesian model），包含分层推断与分位数压缩（HIQC）这一通用近似方法用于分层回收似然，以及通过拟合基函数进行时域率估计。方法在模拟数据中验证后应用于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四观测期数据。

Result: 该方法在24小时周期内实现了时间分辨的噪声率推断，推断结果与触发计数估计一致但无需任意阈值，提供了更精细的时间行为视图。同时展示了如何将单探测器率估计转换为同时噪声概率，并验证了撤回的引力波候选事件GW230630_070659很可能是同时噪声对。

Conclusion: 分层贝叶斯模型能够准确测量低信噪比区域的噪声率而不受高斯噪声背景污染，为引力波数据分析提供了改进的噪声率估计方法，有助于区分真实信号与噪声事件。

Abstract: Ground-based gravitational wave detectors are now routinely surveying the dark Universe, finding hundreds of collisions between compact objects such as black holes and neutron stars. However, terrestrial non-Gaussian noise artefacts, commonly known as glitches, reduce the sensitivity to signals and can overlap signals, producing biased astrophysical inferences. We introduce a hierarchical Bayesian model to measure the glitch rate, which improves upon existing trigger-counting methods in its capacity to measure the rate down into the low signal-to-noise regime without contamination from the Gaussian noise background, provided the population is accurately modelled. The methodology builds on standard hierarchical inference, but includes several novel features, including hierarchical inference with quantile compression (HIQC), a generic approximation method for the hierarchical recycled likelihood, and a time-domain rate estimated by fitting basis functions. We validate the methodology using simulated data with injected glitches and then apply it to data from the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run, demonstrating time-resolved inferences of the glitch rate over a 24 h period. The inferred glitch rate is consistent with estimates from trigger counts, but does not require an arbitrary threshold and provides a more fine-grained view of the temporal behaviour. Finally, we demonstrate how our individual-detector rate estimates can be transformed into a coincident glitch probability and utilise this to validate that the retracted gravitational-wave candidate GW230630_070659 is likely a pair of coincident glitches.

### [113] [Frame invariant diffusive formulation of scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16094)
*Laur Järv,Sotirios Karamitsos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）热力学解释中有效温度（effective temperature）的非规范不变性，并提出了基于规范不变（frame invariant）公式的替代热力学描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究将热力学解释应用于标量-张量引力，其中非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）产生的有效非理想流体具有与广义相对论偏离相关的温度。然而，这种构造中的热力学量依赖于特定的规范框架（conformal frame），引发温度是否可作为理论内在属性的疑问。

Method: 采用标量-张量引力的规范不变（frame invariant）表述，重新分析有效流体的热力学性质。通过比较不同规范框架下的温度定义，检验其规范不变性，并寻找替代的热力学描述。

Result: 研究发现，最初为非最小耦合标量场理论定义的有效温度（effective temperature）不具有规范不变性，可通过规范变换任意调整。在规范不变表述中，有效流体是理想流体（perfect fluid），温度恒为零。广义相对论的偏离由规范不变的化学势（chemical potential）控制，类似于最小理论（minimal theories）。

Conclusion: 广义相对论可被解释为任何标量-张量理论（无论是最小还是非最小耦合）的扩散平衡态（diffusive equilibrium）。温度不能作为标量-张量理论的内在属性，而规范不变的化学势提供了更合适的热力学描述框架。

Abstract: Thermodynamics provides a useful interpretation of scalar-tensor gravity, in which the effective imperfect fluid admitted by the nonminimal coupling features a temperature that is associated with the departure from general relativity. However, in this construction, certain thermodynamical quantities are defined with respect to a particular conformal frame. In the present work, we show that the originally proposed effective temperature assigned to nonminimally coupled scalar field theories is not frame invariant, and can thus be arbitrarily tuned by a change of frame. This raises the question of whether temperature can be viewed as an intrinsic property of a scalar-tensor theory rather than a particular representation of it. Working instead with the frame invariant formulation of scalar-tensor gravity, we find that the frame invariant effective fluid is perfect with identically vanishing temperature. The departure from general relativity is then governed not by temperature, but rather by a frame invariant chemical potential, similar to minimal theories. Therefore, general relativity can be interpreted as a state of diffusive equilibrium for any scalar-tensor theory, regardless of whether it is minimal or nonminimal.

### [114] [Post-Newtonian Constraints on Scalar-Tensor Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16226)
*Alexandros Karam,Samuel Sánchez López,José Jaime Terente Díaz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在度规和Palatini形式下，具有一般非最小耦合函数、非正则动能函数和标量势的广义标量-张量理论在太阳系中的约束条件。通过统一的后牛顿处理，得到了有效标量质量、有效引力耦合以及参数化后牛顿参数γ和β的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究广义标量-张量理论在太阳系观测约束下的表现，特别关注变分原理选择（度规形式与Palatini形式）对弱场现象学的影响。研究动机源于理解不同理论形式在局部引力测试中的可观测差异。

Method: 采用统一的后牛顿（post-Newtonian）处理方法，推导出有效标量质量（effective scalar mass）、有效引力耦合（effective gravitational coupling）以及参数化后牛顿参数γ和β的解析表达式。研究在度规（metric）和Palatini两种形式下进行，考虑了具有一般非最小耦合函数（generic non-minimal coupling function）、非正则动能函数（non-canonical kinetic function）和标量势（scalar potential）的标量-张量理论。

Result: 结果表明，变分原理的选择明确影响弱场现象学。与太阳系观测（主要是Cassini对γ的约束）的比较显示，形式主义的观测影响强烈依赖于具体模型。在Palatini情况下，一般非最小耦合标量场可能满足显著更弱的局部约束，这是由于更强的汤川抑制（Yukawa suppression）。而在Brans-Dicke引力中，差异通常较小，仅在参数空间的受限区域才变得显著。对于所考虑的点粒子源，Palatini f(̂R)引力再现了广义相对论的外部后牛顿极限，这与度规f(R)引力不同。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了度规和Palatini形式在太阳系约束下的重要差异：Palatini形式中的一般非最小耦合标量场可能因更强的汤川抑制而满足更弱的局部约束；在Brans-Dicke引力中，两种形式的差异通常较小；Palatini f(̂R)引力能够再现广义相对论的外部后牛顿极限，而度规f(R)引力则不能。这些发现强调了变分原理选择对理论可观测预测的重要性。

Abstract: Solar-System constraints on a general scalar-tensor theory with generic non-minimal coupling function, non-canonical kinetic function, and scalar potential, are investigated in both the metric and Palatini formalisms. A unified post-Newtonian treatment is developed, yielding analytical expressions for the effective scalar mass, the effective gravitational coupling, and the parametrised post-Newtonian parameters $γ$ and $β$. The results show explicitly how the choice of variational principle affects the weak-field phenomenology. Comparison with Solar-System observations, primarily the Cassini bound on $γ$, indicates that the observational impact of the formalism is strongly model dependent. Generic non-minimally coupled scalar fields may satisfy significantly weaker local bounds in the Palatini case because of stronger Yukawa suppression, whereas in Brans-Dicke gravity the differences are typically small and become appreciable only in restricted regions of parameter space. For the point-particle source considered here, Palatini $f(\hat{R})$ gravity reproduces the general-relativistic exterior post-Newtonian limit, unlike metric $f(R)$ gravity.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了速度场、压力、电势和离子通量密度的有界性（boundedness），这些先验估计揭示了流体的特定行为特征。

Abstract: We study a model problem on the filtration of a conducting fluid through a porous layer. A porous medium is presented as an assemblage of identical spherical cells. Each cell consists of a porous core and liquid shell. We show the dependence of each flow parameter on the Debye radius which characterizes how far the influence of a charge extends in electrolyte. The common case of finite Debye radius in comparison to the cell radius is analyzed. We derive apriori estimates for flow characteristics which show the specific behavior of the fluid. The boundedness of velocity field, pressure, electric potential and ion flux densities was proved.

### [116] [Jet-Density of Finite-Gap Solutions for Classes of BKM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16233)
*Manuel Quaschner,Wijnand Steneker*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文证明，对于BKM系统（Bolsinov-Konyaev-Matveev引入的PDE类），初始数据射流（jets of initial data）可通过有限间隙解（finite-gap solutions）任意阶近似。这些系统包含KdV、Kaup-Boussinesq和Camassa-Holm等经典PDE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究BKM系统（Bolsinov-Konyaev-Matveev systems）中初始数据射流与有限间隙解之间的近似关系，这类系统包含多个重要经典偏微分方程如KdV、Kaup-Boussinesq和Camassa-Holm方程。

Method: 通过有限约化映射（finite-reduction map）将Stäckel系统的解映射到BKM偏微分方程的解，从而获得有限间隙解。对于包含KdV和Kaup-Boussinesq的类别，利用三角结构（triangular structure）实现完全射流满射性（full jet-surjectivity）。

Result: 对于包含KdV和Kaup-Boussinesq的类别获得完全射流满射性；对于包含Camassa-Holm的类别，在实数域上初始数据的开集和复数域上的Zariski开（稠密）集上建立了射流满射性（jet-surjectivity）。

Conclusion: BKM系统的初始数据射流可通过有限间隙解任意阶近似，不同类别的系统具有不同的射流满射性范围，这为研究此类偏微分方程的近似解提供了代数方法框架。

Abstract: We show that jets of initial data can be approximated up to arbitrary order by finite-gap solutions for classes of so-called BKM systems of PDEs introduced by Bolsinov--Konyaev--Matveev, which include classical PDEs such as KdV, Kaup--Boussinesq and Camassa--Holm. Finite-gap solutions are obtained via a finite-reduction map, defined algebraically, which sends solutions of a Stäckel system to solutions of the BKM PDE. For the classes containing KdV and Kaup--Boussinesq we obtain full jet-surjectivity via a triangular structure, whereas for the class containing Camassa--Holm we establish jet-surjectivity on an open set of initial data over $\mathbb{R}$ and a Zariski-open (dense) set over $\mathbb{C}$.

### [117] [Phase transitions in Doi-Onsager, Noisy Transformer, and other multimodal models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16288)
*Kyunghoo Mun,Matthew Rosenzweig*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了圆环上具有排斥-吸引相互作用的平均场自由能的相变行为。对于满足特定傅里叶系数衰减条件的周期相互作用，证明了临界耦合强度K_c与均匀分布的线性稳定性阈值K_#重合，且相变是连续的。该结果应用于三个具体模型，确定了相变的连续/不连续性质及精确阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究圆环上排斥-吸引平均场自由能的相变行为，旨在理解均匀分布作为全局最小化子的稳定性条件。特别关注三个具体模型：二维Doi-Onsager模型、噪声变压器模型和噪声Hegselmann-Krause模型，这些模型的相变精确值和连续性尚未完全明确。

Method: 基于约束的Lebedev-Milin不等式，获得了自由能的尖锐强制性估计（sharp coercivity estimate）。该方法用于证明临界耦合强度K_c与线性稳定性阈值K_#的重合性，以及相变的连续性。

Result: 对于满足特定傅里叶系数衰减条件的周期相互作用，证明了K_c = K_#且相变连续。具体应用结果包括：二维Doi-Onsager模型在K_c=K_#=3π/4处呈现连续相变；噪声变压器模型存在临界阈值β_*，当β≤β_*时K_c(β)=K_#(β)且相变连续，β>β_*时K_c(β)<K_#(β)且相变不连续；噪声Hegselmann-Krause模型也有类似的尖锐二分性质。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了圆环上排斥-吸引平均场系统相变行为的理论框架，通过Lebedev-Milin不等式获得的强制性估计为分析相变连续性提供了有效工具。研究结果完全确定了三个具体模型的相变性质，填补了相关模型参数空间中相变行为的知识空白。

Abstract: We study phase transitions for repulsive-attractive mean-field free energies on the circle. For a $\frac{1}{n+1}$-periodic interaction whose Fourier coefficients satisfy a certain decay condition, we prove that the critical coupling strength $K_c$ coincides with the linear stability threshold $K_\#$ of the uniform distribution and that the phase transition is continuous, in the sense that the uniform distribution is the unique global minimizer at criticality. The proof is based on a sharp coercivity estimate for the free energy obtained from the constrained Lebedev--Milin inequality.
  We apply this result to three motivating models for which the exact value of the phase transition and its (dis)continuity in terms of the model parameters was not fully known. For the two-dimensional Doi--Onsager model $W(θ)=-|\sin(2πθ)|$, we prove that the phase transition is continuous at $K_c=K_\#=3π/4$. For the noisy transformer model $W_β(θ)=(e^{β\cos(2πθ)}-1)/β$, we identify the sharp threshold $β_*$ such that $K_c(β) = K_\#(β)$ and the phase transition is continuous for $β\leq β_*$, while $K_c(β)<K_\#(β)$ and the phase transition is discontinuous for $β> β_*$. We also obtain the corresponding sharp dichotomy for the noisy Hegselmann--Krause model $W_{R}(θ) = (R-2π|θ|)_{+}^2$ .

### [118] [Local CFTs extremise $F$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15420)
*Ludo Fraser-Taliente*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在由基本场标度维度Δ参数化的非局域共形场论（CFT）线上，局域CFT点对应于球面自由能F̃(Δ)的极值点，且在幺正CFT中为局部极大值点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多共形场论（CFT）可以扩展到由作用量中基本场标度维度Δ参数化的非局域CFT线。当Δ调整到局域CFT中基本场的标度维度Δ_local时，会恢复该局域CFT的共形数据。一个自然的问题是：局域点在这条非局域CFT线上有何特殊性？

Method: 证明基于球面自由能（sphere free energy）F̃(Δ) = sin(πd/2) log Z_S^d的导数分析。证明F̃对Δ的导数仅来自作用量中的非局域项，而在Δ→Δ_local极限下这些项必须消失，因此导数为零。为证明极大化，需要建立共形微扰理论中广义F-定理到次领头阶的证明。

Result: 证明局域CFT位于长程CFT球面自由能F̃(Δ)的极值点：dF̃/dΔ|_{Δ=Δ_local} = 0；对于幺正CFT，它们局部极大化F̃。通过O(N) φ^4理论和立方CFT在ε展开和大N极限下的计算验证了这一结果。

Conclusion: 该结果提供了许多CFT中基本场标度维度的最小编码，并解释了O(N)模型中Δ_φ大N展开的奇异导数结构。这种非局域F-极值化可视为已知c,F,a-极值化机制的非超对称版本。

Abstract: Many CFTs can be extended to lines of nonlocal CFTs parametrised by the scaling dimension $Δ$ of the fundamental field appearing in the action. $Δ=\frac{d}{2}-ζ$ is set by the exponent of the kinetic term $(-\partial^2)^ζ$, which is nonlocal for noninteger $ζ$. If $Δ$ is tuned to $Δ_\mathrm{local}$, the scaling dimension of the fundamental field in the local CFT, arXiv:1703.05325 showed that we recover the conformal data of that CFT (plus a decoupled sector). One natural question is: how is the local point special on this line of nonlocal CFTs? We prove that these local CFTs lie at the extrema of the (universal part of the) sphere free energy $\tilde{F}(Δ)=\sin(\frac{πd}{2}) \log Z_{S^d}$ of the long-range CFTs: $d\tilde{F}/dΔ|_{Δ=Δ_\mathrm{local}}=0$; and for unitary CFTs they locally maximise it. The simple proof uses the fact that the derivative of $\tilde{F}$ with respect to $Δ$ receives contributions only from the nonlocal terms in the action. The nonlocal terms must be absent in the limit $Δ\to Δ_\mathrm{local}$, and hence the derivative is zero. Demonstrating maximisation then requires a proof of the generalised $F$-theorem in conformal perturbation theory to subleading order. We check our result with the O$(N)$ $φ^4$ and cubic CFTs in the $ε$ expansion and the large-$N$ limit. This result provides a minimal encoding of the scaling dimension of the fundamental field in many CFTs, and also explains the curious derivative structure of the large-$N$ expansion of $Δ_φ$ in the O$(N)$ model. Finally, this nonlocal $F$-extremisation can be viewed as a non-supersymmetric version of the known $c,F,a$-extremisation mechanisms.

</details>


### [119] [Semiclassics at the cusp](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15422)
*Jahmall Bersini,Domenico Orlando,Susanne Reffert,Jesse Woods*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在d=4-ε维度的阿贝尔希格斯模型中，针对大外电荷的尖角威尔逊线算符，采用双标度极限Q→∞、ε→0且Qε固定的方法，建立了超越固定阶微扰论（fixed-order perturbation theory）的半经典框架，计算了尖角反常维度（cusp anomalous dimension）并应用于缺陷共形场论（defect CFT）可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解阿贝尔希格斯模型（Abelian Higgs model）中大外电荷尖角威尔逊线算符（cusped Wilson line operators）的行为，特别是超越固定阶微扰论（fixed-order perturbation theory）的解析控制。

Method: 采用双标度极限（double-scaling limit）方法：Q→∞、ε→0且Qε固定，建立半经典框架（semiclassical framework）。计算了尖角反常维度（cusp anomalous dimension）至规范耦合（gauge coupling）的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order），同时将标量自相互作用（scalar self-interactions）重求和至所有阶。

Result: 研究结果在微扰论和大电荷区域之间实现了插值，访问了固定阶微扰论（fixed-order perturbation theory）中不可见的区域。提供了缺陷共形场论（defect CFT）各种可观测量（observables）的新预测，包括描述超导相变（superconducting phase transition）的Mandelstam-Schwinger修饰两点函数（two-point function）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了处理大外电荷尖角威尔逊线算符（cusped Wilson line operators）的半经典框架，实现了超越固定阶微扰论（fixed-order perturbation theory）的解析控制，并为缺陷共形场论（defect CFT）提供了新的理论预测。

Abstract: We study cusped Wilson line operators in the Abelian Higgs model in $ d = 4 - ε$ at large external charges. Using a double-scaling limit $ Q \to \infty $, $ ε\to 0 $ with $ Qε$ fixed, we develop a semiclassical framework that provides analytic control beyond fixed-order perturbation theory. We compute the cusp anomalous dimension for arbitrary charges up to next-to-next-to-leading order in the gauge coupling, while resumming scalar self-interactions to all orders. Our results interpolate between perturbative and large-charge regimes, accessing domains that are invisible in fixed-order perturbation theory. As an application, we provide new predictions for various defect CFT observables, including the Mandelstam-Schwinger-dressed two-point function characterizing the superconducting phase transition.

Method: 该方法基于一类新的解析色散关系（analytic dispersion relations），这些关系非线性地依赖于散射振幅（scattering amplitude），适用于极其广泛的理论和运动学框架。

Result: 研究证明重粒子树级谱可以直接从相应低能有效场论的威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）中提取，当共振数量有限时该过程精确，否则为近似。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种从低能有效场论参数中提取高能物理信息的系统性方法，基于新型非线性解析色散关系，具有广泛的适用性。

This procedure is exact when the number of resonances is finite, and otherwise approximate. Our results are derived from a new class of analytic dispersion relations that depend nonlinearly on the scattering amplitude and apply to an exceedingly broad class of theories and kinematics.

*Federico Ambrosino,Alessandro Duci,Pietro Antonio Grassi,Silvia Penati*

Method: 采用超流形（supermanifold）上的超几何方法，根据费米分级（fermionic grading）显式组织对称性。将SuSymTFT构建为生活在(n|m)维超流形中的超BF理论（super-BF theory），并在二维紧致和手征超玻色子两个具体例子中验证该方案。

Conclusion: 本文建立了超对称模型的对称拓扑场论（SuSymTFT）的显式超对称表述，填补了费米对称性在SymTFT框架中的分析空白。超流形上的超几何方法为组织超对称性提供了自然框架，为理解超对称量子场论的对称结构和反常提供了新工具。

Abstract: We propose a manifestly supersymmetric formulation of the Symmetry Topological Field Theory (SuSymTFT) for theories with supersymmetry. The SymTFT is a framework that helps organizing symmetries and anomalies of a QFT. Albeit a lot of activity in the field has been devoted to the construction of the SymTFT for the bosonic symmetry structure, the fermionic case has not been analyzed in detail. Here, we consider the most prominent example of theories exhibiting fermionic symmetries, that is supersymmetric models. These are most naturally formulated on supermanifolds, where the supergeometry approach allows for a manifest organization of the symmetries according to their fermionic grading. We provide the general construction of the SuSymTFT as a super-BF theory living in a (n|m)-dimensional supermanifold and check our proposal in two particular examples, the compact and the chiral super-bosons in two dimensions.

### [122] [Systematic Analytic Regularization in $\varphi^4$ and Yukawa Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15429)
*Jarryd Bath,W. A. Horowitz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的正则化方案：系统解析正则化（SAR）。该方案通过在作用量层面解析延拓动能算子的幂次来正则化理论，确保在计算戴森级数（Dyson series）各项之前理论形式上是有限的。研究证明SAR能够完全且自洽地正则化φ⁴理论和Yukawa理论至次领头阶（NLO）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了系统解析正则化（Systematic Analytic Regularization, SAR）方案，通过在作用量（action）层面解析延拓（analytically continuing）动能算子（kinetic operator）的幂次来实现正则化。该方法确保理论在形式上是有限的，然后再进行戴森级数（Dyson series）各项的计算。

Result: 研究证明SAR能够完全且自洽地（fully and self-consistently）正则化φ⁴理论和Yukawa理论至次领头阶（Next-to-Leading Order, NLO）。该方案在计算戴森级数各项之前就确保了理论的有限性。

Conclusion: 系统解析正则化（SAR）是一种有效的新型正则化方案，能够在作用量层面实现理论的正则化，为量子场论计算提供了系统化的有限性保证。该方案成功应用于φ⁴和Yukawa理论的正则化处理。

Abstract: We introduce a novel regularization scheme: Systematic Analytic Regularization (SAR). SAR regularizes a theory at the level of the action by analytically continuing the power of the kinetic operator, ensuring that the theory is formally finite before any terms in the Dyson series are evaluated. We demonstrate that SAR fully and self-consistently regularizes $\varphi^4$ and Yukawa theories at NLO.

</details>


### [123] [Exact solution of two-dimensional Palatini Gauss-Bonnet theory on a strip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15471)
*Máximo Bañados,Marc Henneaux*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维Palatini Gauss-Bonnet理论在无限带状区域上的性质，发现该理论仅有边界自由度，其相空间为SL(2,R)群流形的余切丛，并受动量二次型约束。在零边界哈密顿量下，理论描述SL(2,R)上的测地线运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维Palatini Gauss-Bonnet理论在无限带状几何上的动力学行为，探索该理论仅具有边界自由度的特性，并分析其相空间结构和对称性。

Method: 在无限带状区域（有限区间与无限直线的乘积）上分析二维Palatini Gauss-Bonnet理论，采用边界哈密顿量方法，特别考虑H=0的最简单情况，并研究其他与规范不变性兼容的边界哈密顿量选择。

Result: 该理论相空间为SL(2,R)群流形的余切丛，受动量二次型（first-class）约束。在零边界哈密顿量下，理论描述SL(2,R)上的测地线运动，其"质量"由Palatini Gauss-Bonnet耦合常数决定。对称群包含SL(2,R)的左右群平移，这些从体观点看是"边界对称性"。

Conclusion: 二维Palatini Gauss-Bonnet理论在无限带状区域上表现为纯边界理论，其动力学可映射到SL(2,R)群流形上的测地线运动，具有丰富的边界对称性结构，为量子理论提供了基础框架。

Abstract: We analyze the two-dimensional Palatini Gauss-Bonnet theory on an infinite strip (product of a finite interval with the infinite line, corresponding to ``time"). The theory has only boundary degrees of freedom. Its phase space is the cotangent bundle to the group manifold of $SL(2,\mathbf{R})$, subject to a (first-class) constraint quadratic in the momenta. With the simplest choice of boundary Hamiltonian, namely $H = 0$, the theory is shown to describe geodesics on the group manifold of $SL(2,\mathbf{R})$, with a ``mass" determined by the Palatini Gauss-Bonnet coupling constant. Other choices of boundary Hamiltonians compatible with gauge invariance are also possible. The symmetry group contains (left and right) group translations on $SL(2,\mathbf{R})$. These are ``boundary symmetries" from the bulk point of view, one copy acting on one end of the interval, the other copy acting on the other end. Comments on the quantum theory are also given.

</details>

Abstract: We formulate a covariant version of Maxwell-like fracton electrodynamics in six dimensions using a symmetric tensor gauge field with scalar gauge symmetry $δA_{μν}=\partial_μ\partial_νΛ$. This provides a relativistic setting in which the characteristic fractonic restriction on mobility follows directly from gauge invariance and the allowed coupling to matter. We construct the stress--energy tensor and show that its trace has a universal dimension-dependent structure that becomes a total derivative in $d=6$. In the presence of sources, the theory enforces conservation of charge and dipole moment, capturing the immobility of isolated charges and the mobility of dipolar bound states. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维带电黑洞近极端量子熵的单圈修正，旨在理解其世界面描述与目标空间几何之间的关系，特别是检验近AdS₂几何中普遍存在的对数修正预期是否成立。

Abstract: We study the one-loop correction to the near-extremal quantum entropy of the charged two-dimensional black hole introduced in \cite{McGuigan:1992}.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在零维矩阵积分中，可以观察到主不变量对应微扰自由度、次不变量对应非微扰态的具体代数实现。完整的不变量环是有限多个次不变量在由主不变量生成的多项式环上的自由模。

Abstract: At finite $N$ the ring of gauge invariant operators is not freely generated. This motivates a physical picture in which the primary invariants are regarded as perturbative degrees of freedom while the secondary invariants are associated with distinguished non-perturbative states or sectors. The one-sided geometry describes a null shell collapsing into the empty AdS vacuum to form a black hole, while the two-sided geometry represents a null shell injected into an eternal black hole background with arbitrary energy. For unperturbed backgrounds, higher-curvature terms introduce explicit corrections to the standard CV proposal, giving rise to a ``competition effect'' absent in the uncorrected framework. In the dynamical settings, we demonstrate that despite novel jumps in the canonical velocities across the null shell, the complexity growth rate remains universally governed by the conserved momentum, just as in Einstein gravity. Furthermore, our two-sided shock wave analysis reveals that Gauss-Bonnet corrections prolong the critical time, preserving the universal logarithmic dependence for the scrambling time.

Abstract: Non-commutative electrodynamics obtained through the Seiberg-Witten map ceases to have equivalent action-level and equation-level realizations once fixed external currents are introduced, and in the action-level construction associated with the Banerjee current map the canonical location of this source-induced obstruction has remained unclear. Working in the full phase space and treating the current as prescribed and non-dynamical, we apply the Dirac-Bergmann algorithm without imposing current conservation as an external condition. The preservation of the Gauss-type secondary constraint produces a third-stage candidate whose phase-space expression is shown to be algebraically identical, at first order in the non-commutativity parameter and for purely space-space non-commutativity, to the canonical pullback of the divergence of the mapped Euler-Lagrange equations. This identity locates the source-compatibility obstruction directly within the Dirac chain. For generic inhomogeneous sources, the next consistency step feeds this object back into the primary multiplier through a source-dependent kernel, so the chain closes by multiplier fixing rather than by the generic appearance of a quaternary constraint. Reduced-phase-space results, including the gauge generator, Dirac brackets and degree-of-freedom count, are obtained only in a restricted sufficient first-class subcase; no broader claim is made for arbitrary source profiles.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We construct cubic scalar field theory on $λ$-Minkowski space by combining the Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism with harmonic analysis, and produce two inequivalent noncommutative quantum field theories. The braided theory is based on a braided $L_\infty$-algebra whereby covariance dictates a spectral decomposition into cylindrical Bessel functions that diagonalise the angular Drinfel'd twist; in this theory we find the usual logarithmic ultraviolet divergences and confirm the absence of UV/IR mixing. ### [131] [Holographic Stirling engines and the route to Carnot efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15790)
*Nikesh Lilani,Manus R. Visser*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究计算了可逆斯特林发动机（Stirling engine）在有/无回热器（regeneration）情况下的效率，针对多种工作物质包括范德瓦尔斯流体（Van der Waals fluids）、量子理想气体、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）和热共形场论（thermal conformal field theories）。研究发现回热通过内部热回收机制提升效率，并确定了达到卡诺效率（Carnot efficiency）的充分条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析斯特林发动机在不同工作物质下的效率表现，特别关注回热机制对效率的影响。研究旨在理解等容分支（isochoric branches）之间的固有热失配（intrinsic heat mismatch）如何控制效率偏离卡诺极限（Carnot bound），并量化内部交换热能被完美回收的程度。

Method: 研究方法包括计算可逆斯特林循环（reversible Stirling cycles）的效率，分析有/无回热器的情况。研究考察了多种工作物质：范德瓦尔斯流体、量子理想气体（玻色和费米气体）、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体、热共形场论以及全息共形场论（holographic CFTs）。对于对偶于AdS-Schwarzschild和AdS-Reissner-Nordström黑洞的热共形场论态，获得了斯特林效率的精确表达式。

Result: 研究确定了达到卡诺效率的充分条件：定容热容（fixed-volume heat capacity）与体积无关，确保等容热失配消失。该条件在经典理想气体和范德瓦尔斯流体中满足，但在量子理想气体和共形场论工作物质中不满足。在固定势系综（fixed-potential ensemble）中，斯特林效率在大势极限下渐近趋近卡诺值，且存在回热时趋近速度更快。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，回热作为内部热回收机制通过减少与外部热源（external reservoirs）的净热交换来提升效率。等容分支间的固有热失配控制着效率偏离卡诺极限的程度，并量化了内部交换热能可被完美回收的范围。对于全息系统，在特定极限下可达到卡诺效率。

Abstract: We compute the efficiency of the reversible Stirling engine, with and without regeneration, for a broad class of working substances including Van der Waals fluids, quantum ideal gases (Bose and Fermi), Bose-Einstein condensates, thermal conformal field theories (CFTs), and holographic CFTs. Regeneration acts as an internal heat recycling mechanism that enhances efficiency by reducing the net heat exchange with external reservoirs. For regenerative Stirling cycles, a central role is played by the intrinsic heat mismatch between the two isochoric branches, which controls the deviation of the efficiency from the Carnot bound and quantifies the extent to which internally exchanged heat can be perfectly recycled. We identify a general sufficient condition for attaining Carnot efficiency, namely that the fixed-volume heat capacity is independent of the volume, ensuring that the isochoric heat mismatch vanishes. While this condition is satisfied for classical ideal gases and Van der Waals fluids, it is violated for quantum ideal gases and CFT working substances. For thermal CFT states dual to AdS-Schwarzschild and AdS-Reissner-Nordström black holes we obtain exact expressions for the Stirling efficiency. In the fixed-potential ensemble, we show that the Stirling efficiency asymptotes to the Carnot value in the large-potential limit, with a faster approach in the presence of regeneration.

</details>


### [132] [Exact expectation values in a boost-invariant fluid of Dirac fermions with finite spin density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15926)
*Andrea Palermo,Daniele Roselli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有有限正则自旋势的非相互作用狄拉克费米子的boost-invariant非平衡流体，通过精确对角化非平衡密度算符，计算了配分函数和相关可观测量，包括自旋极化、能量密度、压力和自旋扭矩，并探讨了其在相对论自旋流体动力学和夸克-胶子等离子体现象学中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有有限自旋势的非相互作用狄拉克费米子在boost-invariant非平衡系统中的行为，特别关注自旋极化现象及其在相对论自旋流体动力学（relativistic spin hydrodynamics）和夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）现象学中的应用。

Method: 方法包括在Milne坐标中求解狄拉克方程，精确对角化非平衡密度算符，计算配分函数和相关观测量的期望值，包括自旋极化、能量密度、纵向和横向压力、自旋密度以及自旋扭矩（spin torque）。

Result: 获得了有限自旋势下配分函数的解析表达式，数值验证了热力学关系在系统中的成立；发现在boost-invariant系统中，剪切诱导极化和自旋霍尔效应均不存在，非零极化只能来源于自由理论中的有限自旋势；在特定情况下获得了自旋极化作为自旋势函数的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 结论表明在boost-invariant自由理论中，自旋极化仅来源于自旋势而非剪切效应，研究结果为相对论自旋流体动力学和夸克-胶子等离子体现象学提供了重要理论见解，特别是关于自旋非守恒源（自旋扭矩）的定量描述。

Abstract: We study a boost-invariant, out-of-equilibrium fluid of non-interacting Dirac fermions with a finite canonical spin potential. After solving the Dirac equation in Milne coordinates, we exactly diagonalize the non-equilibrium density operator and compute the partition function and expectation values of relevant observables, including spin polarization, energy density, longitudinal and transverse pressures, spin density, and \emph{spin torque}, i.e. the source of spin non-conservation. We find an analytic expression for the partition function at finite spin potential, and show numerically that thermodynamic relations connecting it to thermodynamic functions hold in the system under consideration. We show that, in a boost-invariant system, both shear-induced polarization and the spin Hall effect are absent, and that a non-vanishing polarization can only arise from a finite spin potential in a free theory. We obtain an analytic expression for the spin polarization as a function of the spin potential in some particular cases, and otherwise compute numerically its exact expectation value at finite spin potential. Our results are discussed in the context of relativistic spin hydrodynamics and quark--gluon plasma phenomenology.

</details>

Within this extended electrodynamics, the photon propagator is obtained in the combined Podolsky-CFJ framework and subsequently applied to Möller scattering. Abstract: We revisit the constrained log-subtracted two-point Padé (LSTP) ensemble for thermal $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang--Mills (SYM) thermodynamics in four spacetime dimensions after upgrading the weak-coupling truncation from $\mathcal{O}(λ^2)$ to the exact $\mathcal{O}(λ^{5/2})$ coefficient. We keep the interpolation ansatz unchanged and shift the weak-side matching points to the regime where the new term is numerically significant. The admissible set collapses from $9$ nominal survivors ($3$ distinct curves) to a single distinct curve, the crossover range shrinks to a unique value, and the pointwise band width drops to zero within numerical resolution. The Hermite-Padé (HP) central curve does not coincide with the unique LSTP survivor, so the exact weak-coupling coefficient removes the LSTP scan uncertainty but not the difference between the two routes. The next step is to compute the unknown $\mathcal{O}(λ^{-3})$ strong-coupling coefficient.

### [137] [Fractal geometry-governed oxygen diffusion: Tumors vs. Normal Tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15478)
*Neda Valizadeh,Robabeh Rahimi,Ramin Abolfath*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何主导的扩散框架，通过显式考虑生物组织的结构异质性和反常输运，解释FLASH超高剂量率（UHDR）照射下组织反应的差异。该模型揭示了组织结构复杂性增加会系统性地抑制长程输运并增强局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一个几何主导的扩散框架，以解释FLASH超高剂量率（UHDR）照射下组织反应的差异。该框架通过显式考虑生物组织的结构异质性和反常输运（anomalous transport）来达成这一目标。

Method: 作者在分形基底（fractal substrates）上构建了一个广义扩散-反应模型来描述异质介质中的分子输运。组织结构通过分形（豪斯多夫）维度（fractal (Hausdorff) dimension）\(D\)来表征，而尺度依赖的输运低效率和记忆效应则通过分数参数（fractional parameter）\(θ\)来捕捉。推导了径向对称几何的解析解，并与经典正常（欧几里得）扩散（classical normal (Euclidean) diffusion）及相同物理条件下的高斯参考模型（Gaussian reference model）进行了比较。

Result: 模型显示，随着组织结构复杂性的增加，长程输运被系统性地抑制，局域化增强。增加\(θ\)会导致亚扩散动力学（subdiffusive dynamics）、有效扩散长度减少，以及即使在稳态下也持续存在的非高斯浓度分布。虽然单独增加\(D\)会增强空间可达性，但当\(θ>0\)时，分数动力学主导输运行为，抵消了几何连通性。这些效应导致了两种机制之间的分离：一种以高效的径迹间重叠（inter-track overlap）和快速均匀化为特征，另一种则以孤立的、长寿命的反应域为标志。

Conclusion: 该几何主导的扩散框架通过整合组织结构的几何特征和反常输运动力学，为解释FLASH超高剂量率照射下组织反应的差异提供了机制性见解。模型揭示了结构异质性和分数输运在塑造生物组织内分子输运行为中的关键作用。

Abstract: {\bf Purpose}: To develop a geometry-governed diffusion framework that explains differential tissue response under FLASH ultra-high dose rate (UHDR) irradiation by explicitly accounting for structural heterogeneity and anomalous transport in biological tissues. {\bf Methods}: We formulate a generalized diffusion--reaction model on fractal substrates to describe molecular transport in heterogeneous media. Tissue architecture is characterized by a fractal (Hausdorff) dimension \(D\), while scale-dependent transport inefficiency and memory effects are captured by a fractional parameter \(θ\). Analytical solutions for radially symmetric geometries are derived and compared with classical normal (Euclidean) diffusion and a Gaussian reference model under identical physical conditions. Transport behavior is quantified through transient probability distributions and steady-state spatial profiles. {\bf Results}: The model reveals systematic suppression of long-range transport and enhanced localization as tissue structural complexity increases. Increasing \(θ\) leads to subdiffusive dynamics, reduced effective diffusion lengths, and persistent non-Gaussian concentration profiles, even in the steady state. While increasing \(D\) alone enhances spatial accessibility, fractional dynamics dominate transport behavior when \(θ>0\), counteracting geometric connectivity. These effects produce a separation between regimes characterized by efficient inter-track overlap and rapid homogenization, and regimes marked by isolated, long-lived reactive domains.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过测量横向极化质子-质子碰撞中喷注内的能量关联器，探索核子的三维结构。这些观测量能够量化喷注内单强子和强子对的能量加权角分布，为研究非微扰动力学和核子横向度（transversity）提供新途径。

Method: 使用RHIC的STAR探测器，在√s=200 GeV的横向极化质子-质子碰撞中，测量喷注内的一点和两点能量关联器。通过将碎裂动力学投影到梅林矩（Mellin moments），增强对核子横向度的敏感性，同时最小化非微扰碎裂函数的不确定性。

Result: 观测到π⁺、π⁻和π⁺π⁻对显著的spin-dependent asymmetries，揭示了非微扰动力学在特定角度尺度的onset。这些测量为核子横向度提供了敏感性，同时减少了非微扰碎裂函数的不确定性。

Conclusion: 能量关联器被确立为研究核子结构的新型精确探针，为未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider）的三维核子层析成像开辟了有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of one- and two-point energy correlators within jets in transversely polarized proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=200$ GeV, using the STAR detector at RHIC. These observables quantify the energy-weighted angular distribution of single hadrons and hadron pairs within jets, respectively. Sizable spin-dependent asymmetries are observed for $π^+$, $π^-$, and $π^+π^-$ pairs, revealing the onset of nonperturbative dynamics at specific angular scales. By projecting the fragmentation dynamics onto Mellin moments, these measurements provide sensitivity to the nucleon's transversity while minimizing uncertainties from nonperturbative fragmentation functions. These results establish energy correlators as a novel and precise probe of nucleon structure and open a promising avenue for three-dimensional nucleon tomography at the future Electron-Ion Collider.

</details>


### [141] [Latest Results from the FASER Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16244)
*Shunliang Zhang,Zhen Hu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: FASER实验在LHC Run 3期间报告了四个方面的最新物理结果：暗光子搜索获得世界领先的排除极限；中微子截面测量和首次粲强子产生搜索；首次在电子探测器中观测到ν_e；以及首次ν_μ相互作用的双微分测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FASER实验旨在利用LHC的高能质子-质子（pp）碰撞数据探索前沿物理，包括暗物质候选粒子暗光子（dark photons）的搜索，以及中微子（neutrino）相互作用的精确测量，这些研究对理解基本粒子物理和宇宙学具有重要意义。

Method: 实验使用LHC Run 3期间收集的√s = 13.6 TeV的pp碰撞数据，采用改进的分析策略进行暗光子搜索（使用177 fb⁻¹数据）；利用FASERν乳胶探测器（emulsion detector）配备681 kg钨靶和9.5 fb⁻¹的2022年数据进行中微子截面测量和粲强子（charm hadron）产生搜索；使用176.8 fb⁻¹数据在电子探测器中观测ν_e；以及使用186 fb⁻¹数据进行ν_μ相互作用的能量和快度（rapidity）双微分测量。

Result: 暗光子搜索获得了世界领先的排除极限（exclusion limits）；首次在FASER电子探测器中以5.5σ显著性观测到ν_e；完成了首次粲强子产生的中微子相互作用搜索；以及实现了首次ν_μ相互作用的能量和快度双微分测量。

Conclusion: FASER实验在LHC Run 3期间取得了多项重要突破，包括暗光子搜索的极限提升、中微子相互作用的首次观测和精确测量，这些结果为粒子物理前沿研究提供了关键数据，推动了暗物质和中微子物理领域的发展。

Abstract: We present the latest physics results from the FASER experiment at the LHC. Using $pp$ collision data at $\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV collected during LHC Run 3, FASER reports new results on four fronts: a search for dark photons with an improved analysis strategy using $177~fb^{-1}$ of data, yielding world-leading exclusion limits; neutrino cross section measurements and the first search for charm hadron production in neutrino interactions, both using the FASER$ν$ emulsion detector with a 681 kg tungsten target and $9.5~fb^{-1}$ of 2022 data; the first observation of $ν_e$ in the FASER electronic detector at $5.5σ$ using $176.8~fb^{-1}$ of data; and the first double-differential measurement of $ν_μ$ interactions as a function of energy and rapidity with $186~fb^{-1}$ of data.

</details>

Abstract: We find an exact nonequilibrium steady state of an open dissipatively driven XXZ spin-1/2 chain with source or sink spin bath at one end and an arbitrary boundary field at the other end.
