### [143] [MF-toolkit: A High-Performance Python Library for Multifractal Analysis with Automated Crossover Detection, Source Identification and Application to Gravitational Waves Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16257)
*Nahuel Mendez,Maria Cristina Mariani Maria Pia Beccar-Varela,Osei Tweneboah,Sebastian Jaroszewicz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: MF-toolkit是一个高性能并行化Python库，旨在解决多分形去趋势波动分析（MFDFA）应用中的关键挑战，包括自动交叉点检测、多分形源识别和合成时间序列生成，并在引力波数据分析中验证了其实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分形去趋势波动分析（Multifractal Detrended Fluctuation Analysis, MFDFA）虽然广泛应用于复杂时间序列的标度特性分析，但在实际应用中面临两大挑战：标度区域（交叉点）的主观识别困难，以及多分形性物理起源的模糊性。

Method: MF-toolkit集成了三项关键技术：1）全自动交叉点检测算法（CDV-A和SPIC），消除操作者偏差；2）内置迭代幅度调整傅里叶变换（Iterative Amplitude Adjusted Fourier Transform, IAAFT）用于生成替代数据，以识别多分形源；3）全面的合成时间序列生成套件，用于严格验证。

Result: 通过应用于引力波（LIGO）数据中非平稳噪声的多分形特性表征，验证了MF-toolkit的严谨性和实用性。该库为高级时间序列分析提供了稳健、高效且用户友好的工具。

Conclusion: MF-toolkit通过提供自动化、可重复的分析流程，促进了物理学及其他数据密集型领域中更严谨和可重复的研究，解决了MFDFA传统应用中的关键局限性。

Abstract: Multifractal Detrended Fluctuation Analysis (MFDFA) is a powerful and widely used technique for characterizing the scaling properties and long-range correlations of complex time series. However, its application often involves significant practical challenges, such as the subjective identification of scaling regions (crossovers) and the disambiguation of the physical origins of multifractality. We introduce MF-toolkit, a high-performance, parallelized Python library designed to address these challenges. It integrates three key innovations: (1) fully automatic crossover detection algorithms (CDV-A and SPIC), which remove operator bias and enhance reproducibility; (2) a built-in implementation of the Iterative Amplitude Adjusted Fourier Transform (IAAFT) for generating surrogate data, enabling the robust identification of the source of multifractality; and (3) a comprehensive suite for generating synthetic time series for rigorous validation. We demonstrate the rigor and utility of MF-toolkit through its application to characterize the multifractal properties of non-stationary noise in gravitational wave (LIGO) data. The MF-toolkit library offers a robust, efficient, and user-friendly tool for advanced time series analysis, facilitating more rigorous and reproducible research across physics and other data-intensive fields.

</details>


### [144] [Extracting conformal data from finite-size tensor-network flow in critical two-dimensional classical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15749)
*Sing-Hong Chan,Pochung Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出了一种从临界二维经典晶格模型中提取共形数据（conformal data）的通用框架，通过有限尺寸张量网络流（finite-size tensor-network flow）识别自洽的有限尺寸窗口和交叉尺度，从而无需临界固定点张量即可估计中心荷、标度维度和共形自旋。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常需要独特的临界固定点张量或对底层共形场论（conformal field theory）的详细先验知识。本文旨在开发一个更通用的框架，能够直接从转移矩阵谱中提取共形数据，减少对特定张量或理论知识的依赖。

Method: 核心方法是识别自洽的有限尺寸窗口和交叉尺度（crossover scale），该尺度将有限尺寸标度区（finite-size-scaling regime）与键维截断（bond-dimension truncation）引起的有限纠缠标度区（finite-entanglement-scaling regime）分开。在此窗口内，通过转移矩阵谱估计中心荷（central charge）、标度维度（scaling dimensions）和共形自旋（conformal spins）。

Result: 使用三种张量网络重整化方案（tensor-network renormalization schemes）对临界二维伊辛模型（Ising model）和三态钟模型（three-state clock model）进行基准测试。在所有方案中，在交叉尺度以下都发现了稳健的普适行为，能够准确提取相对较高共形能级的共形数据。

Conclusion: 该框架为经典张量网络计算提供了纠缠标度的自然操作定义，并产生了中心荷的互补估计量。方法不依赖独特的临界固定点张量，为从晶格模型中提取共形数据提供了更通用的途径。

Abstract: We present a general framework for extracting conformal data from critical two-dimensional classical lattice models using finite-size tensor-network flow. The central idea is to identify, from transfer-matrix spectra, a self-consistent finite-size window together with a crossover scale that separates the finite-size-scaling regime from the finite-entanglement-scaling regime induced by bond-dimension truncation. Within this window, the central charge, scaling dimensions, and conformal spins can be estimated without requiring a unique critical fixed-point tensor or detailed prior knowledge of the underlying conformal field theory. We benchmark the framework using three tensor-network renormalization schemes for the critical two-dimensional Ising and three-state clock models. Across schemes, we find robust universal behavior below the crossover scale, enabling accurate extraction of conformal data up to relatively high conformal levels. The analysis also yields a natural operational definition of entanglement scaling for classical tensor-network calculations and, in turn, a complementary estimator of the central charge.

</details>


### [145] [Phase Transitions as the Breakdown of Statistical Indistinguishability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15773)
*Taiyo Narita,Hideyuki Miyahara*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于假设检验（hypothesis testing）的相变（phase transition）新表征方法，将相变定义为热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下参数微扰导致的统计不可区分性（statistical indistinguishability）破坏，并展示了该方法在二维伊辛模型（Ising model）中的成功应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相变表征方法通常依赖于序参量（order parameter）或模型特定知识，该研究旨在建立一个不依赖序参量的通用框架，为相变研究提供更基础的理论视角。

Method: 采用基于假设检验的统计方法，将相变定义为热力学极限下参数微扰导致的统计不可区分性破坏。具体实现中使用了无分布（distribution-free）的双样本游程检验（two-sample run test）。

Result: 该方法成功识别了二维伊辛模型的临界点（critical point），且无需序参量的先验知识。传统方法如基于Binder参数（Binder parameter）的相变检测可被重新解释为该框架的特例。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个不依赖序参量的通用相变表征框架，将相变本质理解为统计不可区分性的破坏，为相变研究提供了新的理论基础和方法论工具。

Abstract: We introduce a novel characterization of phase transitions based on hypothesis testing.
  In our formulation, a phase transition is defined as the breakdown of statistical indistinguishability under vanishing parameter perturbations in the thermodynamic limit.
  This perspective provides a general, order-parameter-free framework that does not rely on model-specific insights or learning procedures.
  We show that conventional approaches, such as those based on the Binder parameter, can be reinterpreted as special cases within this framework.
  As a concrete realization, we employ a distribution-free two-sample run test and demonstrate that the critical point of the two-dimensional Ising model is accurately identified without prior knowledge of the order parameter.

</details>


### [146] [General perturbative framework for kinetics of rare transitions in 1-dimensional active particle systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15826)
*Vito Seinen,Peter G. Bolhuis,Daan Crommelin,Sara Jabbari Farouji,Michel Mandjes*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个理论框架，用于研究活性粒子在外势场中罕见跃迁（rare transitions）的动力学，特别关注热活性奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克粒子（AOUP）模型。通过投影算符形式（projection-operator formalism）和微扰计算，获得了跨越所有持续时间（persistence times）和活性强度的解析跃迁速率表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立一个通用理论框架，用于研究活性粒子在外势场中的罕见跃迁现象，其中热活性奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克粒子（Active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck Particle, AOUP）作为特例。该框架旨在解决广泛驱动系统中罕见跃迁的理论分析问题。

Method: 采用投影算符形式（projection-operator formalism），在两个不同的渐近区域（asymptotic regimes）进行微扰计算：小持续时间和大持续时间区域。通过分别积分掉活性（activity）和位置（position）自由度，获得相应的跃迁速率表达式。

Result: 在小持续时间区域，积分掉活性自由度后重现了文献中已有的速率结果；在大持续时间区域，积分掉位置自由度后获得了相应的解析速率。通过结合这两个渐近展开（asymptotic expansions），构建了一个有理近似（rational approximation），该近似在中间持续时间区域保持准确性。

Conclusion: 最终获得了一个在罕见事件极限（rare-event limit）下对所有持续时间和活性强度都有效的解析跃迁速率表达式，该结果与数值模拟高度一致。所提出的框架适用于广泛驱动系统中的罕见跃迁分析。

Abstract: We present a theoretical framework that enables investigating rare transitions in a general model of an active particle in an external potential, with the thermal Active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck Particle (AOUP) appearing as a special case. Using a projection-operator formalism, we compute transition rates perturbatively in two distinct asymptotic regimes. In the regime of small persistence times-where the activity evolves much faster than the particle's position-integrating out the activity reproduces the rates previously reported in the literature. In the opposite regime of large persistence times, we instead integrate out the position and obtain the corresponding rates analytically. Together, these asymptotic expansions uniquely specify a rational approximation that remains accurate across intermediate persistence times. As a result, we obtain an analytic expression for the rate valid across all persistence times and activity strengths in the rare-event limit, which are in excellent agreement with numerical simulations. The presented framework applies to rare transitions in a broad class of driven systems.

</details>


### [147] [On the role of the slowest observable in one-dimensional Markov processes to construct quasi-exactly-solvable generators with $N=2$ explicit levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15908)
*Cecile Monthus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从一维马尔可夫过程（Markov processes）的视角重新审视准精确可解（Quasi-Exactly-Solvable）量子哈密顿量（Hamiltonians）的构造，其中仅前两个本征态是显式的。研究显示，马尔可夫观点提供了新的解释，且以最慢可观测量（slowest observable）为中心构造N=2模型更为直观和简单。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在从满足细致平衡（detailed-balance）的一维马尔可夫过程角度重新审视准精确可解量子哈密顿量的构造问题。这种视角转换旨在为仅前两个本征态显式的模型提供更直观的理解框架。

Method: 通过相似变换（similarity transformations）将马尔可夫过程的生成元（generators）与量子哈密顿量联系起来。研究以最慢可观测量L₁(x)为中心对象，从该量出发重构所有其他性质。该方法随后应用于连续空间的福克-普朗克生成元（Fokker-Planck generators）和格点上的马尔可夫跳跃生成元（Markov jump generators）。

Result: 马尔可夫视角为量子哈密顿量的构造提供了有趣的新解释。研究发现，对于N=2显式能级的准精确可解模型，以最慢可观测量L₁(x)为中心进行构造比传统方法更为直观且技术更简单。

Conclusion: 马尔可夫过程视角显著改进了准精确可解量子哈密顿量的理解与构造方法。以最慢可观测量为中心对象的框架为N=2模型提供了更直观和简化的技术途径，这一方法可推广到连续空间和格点系统的各类生成元。

Abstract: The construction of Quasi-Exactly-Solvable quantum Hamiltonians where only the two first eigenstates $Φ_0(x)$ and $Φ_1(x)$ of energies $E_0$ and $E_1$ are explicit is revisited from the point of view of one-dimensional Markov processes satisfying detailed-balance, whose generators are related to quantum Hamiltonians via similarity transformations. Here the lowest energy vanishes $E_0=0$ and is associated the conservation of probability and to the steady state $P_*(x)$, while $E_1>0$ is the rate that governs the exponential relaxation towards the steady-state, and is associated to the slowest observable $L_1(x)$ that corresponds to the ratio $ \frac{Φ_1(x) }{Φ_0(x)}$ of the two quantum eigenstates. Our main conclusion is that the Markov perspective leads to interesting re-interpretations and that the construction of quasi-exactly-solvable models with $N=2$ explicit levels is more intuitive and technically simpler if one takes the slowest observable $L_1(x)$ as the central object from which all the other properties can be reconstructed. This general approach is then applied to Fokker-Planck generators in continuous space and to Markov jump generators on the lattice.

</details>


### [148] [Ergodic properties of functionals of Gaussian processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15952)
*Vicenç Méndez,Carlos Hervás,Rosa Flaquer-Galmés*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究推导了随机游走中正随机泛函的前两阶矩表达式，证明了平稳随机游走中观测量的遍历性，并将理论应用于高斯随机游走、标度布朗运动和分数布朗运动的占据时间分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立随机游走中正随机泛函（positive stochastic functionals）的矩理论框架，并探索其在各种随机过程（包括高斯随机游走、标度布朗运动和分数布朗运动）占据时间（occupation times）分析中的应用。

Method: 基于随机游走的一时间和两时间概率密度函数推导正随机泛函的前两阶矩表达式，证明平稳随机游走中观测量的遍历性（ergodicity），并将理论框架扩展到标度布朗运动（scaled Brownian motion）和分数布朗运动（fractional Brownian motion）。

Result: 获得了高斯随机游走半占据时间（half-occupation time）和区间占据时间的前两阶矩精确解析表达式，计算了遍历性破坏参数（ergodicity breaking parameter），建立了占据时间概率密度的简单标度形式（scaling form），并在无限遍历理论（infinite ergodic theory）框架下识别了正观测量的普适性质。

Conclusion: 研究建立了随机游走中正随机泛函的矩理论，证明了其在多种随机过程占据时间分析中的有效性，所有解析预测均通过数值模拟得到充分验证，揭示了正观测量的普适性质。

Abstract: We derive the first two moments of generic positive stochastic functionals in terms of the one- and two-time probability density functions of the underlying random walk, and we prove ergodicity of observables in stationary random walks. These general results are applied to the half-occupation time and the occupation time in an interval of a Gaussian random walk, for which we obtain exact analytic expressions for the first two moments. We then extend the analysis to scaled Brownian motion and fractional Brownian motion, computing the ergodicity breaking parameter and establishing a simple scaling form for the probability densities of occupation times. Within the framework of infinite ergodic theory, we further identify universal properties of positive observables. All analytical predictions are fully confirmed by numerical simulations.

</details>
